  203: 	)

  205: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  206: 			"construct LLM-request pricing calculator: %w",
  207: 			err,
  208: 		)
  209: 	}
  210: 	pricingUsageResolver, err := pricingapp.NewUsageResolver(
  211: 		forwardingInfrastructure.UsageExtractor,
  212: 		tokenEstimator,
  213: 		pricingCalculator,
  214: 	)
  215: 	if err != nil {
  216: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  217: 			"construct LLM-request pricing usage resolver: %w",
  218: 			err,
  219: 		)
  220: 	}
  221: 	usageResolver, err := NewLLMRequestUsageResolver(
  222: 		pricingUsageResolver,
  223: 	)
  224: 	if err != nil {
  225: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  226: 			"construct LLM-request usage resolver adapter: %w",
  227: 			err,
  228: 		)
  229: 	}
  230: 	requestFinalizer, err := NewLLMRequestFinalizer(
  231: 		ledgerService,
  232: 	)
  233: 	if err != nil {
  234: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  235: 			"construct LLM-request finalizer: %w",
  236: 			err,
  237: 		)
  238: 	}
  239: 	requestAutoCharger, err := NewLLMRequestAutoCharger(
  240: 		autoCharge,
  241: 	)
  242: 	if err != nil {
  243: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  244: 			"construct LLM-request auto charger: %w",
  245: 			err,
  246: 		)
  247: 	}
  248: 
  249: 	preflightPricer, err := pricingapp.NewPreflightPricer(
  250: 		tokenEstimator,
  251: 		pricingCalculator,
  252: 	)
  253: 	if err != nil {
  254: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  255: 			"construct LLM-request preflight pricer: %w",
  256: 			err,
  257: 		)
  258: 	}
  259: 	routePreflighter, err := NewLLMRequestRoutePreflighter(
  260: 		security.SecretPresence,
  261: 		preflightPricer,
  262: 		primitives.RouteCapacity,
  263: 		forwardingInfrastructure.AdapterSupport,
  264: 		forwardingInfrastructure.ModelRewriteSupport,
  265: 	)
  266: 	if err != nil {
  267: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  268: 			"construct LLM-request route preflighter: %w",
  269: 			err,
  270: 		)
  271: 	}
  272: 	routeSelector, err := NewLLMRequestRouteSelector(
  273: 		primitives.Clock,
  274: 	)
  275: 	if err != nil {
  276: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  277: 			"construct LLM-request route selector: %w",
  278: 			err,
  279: 		)
  280: 	}
  281: 	routePlanner, err := llmrequest.NewRepositoryRoutePlanner(
  282: 		repositories.Routes,
  283: 		repositories.Resellers,
  284: 		repositories.RoutePrices,
  285: 		routePreflighter,
  286: 		routeSelector,
  287: 	)
  288: 	if err != nil {
  289: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  290: 			"construct LLM-request route planner: %w",
  291: 			err,
  292: 		)
  293: 	}
  294: 	requestAuthenticator, err := NewLLMRequestAuthenticator(
  295: 		publicAuthentication,
  296: 	)
  297: 	if err != nil {
  298: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  299: 			"construct LLM-request authenticator: %w",
  300: 			err,
  301: 		)
  302: 	}
  303: 	billingAdmission, err := billingapp.NewAdmissionService(
  304: 		billingInfrastructure.Identity,
  305: 		billingInfrastructure.Balance,
  306: 		repositories.UsageLedger,
  307: 	)
  308: 	if err != nil {
  309: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  310: 			"construct LLM-request billing admission service: %w",
  311: 			err,
  312: 		)
  313: 	}
  314: 	billingAdmitter, err := NewLLMRequestBillingAdmitter(
  315: 		billingAdmission,
  316: 	)
  317: 	if err != nil {
  318: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  319: 			"construct LLM-request billing admitter: %w",
  320: 			err,
  321: 		)
  322: 	}
  323: 	llmRequestService, err := llmrequest.NewService(
  324: 		llmrequest.Dependencies{
  325: 			Authenticator:      requestAuthenticator,
  326: 			RequestParser:      requestMetadata,
  327: 			CapabilityDetector: requestMetadata,
  328: 			RoutePlanner:       routePlanner,

  332: 			Finalizer:          requestFinalizer,
  333: 			AutoCharger:        requestAutoCharger,
  334: 		},
  335: 	)
  336: 	if err != nil {
  337: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  338: 			"construct LLM-request service: %w",
  339: 			err,

  357: 	)

  364: 		Routes:         repositories.AdminRoutes,
  365: 		Prices:         repositories.AdminRoutePrices,
  366: 		PriceValidator: adminRoutePriceValidator{},

  368: 		Ledger:         repositories.AdminUsage,
  369: 		Audit:          repositories.AdminAudit,
  370: 		Secrets:        security.SecretPresence,
  371: 		AdapterSupport: forwardingInfrastructure.AdapterSupport,
  372: 		KeyGenerator:   security.APIKeyGenerator,
  373: 		Hasher:         security.APIKeyHasher,
  374: 		Clock:          primitives.Clock,
  375: 		BatchRetrier:   adminBatchRetrier,
  376: 	})
  377: 	if err != nil {
  378: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  379: 			"construct admin service: %w",
  380: 			err,
  381: 		)
  382: 	}
  383: 
  384: 	graph := ApplicationGraph{
  385: 		PublicAuthentication:      publicAuthentication,
  386: 		ModelCatalog:              modelCatalog,
  387: 		ProvisioningEnabled:       provisioningInfrastructure.Enabled,
  388: 		Provisioning:              provisioningService,
  389: 		Ledger:                    ledgerService,
  390: 		AutoCharge:                autoCharge,
  391: 		FailedBatchRetry:          failedBatchRetry,
  392: 		UsageResolver:             pricingUsageResolver,
  393: 		LLMRequest:                llmRequestService,
  394: 		ForwardingAttemptRecovery: forwardingAttemptRecovery,
  395: 		Admin:                     adminService,
  396: 	}
  397: 	if err := graph.Validate(); err != nil {
  398: 		return ApplicationGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
  399: 			"validate application graph: %w",
  400: 			err,
  401: 		)
  402: 	}
  403: 	return graph, nil
  404: }
  405: 
  406: func (g ApplicationGraph) Validate() error {
  407: 	switch {
  408: 	case g.PublicAuthentication == nil:
  409: 		return fmt.Errorf("public authentication use case is nil")
  410: 	case g.ModelCatalog == nil:
  411: 		return fmt.Errorf("model catalog service is nil")
  412: 	case g.ProvisioningEnabled && g.Provisioning == nil:
  413: 		return fmt.Errorf("enabled provisioning service is nil")
  414: 	case !g.ProvisioningEnabled && g.Provisioning != nil:
  415: 		return fmt.Errorf("disabled provisioning service is non-nil")
  416: 	case g.Ledger == nil:
  417: 		return fmt.Errorf("ledger service is nil")
  418: 	case g.AutoCharge == nil:
  419: 		return fmt.Errorf("auto-charge service is nil")
  420: 	case g.FailedBatchRetry == nil:
  421: 		return fmt.Errorf("failed billing batch retry service is nil")
  422: 	case g.UsageResolver == nil:
  423: 		return fmt.Errorf("LLM-request usage resolver is nil")
  424: 	case g.LLMRequest == nil:
  425: 		return fmt.Errorf("LLM-request service is nil")
  426: 	case g.ForwardingAttemptRecovery == nil:
  427: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  428: 			"forwarding attempt recovery service is nil",
  429: 		)
  430: 	case g.Admin == nil:
  431: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin service is nil")
  432: 	default:
  433: 		return nil
  434: 	}
  435: }

FILE: internal/app/llmrequest_auto_charger.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: df9be7602fd29776d983d8a793520fef5137f118
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package app
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"errors"
    6: 
    7: 	billingapp "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/billing"
    8: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/llmrequest"
    9: )
   10: 
   11: type llmRequestAutoChargeService interface {
   12: 	Run(
   13: 		context.Context,
   14: 		billingapp.AutoChargeInput,
   15: 	) (billingapp.AutoChargeResult, error)
   16: }
   17: 
   18: type LLMRequestAutoCharger struct {
   19: 	service llmRequestAutoChargeService
   20: }
   21: 
   22: var _ llmrequest.AutoCharger = (*LLMRequestAutoCharger)(nil)
   23: 
   24: func NewLLMRequestAutoCharger(
   25: 	service llmRequestAutoChargeService,
   26: ) (*LLMRequestAutoCharger, error) {
   27: 	if service == nil {
   28: 		return nil, llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   29: 	}
   30: 	return &LLMRequestAutoCharger{service: service}, nil
   31: }
   32: 
   33: func (a *LLMRequestAutoCharger) Run(
   34: 	ctx context.Context,
   35: 	input llmrequest.AutoChargeInput,
   36: ) llmrequest.AutoChargeResult {
   37: 	if a == nil || a.service == nil {
   38: 		return llmrequest.AutoChargeResult{
   39: 			Status: llmrequest.AutoChargeStatusFailed,
   40: 		}
   41: 	}
   42: 
   43: 	result, err := a.service.Run(
   44: 		ctx,
   45: 		billingapp.AutoChargeInput{
   46: 			UserID: input.Principal.UserID,
   47: 			BillingSubjectUserID: input.Principal.
   48: 				BillingSubjectUserID,
   49: 			Currency: input.FinalUsageRecord.Currency,
   50: 		},
   51: 	)
   52: 	switch {
   53: 	case errors.Is(err, billingapp.ErrChargeDeferred):
   54: 		return llmrequest.AutoChargeResult{
   55: 			Status: llmrequest.AutoChargeStatusDeferred,
   56: 		}
   57: 	case err != nil:
   58: 		return llmrequest.AutoChargeResult{
   59: 			Status: llmrequest.AutoChargeStatusFailed,
   60: 		}
   61: 	}
   62: 
   63: 	status := llmrequest.AutoChargeStatusProcessed
   64: 	if result.Deferred &&
   65: 		len(result.ProcessedBatchIDs) == 0 {
   66: 		status = llmrequest.AutoChargeStatusDeferred
   67: 	}
   68: 
   69: 	var balance *int64
   70: 	if result.BillingBalanceCents != nil {
   71: 		copied := *result.BillingBalanceCents
   72: 		balance = &copied
   73: 	}
   74: 
   75: 	return llmrequest.AutoChargeResult{
   76: 		Status:              status,
   77: 		ProcessedBatchIDs:   append([]string(nil), result.ProcessedBatchIDs...),
   78: 		ChargedAmountCents:  result.ChargedAmountCents,
   79: 		BillingBalanceCents: balance,
   80: 	}
   81: }

GIT_BLOB_SHA: b59da3605919fea40705bc8c99df8e54c3691ed0

    1: package app
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"fmt"
    6: 
    7: 	billingapp "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/billing"
    8: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/llmrequest"
    9: )
   10: 
   11: type billingAdmissionService interface {
   12: 	Admit(
   13: 		context.Context,
   14: 		billingapp.AdmissionInput,
   15: 	) (billingapp.AdmissionResult, error)
   16: }
   17: 
   18: type LLMRequestBillingAdmitter struct {
   19: 	billing billingAdmissionService
   20: }
   21: 
   22: var _ llmrequest.BillingAdmitter = (*LLMRequestBillingAdmitter)(nil)
   23: 
   24: func NewLLMRequestBillingAdmitter(
   25: 	billing billingAdmissionService,
   26: ) (*LLMRequestBillingAdmitter, error) {
   27: 	if billing == nil {
   28: 		return nil, llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   29: 	}
   30: 	return &LLMRequestBillingAdmitter{billing: billing}, nil
   31: }
   32: 
   33: func (a *LLMRequestBillingAdmitter) Admit(
   34: 	ctx context.Context,
   35: 	input llmrequest.BillingAdmissionInput,
   36: ) (llmrequest.BillingAdmissionResult, error) {
   37: 	if a == nil || a.billing == nil {
   38: 		return llmrequest.BillingAdmissionResult{},
   39: 			llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   40: 	}
   41: 	if ctx == nil {
   42: 		return llmrequest.BillingAdmissionResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   43: 			"%w: nil billing admission context",
   44: 			llmrequest.ErrInvalidInput,
   45: 		)
   46: 	}
   47: 	if err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {
   48: 		return llmrequest.BillingAdmissionResult{}, err
   49: 	}
   50: 
   51: 	result, err := a.billing.Admit(
   52: 		ctx,
   53: 		billingapp.AdmissionInput{
   54: 			UserID: input.Principal.UserID,
   55: 			BillingSubjectUserID: input.Principal.
   56: 				BillingSubjectUserID,
   57: 			RequiredReserveCents: input.RequiredReserveCents,
   58: 			Currency:             input.Currency,
   59: 		},
   60: 	)
   61: 	if err != nil {
   62: 		return llmrequest.BillingAdmissionResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   63: 			"admit LLM-request billing reserve: %w",
   64: 			err,
   65: 		)
   66: 	}
   67: 
   68: 	return llmrequest.BillingAdmissionResult{
   69: 		Allowed:               result.Allowed,
   70: 		RemoteBalanceCents:    result.RemoteBalanceCents,
   71: 		PendingAmountCents:    result.PendingAmountCents,
   72: 		EffectiveBalanceCents: result.EffectiveBalanceCents,
   73: 		RequiredReserveCents:  result.RequiredReserveCents,
   74: 		Currency:              result.Currency,
   75: 	}, nil
   76: }

FILE: internal/app/llmrequest_finalizer.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: f6cb540bf1a26ba43b6ac5cf744730b05eb22f84
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package app
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"fmt"
    6: 
    7: 	ledgerapp "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/ledger"
    8: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/llmrequest"
    9: 	pricingapp "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/pricing"
   10: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
   11: )
   12: 
   13: type llmRequestLedger interface {
   14: 	CommitBillable(
   15: 		context.Context,
   16: 		ledgerapp.CommitBillableInput,
   17: 	) (domain.UsageRecord, error)
   18: 	MarkPricingFailed(
   19: 		context.Context,
   20: 		ledgerapp.MarkPricingFailedInput,
   21: 	) (domain.UsageRecord, error)
   22: }
   23: 
   24: type LLMRequestFinalizer struct {
   25: 	ledger llmRequestLedger
   26: }
   27: 
   28: var _ llmrequest.Finalizer = (*LLMRequestFinalizer)(nil)
   29: 
   30: func NewLLMRequestFinalizer(
   31: 	ledger llmRequestLedger,
   32: ) (*LLMRequestFinalizer, error) {
   33: 	if ledger == nil {
   34: 		return nil, llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   35: 	}
   36: 	return &LLMRequestFinalizer{ledger: ledger}, nil
   37: }
   38: 
   39: func (f *LLMRequestFinalizer) Commit(
   40: 	ctx context.Context,
   41: 	input llmrequest.FinalizationInput,
   42: ) (llmrequest.FinalizationResult, error) {
   43: 	if f == nil || f.ledger == nil {
   44: 		return llmrequest.FinalizationResult{},
   45: 			llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   46: 	}
   47: 	completeness, err := pricingapp.ParseUsageCompleteness(
   48: 		input.ResolvedUsage.Completeness,
   49: 	)
   50: 	if err != nil {
   51: 		return llmrequest.FinalizationResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   52: 			"parse final usage completeness: %w",
   53: 			err,
   54: 		)
   55: 	}
   56: 	record, err := f.ledger.CommitBillable(
   57: 		ctx,
   58: 		ledgerapp.CommitBillableInput{
   59: 			LocalRequestID:    input.Reserved.Prepared.LocalRequestID,
   60: 			Usage:             input.ResolvedUsage.Usage,
   61: 			UsageCompleteness: completeness,
   62: 			ClientAmountCents: input.ResolvedUsage.
   63: 				ClientAmountCents,
   64: 			ActualUpstreamCostCents: input.ResolvedUsage.
   65: 				UpstreamCostCents,
   66: 			ProviderRequestID: input.ResolvedUsage.
   67: 				ProviderRequestID,
   68: 			ProviderResponseModel: input.ResolvedUsage.
   69: 				ProviderResponseModel,
   70: 		},
   71: 	)
   72: 	if err != nil {
   73: 		return llmrequest.FinalizationResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   74: 			"commit billable usage: %w",
   75: 			err,
   76: 		)
   77: 	}
   78: 	return llmrequest.FinalizationResult{Usage: record}, nil
   79: }
   80: 
   81: func (f *LLMRequestFinalizer) MarkPricingFailed(
   82: 	ctx context.Context,
   83: 	input llmrequest.PricingFailureInput,
   84: ) (llmrequest.FinalizationResult, error) {
   85: 	if f == nil || f.ledger == nil {
   86: 		return llmrequest.FinalizationResult{},
   87: 			llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   88: 	}
   89: 	record, err := f.ledger.MarkPricingFailed(
   90: 		ctx,
   91: 		ledgerapp.MarkPricingFailedInput{
   92: 			LocalRequestID: input.Reserved.Prepared.LocalRequestID,
   93: 			Usage: input.Reserved.Prepared.Plan.
   94: 				EstimatedUsage,
   95: 			UsageCompleteness: pricingapp.
   96: 				UsageCompletenessFailed,
   97: 			FailureReason: input.FailureReason,
   98: 		},
   99: 	)
  100: 	if err != nil {
  101: 		return llmrequest.FinalizationResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
  102: 			"mark pricing failed usage: %w",
  103: 			err,
  104: 		)
  105: 	}
  106: 	return llmrequest.FinalizationResult{Usage: record}, nil
  107: }

    1: package app
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"testing"
    6: 	"time"
    7: 
    8: 	ledgerapp "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/ledger"
    9: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/llmrequest"
   10: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
   11: )
   12: 
   13: type finalizerLedger struct {

   15: 	failureInput ledgerapp.MarkPricingFailedInput
   16: }

   26: 	}, nil
   27: }

   48: func TestLLMRequestForwardingExecutorUsesSemanticBoundary(t *testing.T) {
   49: 	input := validExecutorInput()
   50: 	original := append([]byte(nil), input.Prepared.Payload...)
   51: 
   52: 	var gotSecretName string
   53: 	var gotFactory ports.ForwardingAdapterFactoryInput
   54: 	var gotClientRouteID string
   55: 	var gotClientBody []byte
   56: 
   57: 	executor := mustLLMRequestForwardingExecutor(
   58: 		t,
   59: 		executorSecretResolverFunc(
   60: 			func(
   61: 				_ context.Context,
   62: 				name string,
   63: 			) (string, error) {
   64: 				gotSecretName = name
   65: 				return "resolved-secret", nil
   66: 			},
   67: 		),
   68: 		executorFactoryFunc(
   69: 			func(
   70: 				value ports.ForwardingAdapterFactoryInput,
   71: 			) (ports.ForwardingClient, error) {
   72: 				gotFactory = value
   73: 				return executorClientFunc(
   74: 					func(
   75: 						_ context.Context,
   76: 						request ports.ForwardingClientRequest,
   77: 					) (ports.ForwardResponse, error) {
   78: 						gotClientRouteID = request.Route.ID
   79: 						gotClientBody = append(
   80: 							[]byte(nil),
   81: 							request.Body...,
   82: 						)
   83: 						request.Body[0] = 'X'
   84: 						return ports.ForwardResponse{
   85: 							StatusCode: 200,
   86: 							Headers: map[string][]string{
   87: 								"Content-Type": {"application/json"},
   88: 							},
   89: 							Body: []byte(`{"ok":true}`),
   90: 						}, nil
   91: 					},
   92: 				), nil
   93: 			},
   94: 		),
   95: 		1024,
   96: 	)
   97: 
   98: 	result, err := executor.Forward(context.Background(), input)
   99: 	if err != nil {
  100: 		t.Fatalf("Forward: %v", err)
  101: 	}
  102: 	if gotSecretName != input.Prepared.Plan.Reseller.APIKeyEnv {
  103: 		t.Fatalf("secret name=%q", gotSecretName)
  104: 	}
  105: 	if gotFactory.Route.ID != input.Prepared.Plan.Route.ID ||
  106: 		gotFactory.Reseller.ID != input.Prepared.Plan.Reseller.ID ||
  107: 		gotFactory.ResellerAPIKey != "resolved-secret" ||
  108: 		gotFactory.MaxResponseBodyBytes != 1024 {
  109: 		t.Fatalf("factory input=%+v", gotFactory)
  110: 	}
  111: 	if gotClientRouteID != input.Prepared.Plan.Route.ID ||
  112: 		!bytes.Equal(gotClientBody, original) {
  113: 		t.Fatalf(
  114: 			"client input route/body=%q/%q",
  115: 			gotClientRouteID,
  116: 			gotClientBody,
  117: 		)
  118: 	}
  119: 	if !bytes.Equal(input.Prepared.Payload, original) {
  120: 		t.Fatalf("caller payload mutated: %q", input.Prepared.Payload)
  121: 	}
  122: 	if result.Response.StatusCode != 200 {
  123: 		t.Fatalf("result=%+v", result)
  124: 	}
  125: }

FILE: internal/app/llmrequest_route_preflighter.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: cb368dce1a8c68ecb7325fa51cc9fabf5df34f71
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package app
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"fmt"
    6: 	"strings"
    7: 
    8: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/llmrequest"
    9: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/pricing"
   10: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
   11: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/ports"
   12: )
   13: 
   14: type LLMRequestRoutePreflighter struct {
   15: 	secrets        ports.SecretPresenceChecker
   16: 	pricer         *pricing.PreflightPricer
   17: 	capacity       ports.RouteCapacityChecker
   18: 	adapterSupport ports.ForwardingAdapterSupport
   19: 	rewriteSupport ports.ModelIdentifierRewriteSupport
   20: }
   21: 
   22: var _ llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflighter = (*LLMRequestRoutePreflighter)(nil)
   23: 
   24: func NewLLMRequestRoutePreflighter(
   25: 	secrets ports.SecretPresenceChecker,
   26: 	pricer *pricing.PreflightPricer,
   27: 	capacity ports.RouteCapacityChecker,
   28: 	adapterSupport ports.ForwardingAdapterSupport,
   29: 	rewriteSupport ports.ModelIdentifierRewriteSupport,
   30: ) (*LLMRequestRoutePreflighter, error) {
   31: 	if secrets == nil ||
   32: 		pricer == nil ||
   33: 		capacity == nil ||
   34: 		adapterSupport == nil ||
   35: 		rewriteSupport == nil {
   36: 		return nil, llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   37: 	}
   38: 	return &LLMRequestRoutePreflighter{
   39: 		secrets:        secrets,
   40: 		pricer:         pricer,
   41: 		capacity:       capacity,
   42: 		adapterSupport: adapterSupport,
   43: 		rewriteSupport: rewriteSupport,
   44: 	}, nil
   45: }
   46: 
   47: func (p *LLMRequestRoutePreflighter) Evaluate(
   48: 	ctx context.Context,
   49: 	input llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightInput,
   50: ) (llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult, error) {
   51: 	if p == nil ||
   52: 		p.secrets == nil ||
   53: 		p.pricer == nil ||
   54: 		p.capacity == nil ||
   55: 		p.adapterSupport == nil ||
   56: 		p.rewriteSupport == nil {
   57: 		return llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult{},
   58: 			llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   59: 	}
   60: 	if ctx == nil {
   61: 		return llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   62: 			"%w: nil route preflight context",
   63: 			llmrequest.ErrInvalidInput,
   64: 		)
   65: 	}
   66: 	if err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {
   67: 		return llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult{}, err
   68: 	}
   69: 	if err := validateLLMRequestRoutePreflightInput(input); err != nil {
   70: 		return llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult{}, err
   71: 	}
   72: 
   73: 	result := llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult{
   74: 		ForwardingAdapterAvailable: p.adapterSupport.SupportsForwardingAdapter(
   75: 			input.Route.APIFamily,
   76: 			input.Route.ProviderType,
   77: 			input.Route.EndpointKind,
   78: 		),
   79: 		ModelIdentifierRewriteAllowed: llmRequestModelRewriteAllowed(
   80: 			p.rewriteSupport,
   81: 			input.Route,
   82: 		),
   83: 	}
   84: 
   85: 	if !input.Route.Enabled || !input.Reseller.Enabled {
   86: 		return result, nil
   87: 	}
   88: 
   89: 	if strings.TrimSpace(input.Reseller.APIKeyEnv) != "" {
   90: 		available, err := p.secrets.Exists(
   91: 			ctx,
   92: 			input.Reseller.APIKeyEnv,
   93: 		)
   94: 		if err != nil {
   95: 			return llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult{},
   96: 				fmt.Errorf(
   97: 					"check reseller secret presence: %w",
   98: 					err,
   99: 				)
  100: 		}
  101: 		result.SecretAvailable = available
  102: 	}
  103: 
  104: 	if input.Price == nil {
  105: 		return result, nil
  106: 	}
  107: 
  108: 	priced, err := p.pricer.Price(
  109: 		ctx,
  110: 		pricing.PreflightInput{
  111: 			Route:                 input.Route,
  112: 			Price:                 *input.Price,
  113: 			RequestBody:           append([]byte(nil), input.Payload...),
  114: 			RequestedCapabilities: input.RequestedCapabilities,
  115: 		},
  116: 	)
  117: 	if err != nil {
  118: 		if contextError := ctx.Err(); contextError != nil {
  119: 			return llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult{},
  120: 				contextError
  121: 		}
  122: 		return result, nil
  123: 	}
  124: 
  125: 	result.CostAvailable = true
  126: 	result.EstimatedUsage = priced.EstimatedUsage
  127: 	result.EstimatedClientAmountCents =
  128: 		priced.EstimatedClientAmountCents
  129: 	result.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents =
  130: 		priced.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents
  131: 	result.Currency = priced.Currency
  132: 	result.Confidence = priced.Confidence
  133: 
  134: 	capacity, err := p.capacity.Check(
  135: 		ctx,
  136: 		ports.RouteCapacityCheckInput{
  137: 			Route:          input.Route,
  138: 			Reseller:       input.Reseller,
  139: 			EstimatedUsage: priced.EstimatedUsage,
  140: 		},
  141: 	)
  142: 	if err != nil {
  143: 		return llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightResult{},
  144: 			fmt.Errorf("check route capacity: %w", err)
  145: 	}
  146: 	result.RateLimitAllowed = capacity.RateLimitAllowed
  147: 	result.ConcurrencyAllowed = capacity.ConcurrencyAllowed
  148: 	return result, nil
  149: }
  150: 
  151: func validateLLMRequestRoutePreflightInput(
  152: 	input llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightInput,
  153: ) error {
  154: 	if strings.TrimSpace(input.Route.ID) == "" ||
  155: 		strings.TrimSpace(input.Route.ResellerID) == "" ||
  156: 		strings.TrimSpace(input.Reseller.ID) == "" ||
  157: 		input.Route.ResellerID != input.Reseller.ID ||
  158: 		input.Route.ProviderType == "" ||
  159: 		input.Route.ProviderType != input.Reseller.ProviderType ||
  160: 		input.Route.APIFamily == "" ||
  161: 		input.Route.EndpointKind == "" ||
  162: 		strings.TrimSpace(input.Route.ClientModel) == "" ||
  163: 		input.Payload == nil {
  164: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  165: 			"%w: invalid route preflight input",
  166: 			llmrequest.ErrStageContractViolation,
  167: 		)
  168: 	}
  169: 	if input.Price != nil &&
  170: 		input.Price.RouteID != input.Route.ID {
  171: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  172: 			"%w: route price identity mismatch",
  173: 			llmrequest.ErrStageContractViolation,
  174: 		)
  175: 	}
  176: 	return nil
  177: }
  178: 
  179: func llmRequestModelRewriteAllowed(
  180: 	support ports.ModelIdentifierRewriteSupport,
  181: 	route domain.Route,
  182: ) bool {
  183: 	switch route.ModelRewritePolicy {
  184: 	case domain.ModelRewritePolicyNone:
  185: 		return true
  186: 	case domain.ModelRewritePolicyProviderModel:
  187: 		return support.SupportsModelIdentifierRewrite(
  188: 			route.APIFamily,
  189: 			route.ProviderType,
  190: 		)
  191: 	default:
  192: 		return false
  193: 	}
  194: }

   77: func TestLLMRequestRoutePreflighterBuildsCompleteFacts(t *testing.T) {
   78: 	input := validLLMRequestRoutePreflightInput()
   79: 	originalPayload := append([]byte(nil), input.Payload...)
   80: 
   81: 	var gotSecretName string
   82: 	var gotCapacity ports.RouteCapacityCheckInput
   83: 	var gotEstimateClientModel string
   84: 	var gotEstimateBody []byte
   85: 	var gotRewriteAPI domain.APIFamily
   86: 	var gotRewriteProvider domain.ProviderType
   87: 
   88: 	preflighter := mustLLMRequestRoutePreflighter(
   89: 		t,
   90: 		llmRequestSecretPresenceFunc(
   91: 			func(
   92: 				_ context.Context,
   93: 				name string,
   94: 			) (bool, error) {
   95: 				gotSecretName = name
   96: 				return true, nil
   97: 			},
   98: 		),
   99: 		mustLLMRequestPreflightPricer(
  100: 			t,
  101: 			llmRequestTokenEstimatorFunc(
  102: 				func(
  103: 					_ context.Context,
  104: 					request ports.TokenEstimateRequest,
  105: 				) (ports.TokenEstimate, error) {
  106: 					gotEstimateClientModel = request.ClientModel
  107: 					gotEstimateBody = append(
  108: 						[]byte(nil),
  109: 						request.RequestBody...,
  110: 					)
  111: 					request.RequestBody[0] = 'X'
  112: 					return ports.TokenEstimate{
  113: 						Usage: domain.TokenUsage{
  114: 							InputTokens:  10,
  115: 							OutputTokens: 5,
  116: 						},
  117: 						Confidence: "conservative",
  118: 					}, nil
  119: 				},
  120: 			),
  121: 		),
  122: 		llmRequestRouteCapacityFunc(
  123: 			func(
  124: 				_ context.Context,
  125: 				value ports.RouteCapacityCheckInput,
  126: 			) (ports.RouteCapacityResult, error) {
  127: 				gotCapacity = value
  128: 				return ports.RouteCapacityResult{
  129: 					RateLimitAllowed:   true,
  130: 					ConcurrencyAllowed: true,
  131: 				}, nil
  132: 			},
  133: 		),
  134: 		llmRequestRewriteSupportFunc(
  135: 			func(
  136: 				apiFamily domain.APIFamily,
  137: 				providerType domain.ProviderType,
  138: 			) bool {
  139: 				gotRewriteAPI = apiFamily
  140: 				gotRewriteProvider = providerType
  141: 				return true
  142: 			},
  143: 		),
  144: 	)
  145: 
  146: 	result, err := preflighter.Evaluate(
  147: 		context.Background(),
  148: 		input,
  149: 	)
  150: 	if err != nil {
  151: 		t.Fatalf("Evaluate: %v", err)
  152: 	}
  153: 
  154: 	if gotSecretName != "RESELLER_API_KEY" {
  155: 		t.Fatalf("secret name = %q", gotSecretName)
  156: 	}
  157: 	if gotCapacity.Route.ID != input.Route.ID ||
  158: 		gotCapacity.Reseller.ID != input.Reseller.ID ||
  159: 		gotCapacity.EstimatedUsage != (domain.TokenUsage{
  160: 			InputTokens:  10,
  161: 			OutputTokens: 5,
  162: 		}) {
  163: 		t.Fatalf("capacity input = %+v", gotCapacity)
  164: 	}
  165: 	if gotEstimateClientModel != input.Route.ClientModel ||
  166: 		!bytes.Equal(gotEstimateBody, originalPayload) {
  167: 		t.Fatalf(
  168: 			"estimate request model/body = %q/%q",
  169: 			gotEstimateClientModel,
  170: 			gotEstimateBody,
  171: 		)
  172: 	}
  173: 	if gotRewriteAPI != input.Route.APIFamily ||
  174: 		gotRewriteProvider != input.Route.ProviderType {
  175: 		t.Fatalf(
  176: 			"rewrite lookup = %q/%q",
  177: 			gotRewriteAPI,
  178: 			gotRewriteProvider,
  179: 		)
  180: 	}
  181: 	if !bytes.Equal(input.Payload, originalPayload) {
  182: 		t.Fatalf("caller payload mutated: %q", input.Payload)
  183: 	}
  184: 
  185: 	if !result.SecretAvailable ||
  186: 		!result.CostAvailable ||
  187: 		!result.ForwardingAdapterAvailable ||
  188: 		!result.RateLimitAllowed ||
  189: 		!result.ConcurrencyAllowed ||
  190: 		!result.ModelIdentifierRewriteAllowed ||
  191: 		result.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents != 20 ||
  192: 		result.EstimatedClientAmountCents != 30 ||
  193: 		result.Currency != "RUB" ||
  194: 		result.Confidence != "conservative" {
  195: 		t.Fatalf("result = %+v", result)
  196: 	}
  197: }

  394: func TestLLMRequestRoutePreflighterPropagatesOperationalErrors(
  395: 	t *testing.T,
  396: ) {
  397: 	dependencyError := errors.New("dependency failed")
  398: 
  399: 	tests := []struct {
  400: 		name     string
  401: 		secrets  ports.SecretPresenceChecker
  402: 		capacity ports.RouteCapacityChecker
  403: 	}{
  404: 		{
  405: 			name: "secret presence",
  406: 			secrets: llmRequestSecretPresenceFunc(
  407: 				func(
  408: 					context.Context,
  409: 					string,
  410: 				) (bool, error) {
  411: 					return false, dependencyError
  412: 				},
  413: 			),
  414: 			capacity: allowedLLMRequestCapacity(),
  415: 		},
  416: 		{
  417: 			name:    "capacity",
  418: 			secrets: alwaysPresentLLMRequestSecret(),
  419: 			capacity: llmRequestRouteCapacityFunc(
  420: 				func(
  421: 					context.Context,
  422: 					ports.RouteCapacityCheckInput,
  423: 				) (ports.RouteCapacityResult, error) {
  424: 					return ports.RouteCapacityResult{},
  425: 						dependencyError
  426: 				},
  427: 			),
  428: 		},
  429: 	}
  430: 
  431: 	for _, test := range tests {
  432: 		t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
  433: 			preflighter := mustLLMRequestRoutePreflighter(
  434: 				t,
  435: 				test.secrets,
  436: 				mustLLMRequestPreflightPricer(
  437: 					t,
  438: 					staticLLMRequestEstimator(),
  439: 				),
  440: 				test.capacity,
  441: 				allowedLLMRequestRewrite(),
  442: 			)
  443: 
  444: 			_, err := preflighter.Evaluate(
  445: 				context.Background(),
  446: 				validLLMRequestRoutePreflightInput(),
  447: 			)
  448: 			if !errors.Is(err, dependencyError) {
  449: 				t.Fatalf(
  450: 					"error = %v, want dependency error",
  451: 					err,
  452: 				)
  453: 			}
  454: 		})
  455: 	}
  456: }

  458: func TestNewLLMRequestRoutePreflighterRequiresDependencies(
  459: 	t *testing.T,
  460: ) {
  461: 	pricer := mustLLMRequestPreflightPricer(
  462: 		t,
  463: 		staticLLMRequestEstimator(),
  464: 	)
  465: 	validSecrets := alwaysPresentLLMRequestSecret()
  466: 	validCapacity := allowedLLMRequestCapacity()
  467: 	validAdapter := allowedLLMRequestAdapterSupport()
  468: 	validRewrite := allowedLLMRequestRewrite()
  469: 
  470: 	tests := []struct {
  471: 		name     string
  472: 		secrets  ports.SecretPresenceChecker
  473: 		pricer   *pricing.PreflightPricer
  474: 		capacity ports.RouteCapacityChecker
  475: 		adapter  ports.ForwardingAdapterSupport
  476: 		rewrite  ports.ModelIdentifierRewriteSupport
  477: 	}{
  478: 		{
  479: 			name:     "secrets",
  480: 			pricer:   pricer,
  481: 			capacity: validCapacity,
  482: 			adapter:  validAdapter,
  483: 			rewrite:  validRewrite,
  484: 		},
  485: 		{
  486: 			name:     "pricer",
  487: 			secrets:  validSecrets,
  488: 			capacity: validCapacity,
  489: 			adapter:  validAdapter,
  490: 			rewrite:  validRewrite,
  491: 		},
  492: 		{
  493: 			name:    "capacity",
  494: 			secrets: validSecrets,
  495: 			pricer:  pricer,
  496: 			adapter: validAdapter,
  497: 			rewrite: validRewrite,
  498: 		},
  499: 		{
  500: 			name:     "adapter",
  501: 			secrets:  validSecrets,
  502: 			pricer:   pricer,
  503: 			capacity: validCapacity,
  504: 			rewrite:  validRewrite,
  505: 		},
  506: 		{
  507: 			name:     "rewrite",
  508: 			secrets:  validSecrets,
  509: 			pricer:   pricer,
  510: 			capacity: validCapacity,
  511: 			adapter:  validAdapter,
  512: 		},
  513: 	}
  514: 
  515: 	for _, test := range tests {
  516: 		t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
  517: 			_, err := NewLLMRequestRoutePreflighter(
  518: 				test.secrets,
  519: 				test.pricer,
  520: 				test.capacity,
  521: 				test.adapter,
  522: 				test.rewrite,
  523: 			)
  524: 			if !errors.Is(
  525: 				err,
  526: 				llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired,
  527: 			) {
  528: 				t.Fatalf(
  529: 					"error = %v, want dependency required",
  530: 					err,
  531: 				)
  532: 			}
  533: 		})
  534: 	}
  535: }

  537: func mustLLMRequestRoutePreflighter(
  538: 	t *testing.T,
  539: 	secrets ports.SecretPresenceChecker,
  540: 	pricer *pricing.PreflightPricer,
  541: 	capacity ports.RouteCapacityChecker,
  542: 	rewrite ports.ModelIdentifierRewriteSupport,
  543: ) *LLMRequestRoutePreflighter {
  544: 	t.Helper()
  545: 
  546: 	value, err := NewLLMRequestRoutePreflighter(
  547: 		secrets,
  548: 		pricer,
  549: 		capacity,
  550: 		allowedLLMRequestAdapterSupport(),
  551: 		rewrite,
  552: 	)
  553: 	if err != nil {
  554: 		t.Fatalf("NewLLMRequestRoutePreflighter: %v", err)
  555: 	}
  556: 	return value
  557: }

  559: func mustLLMRequestPreflightPricer(
  560: 	t *testing.T,
  561: 	estimator ports.TokenEstimator,
  562: ) *pricing.PreflightPricer {
  563: 	t.Helper()
  564: 
  565: 	calculator, err := pricing.NewCalculator(1, 1)
  566: 	if err != nil {
  567: 		t.Fatalf("NewCalculator: %v", err)
  568: 	}
  569: 	value, err := pricing.NewPreflightPricer(
  570: 		estimator,
  571: 		calculator,
  572: 	)
  573: 	if err != nil {
  574: 		t.Fatalf("NewPreflightPricer: %v", err)
  575: 	}
  576: 	return value
  577: }

  579: func validLLMRequestRoutePreflightInput() llmrequest.
  580: 	RouteCandidatePreflightInput {
  581: 	price := domain.RoutePrice{
  582: 		RouteID:                     "route-1",
  583: 		Currency:                    "RUB",
  584: 		InputPricePer1MTokensCents:  1_000_000,
  585: 		OutputPricePer1MTokensCents: 2_000_000,
  586: 		MarkupCoefficient:           1.5,
  587: 		Enabled:                     true,
  588: 	}
  589: 	return llmrequest.RouteCandidatePreflightInput{
  590: 		Route: domain.Route{
  591: 			ID:                 "route-1",
  592: 			ResellerID:         "reseller-1",
  593: 			ProviderType:       domain.ProviderOpenAI,
  594: 			APIFamily:          domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible,
  595: 			EndpointKind:       domain.EndpointChat,

FILE: internal/app/llmrequest_route_selector.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: 9a605261020b251ec03e46e5db62df748aa71c14
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package app
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"errors"
    6: 	"fmt"
    7: 
    8: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/llmrequest"
    9: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/routing"
   10: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/ports"
   11: )
   12: 
   13: type LLMRequestRouteSelector struct {
   14: 	clock ports.Clock
   15: }
   16: 
   17: var _ llmrequest.RouteCandidateSelector = (*LLMRequestRouteSelector)(nil)
   18: 
   19: func NewLLMRequestRouteSelector(
   20: 	clock ports.Clock,
   21: ) (*LLMRequestRouteSelector, error) {
   22: 	if clock == nil {
   23: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf(
   24: 			"%w: nil route selector clock",
   25: 			llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired,
   26: 		)
   27: 	}
   28: 	return &LLMRequestRouteSelector{
   29: 		clock: clock,
   30: 	}, nil
   31: }
   32: 
   33: func (s *LLMRequestRouteSelector) Select(
   34: 	ctx context.Context,
   35: 	input llmrequest.RouteSelectionInput,
   36: ) (llmrequest.RouteSelectionResult, error) {
   37: 	if s == nil || s.clock == nil {
   38: 		return llmrequest.RouteSelectionResult{},
   39: 			llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   40: 	}
   41: 	if ctx == nil {
   42: 		return llmrequest.RouteSelectionResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   43: 			"%w: nil route selector context",
   44: 			llmrequest.ErrInvalidInput,
   45: 		)
   46: 	}
   47: 	if err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {
   48: 		return llmrequest.RouteSelectionResult{}, err
   49: 	}
   50: 
   51: 	now := s.clock.Now()
   52: 	if now.IsZero() {
   53: 		return llmrequest.RouteSelectionResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   54: 			"%w: zero route selector clock",
   55: 			llmrequest.ErrStageContractViolation,
   56: 		)
   57: 	}
   58: 
   59: 	candidates := make(
   60: 		[]routing.Candidate,
   61: 		len(input.Candidates),
   62: 	)
   63: 	for index, candidate := range input.Candidates {
   64: 		candidates[index] = routing.Candidate{
   65: 			Route:           candidate.Route,
   66: 			Reseller:        candidate.Reseller,
   67: 			SecretAvailable: candidate.Preflight.SecretAvailable,
   68: 			CostAvailable:   candidate.Preflight.CostAvailable,
   69: 			ForwardingAdapterAvailable: candidate.Preflight.
   70: 				ForwardingAdapterAvailable,
   71: 			EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: candidate.Preflight.
   72: 				EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
   73: 			RateLimitAllowed: candidate.Preflight.
   74: 				RateLimitAllowed,
   75: 			ConcurrencyAllowed: candidate.Preflight.
   76: 				ConcurrencyAllowed,
   77: 			ModelIdentifierRewriteAllowed: candidate.Preflight.
   78: 				ModelIdentifierRewriteAllowed,
   79: 		}
   80: 	}
   81: 
   82: 	selected, err := routing.Select(
   83: 		routing.SelectionInput{
   84: 			Query: ports.RouteQuery{
   85: 				APIFamily:    input.APIFamily,
   86: 				EndpointKind: input.EndpointKind,
   87: 				ClientModel:  input.ClientModel,
   88: 			},
   89: 			RequestedCapabilities: input.RequestedCapabilities,
   90: 			Candidates:            candidates,
   91: 			Now:                   now,
   92: 		},
   93: 	)
   94: 	if err != nil {
   95: 		return llmrequest.RouteSelectionResult{},
   96: 			mapLLMRequestRouteSelectionError(err)
   97: 	}
   98: 
   99: 	fallbackRouteIDs := make(
  100: 		[]string,
  101: 		len(selected.Fallbacks),
  102: 	)
  103: 	for index, fallback := range selected.Fallbacks {
  104: 		fallbackRouteIDs[index] = fallback.Route.ID
  105: 	}
  106: 	return llmrequest.RouteSelectionResult{
  107: 		SelectedRouteID:  selected.Selected.Route.ID,
  108: 		FallbackRouteIDs: fallbackRouteIDs,
  109: 	}, nil
  110: }
  111: 
  112: func mapLLMRequestRouteSelectionError(err error) error {
  113: 	switch {
  114: 	case errors.Is(err, routing.ErrUnknownModel):
  115: 		return llmrequest.ErrUnknownModel
  116: 	case errors.Is(err, routing.ErrUnsupportedCapability):
  117: 		return llmrequest.ErrUnsupportedCapability
  118: 	case errors.Is(err, routing.ErrNoRouteAvailable):
  119: 		return llmrequest.ErrNoRouteAvailable
  120: 	case errors.Is(err, routing.ErrInvalidSelectionInput),
  121: 		errors.Is(err, routing.ErrInvalidRouteData):
  122: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  123: 			"%w: %v",
  124: 			llmrequest.ErrStageContractViolation,
  125: 			err,
  126: 		)
  127: 	default:
  128: 		return fmt.Errorf("select route candidate: %w", err)
  129: 	}
  130: }

   21: func TestLLMRequestRouteSelectorDelegatesDeterministicSelection(
   22: 	t *testing.T,
   23: ) {
   24: 	now := time.Date(
   25: 		2026,
   26: 		time.June,
   27: 		14,
   28: 		12,
   29: 		0,
   30: 		0,
   31: 		0,
   32: 		time.UTC,
   33: 	)

   37: 		validLLMRequestRouteSelectionCandidate(
   38: 			"route-b",
   39: 			20,
   40: 			1,
   41: 		),
   42: 		validLLMRequestRouteSelectionCandidate(
   43: 			"route-a",
   44: 			10,
   45: 			10,
   46: 		),
   47: 	}
   48: 
   49: 	result, err := selector.Select(context.Background(), input)
   50: 	if err != nil {
   51: 		t.Fatalf("Select: %v", err)
   52: 	}

   54: 		t.Fatalf(
   55: 			"selected route = %q, want route-a",
   56: 			result.SelectedRouteID,
   57: 		)
   58: 	}
   59: 	if len(result.FallbackRouteIDs) != 1 ||
   60: 		result.FallbackRouteIDs[0] != "route-b" {
   61: 		t.Fatalf(
   62: 			"fallback routes = %#v, want route-b",
   63: 			result.FallbackRouteIDs,
   64: 		)
   65: 	}
   66: 	if input.Candidates[0].Route.ID != "route-b" ||
   67: 		input.Candidates[1].Route.ID != "route-a" {
   68: 		t.Fatalf("input candidate order was mutated")
   69: 	}
   70: }

FILE: internal/app/llmrequest_usage_resolver.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: afaa1b049f87d2e15cfcc7894f7e3d4cfc2fd547
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package app
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"fmt"
    6: 
    7: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/llmrequest"
    8: 	pricingapp "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/application/pricing"
    9: )
   10: 
   11: type LLMRequestUsageResolver struct {
   12: 	pricing *pricingapp.UsageResolver
   13: }
   14: 
   15: var _ llmrequest.UsageResolver = (*LLMRequestUsageResolver)(nil)
   16: 
   17: func NewLLMRequestUsageResolver(
   18: 	pricing *pricingapp.UsageResolver,
   19: ) (*LLMRequestUsageResolver, error) {
   20: 	if pricing == nil {
   21: 		return nil, llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   22: 	}
   23: 	return &LLMRequestUsageResolver{pricing: pricing}, nil
   24: }
   25: 
   26: func (r *LLMRequestUsageResolver) Resolve(
   27: 	ctx context.Context,
   28: 	input llmrequest.UsageResolutionInput,
   29: ) (llmrequest.UsageResolutionResult, error) {
   30: 	if r == nil || r.pricing == nil {
   31: 		return llmrequest.UsageResolutionResult{},
   32: 			llmrequest.ErrDependencyRequired
   33: 	}
   34: 	if ctx == nil {
   35: 		return llmrequest.UsageResolutionResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   36: 			"%w: nil usage resolution context",
   37: 			llmrequest.ErrInvalidInput,
   38: 		)
   39: 	}
   40: 	if err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {
   41: 		return llmrequest.UsageResolutionResult{}, err
   42: 	}
   43: 
   44: 	prepared := input.Reserved.Prepared
   45: 	result, err := r.pricing.Resolve(
   46: 		ctx,
   47: 		pricingapp.ResolveUsageInput{
   48: 			Route:        prepared.Plan.Route,
   49: 			Price:        prepared.Plan.Price,
   50: 			RequestBody:  append([]byte(nil), prepared.Payload...),
   51: 			ResponseBody: append([]byte(nil), input.Response.Body...),
   52: 			RequestedCapabilities: prepared.
   53: 				RequestedCapabilities,
   54: 			Modalities: pricingapp.InputModalities{
   55: 				Image: prepared.RequestedCapabilities.ImageInput,
   56: 				Audio: prepared.RequestedCapabilities.AudioInput,
   57: 				File:  prepared.RequestedCapabilities.FileInput,
   58: 				Video: prepared.RequestedCapabilities.VideoInput,
   59: 			},
   60: 			ZeroUsageAllowed: false,
   61: 		},
   62: 	)
   63: 	if err != nil {
   64: 		return llmrequest.UsageResolutionResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   65: 			"resolve LLM-request usage and pricing: %w",
   66: 			err,
   67: 		)
   68: 	}
   69: 
   70: 	return llmrequest.UsageResolutionResult{
   71: 		Usage:                 result.Usage,
   72: 		Completeness:          string(result.Completeness),
   73: 		Estimated:             result.Estimated,
   74: 		UpstreamCostCents:     result.UpstreamCostCents,
   75: 		ClientAmountCents:     result.ClientAmountCents,
   76: 		Currency:              result.Currency,
   77: 		ProviderRequestID:     result.ProviderRequestID,
   78: 		ProviderResponseModel: result.ProviderResponseModel,
   79: 	}, nil
   80: }

   32: 	context.Context,
   33: 	ports.TokenEstimateRequest,
   34: ) (ports.TokenEstimate, error) {
   35: 	return ports.TokenEstimate{}, errors.New("unexpected estimation")
   36: }
   37: 
   38: func TestLLMRequestUsageResolverMapsPricingResult(t *testing.T) {
   39: 	calculator, err := pricingapp.NewCalculator(1.25, 1.10)
   40: 	if err != nil {
   41: 		t.Fatal(err)
   42: 	}
   43: 	pricingResolver, err := pricingapp.NewUsageResolver(
   44: 		usageResolverExtractor{},
   45: 		usageResolverEstimator{},
   46: 		calculator,
   47: 	)
   48: 	if err != nil {
   49: 		t.Fatal(err)
   50: 	}
   51: 	resolver, err := NewLLMRequestUsageResolver(pricingResolver)
   52: 	if err != nil {
   53: 		t.Fatal(err)
   54: 	}
   55: 
   56: 	result, err := resolver.Resolve(
   57: 		context.Background(),
   58: 		llmrequest.UsageResolutionInput{
   59: 			Reserved: llmrequest.ReservedRequest{
   60: 				Prepared: llmrequest.PreparedRequest{
   61: 					RequestedCapabilities: domain.CapabilitySet{
   62: 						Chat: true,
   63: 					},
   64: 					Payload: []byte(`{"model":"model-1"}`),
   65: 					Plan: llmrequest.RoutePlan{
   66: 						Route: domain.Route{
   67: 							ID:           "route-1",
   68: 							APIFamily:    domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible,
   69: 							EndpointKind: domain.EndpointChat,
   70: 							ClientModel:  "model-1",
   71: 						},
   72: 						Price: domain.RoutePrice{
   73: 							RouteID:                     "route-1",
   74: 							Currency:                    "RUB",
   75: 							InputPricePer1MTokensCents:  1000000,
   76: 							OutputPricePer1MTokensCents: 2000000,
   77: 							MarkupCoefficient:           1,
   78: 							Enabled:                     true,
   79: 						},
   80: 					},
   81: 				},
   82: 			},
   83: 			Response: ports.ForwardResponse{
   84: 				StatusCode: 200,
   85: 				Body:       []byte(`{"usage":{}}`),
   86: 			},
   87: 		},
   88: 	)
   89: 	if err != nil {
   90: 		t.Fatalf("Resolve: %v", err)
   91: 	}
   92: 	if result.Usage.InputTokens != 10 ||
   93: 		result.Usage.OutputTokens != 5 ||
   94: 		result.Completeness != "detailed" ||
   95: 		result.Estimated ||
   96: 		result.UpstreamCostCents <= 0 ||
   97: 		result.ClientAmountCents <= 0 ||
   98: 		result.Currency != "RUB" {
   99: 		t.Fatalf("result = %+v", result)
  100: 	}
  101: }

  230: func (g RepositoryGraph) Validate() error {
  231: 	switch {
  232: 	case g.Users == nil:
  233: 		return fmt.Errorf("user repository is nil")
  234: 	case g.APIKeys == nil:
  235: 		return fmt.Errorf("API-key repository is nil")
  236: 	case g.Resellers == nil:
  237: 		return fmt.Errorf("reseller query repository is nil")
  238: 	case g.Routes == nil:
  239: 		return fmt.Errorf("route repository is nil")
  240: 	case g.ModelCatalogRoutes == nil:
  241: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  242: 			"model catalog route repository is nil",
  243: 		)
  244: 	case g.RoutePrices == nil:
  245: 		return fmt.Errorf("route-price repository is nil")
  246: 	case g.UsageLedger == nil:
  247: 		return fmt.Errorf("usage ledger is nil")
  248: 	case g.ForwardingAttempts == nil:
  249: 		return fmt.Errorf("forwarding-attempt store is nil")
  250: 	case g.LLMRequestAtomicReservation == nil:
  251: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  252: 			"LLM-request atomic reservation is nil",
  253: 		)
  254: 	case g.LLMRequestRouteReservationTransfer == nil:
  255: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  256: 			"LLM-request route reservation transfer is nil",
  257: 		)
  258: 	case g.AdminUsers == nil:
  259: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin user repository is nil")
  260: 	case g.AdminAPIKeys == nil:
  261: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin API-key repository is nil")
  262: 	case g.AdminProvisioning == nil:
  263: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  264: 			"admin API-key provisioning repository is nil",
  265: 		)
  266: 	case g.AdminAudit == nil:
  267: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin audit store is nil")
  268: 	case g.AdminResellers == nil:
  269: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin reseller repository is nil")
  270: 	case g.AdminRoutes == nil:
  271: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin route repository is nil")
  272: 	case g.AdminRoutePrices == nil:
  273: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin route-price repository is nil")
  274: 	case g.AdminUsage == nil:
  275: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin usage ledger is nil")
  276: 	case g.BillingSessions == nil:
  277: 		return fmt.Errorf("billing-session store is nil")
  278: 	case g.RouteEvents == nil:
  279: 		return fmt.Errorf("route-event store is nil")
  280: 	case g.TelegramAlerts == nil:
  281: 		return fmt.Errorf("Telegram-alert store is nil")
  282: 	case g.APIKeyProvisioning == nil:
  283: 		return fmt.Errorf("API-key provisioning store is nil")
  284: 	default:
  285: 		return nil
  286: 	}

  224: 	}
  225: 	if runtime.Handler != runtime.Transports.Root {
  226: 		t.Fatal(
  227: 			"runtime handler is not transport graph root",
  228: 		)
  229: 	}
  230: 	if err := runtime.Ping(
  231: 		context.Background(),
  232: 	); err != nil {
  233: 		t.Fatalf("runtime ping: %v", err)
  234: 	}
  235: 
  236: 	runtime.Close()
  237: 	runtime.Close()
  238: }

FILE: internal/app/transport.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: afd78b0d5656cb02f8b08f7fc060309deff052b5
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package app
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"fmt"
    5: 	"net/http"
    6: 
    7: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/config"
    8: 	adminhttp "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/transport/http/admin"
    9: 	provisioninghttp "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/transport/http/provisioning"
   10: 	publicapi "github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/transport/http/publicapi"
   11: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/transport/httptransport"
   12: )
   13: 
   14: type TransportGraph struct {
   15: 	Public http.Handler
   16: 	LLM    http.Handler
   17: 	Admin  http.Handler
   18: 
   19: 	ProvisioningEnabled bool
   20: 	Provisioning        http.Handler
   21: 
   22: 	Root http.Handler
   23: }
   24: 
   25: func NewTransportGraph(
   26: 	cfg config.Config,
   27: 	primitives RuntimePrimitives,
   28: 	security SecurityGraph,
   29: 	applications ApplicationGraph,
   30: ) (TransportGraph, error) {
   31: 	if err := primitives.Validate(); err != nil {
   32: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf("validate runtime primitives: %w", err)
   33: 	}
   34: 	if err := security.Validate(); err != nil {
   35: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf("validate security graph: %w", err)
   36: 	}
   37: 	if err := applications.Validate(); err != nil {
   38: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf("validate application graph: %w", err)
   39: 	}
   40: 	if security.ProvisioningEnabled != applications.ProvisioningEnabled {
   41: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
   42: 			"provisioning security and application capabilities disagree",
   43: 		)
   44: 	}
   45: 
   46: 	publicRouter, err := publicapi.NewRouter(
   47: 		applications.PublicAuthentication,
   48: 		applications.ModelCatalog,
   49: 		primitives.RequestIDs,
   50: 	)
   51: 	if err != nil {
   52: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
   53: 			"construct public API HTTP router: %w",
   54: 			err,
   55: 		)
   56: 	}
   57: 
   58: 	llmRouter, err := publicapi.NewLLMRouter(
   59: 		applications.LLMRequest,
   60: 		primitives.RequestIDs,
   61: 		cfg.RequestBodyMaxBytes,
   62: 	)
   63: 	if err != nil {
   64: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
   65: 			"construct public LLM HTTP router: %w",
   66: 			err,
   67: 		)
   68: 	}
   69: 
   70: 	adminRouter, err := adminhttp.NewRouter(
   71: 		applications.Admin,
   72: 		security.AdminAuthenticator,
   73: 		primitives.RequestIDs,
   74: 	)
   75: 	if err != nil {
   76: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf("construct admin HTTP router: %w", err)
   77: 	}
   78: 
   79: 	var provisioningRouter http.Handler
   80: 	if applications.ProvisioningEnabled {
   81: 		router, routerErr := provisioninghttp.NewRouter(
   82: 			applications.Provisioning,
   83: 			security.ProvisioningAuthenticator,
   84: 			primitives.RequestIDs,
   85: 			cfg.RequestBodyMaxBytes,
   86: 		)
   87: 		if routerErr != nil {
   88: 			return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf(
   89: 				"construct provisioning HTTP router: %w",
   90: 				routerErr,
   91: 			)
   92: 		}
   93: 		provisioningRouter = router
   94: 	}
   95: 
   96: 	rootRouter, err := httptransport.NewRouter(
   97: 		publicRouter,
   98: 		llmRouter,
   99: 		adminRouter,
  100: 		provisioningRouter,
  101: 	)
  102: 	if err != nil {
  103: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf("construct root HTTP router: %w", err)
  104: 	}
  105: 
  106: 	graph := TransportGraph{
  107: 		Public:              publicRouter,
  108: 		LLM:                 llmRouter,
  109: 		Admin:               adminRouter,
  110: 		ProvisioningEnabled: applications.ProvisioningEnabled,
  111: 		Provisioning:        provisioningRouter,
  112: 		Root:                rootRouter,
  113: 	}
  114: 	if err := graph.Validate(); err != nil {
  115: 		return TransportGraph{}, fmt.Errorf("validate transport graph: %w", err)
  116: 	}
  117: 	return graph, nil
  118: }
  119: 
  120: func (g TransportGraph) Validate() error {
  121: 	switch {
  122: 	case g.Public == nil:
  123: 		return fmt.Errorf("public API HTTP handler is nil")
  124: 	case g.LLM == nil:
  125: 		return fmt.Errorf("public LLM HTTP handler is nil")
  126: 	case g.Admin == nil:
  127: 		return fmt.Errorf("admin HTTP handler is nil")
  128: 	case g.ProvisioningEnabled && g.Provisioning == nil:
  129: 		return fmt.Errorf("enabled provisioning HTTP handler is nil")
  130: 	case !g.ProvisioningEnabled && g.Provisioning != nil:
  131: 		return fmt.Errorf("disabled provisioning HTTP handler is non-nil")
  132: 	case g.Root == nil:
  133: 		return fmt.Errorf("root HTTP handler is nil")
  134: 	default:
  135: 		return nil
  136: 	}
  137: }

FILE: internal/application/llmrequest/contracts.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: 76abe43c4b7b520194e2a15b2c2288e2f18bba90
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package llmrequest
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 
    6: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
    7: )
    8: 
    9: type Authenticator interface {
   10: 	Authenticate(context.Context, string) (Principal, error)
   11: }
   12: 
   13: type RequestParser interface {
   14: 	Parse(context.Context, ParseInput) (ParsedRequest, error)
   15: }
   16: 
   17: type CapabilityDetector interface {
   18: 	Detect(context.Context, CapabilityInput) (domain.CapabilitySet, error)
   19: }
   20: 
   21: type RoutePlanner interface {
   22: 	Plan(context.Context, RoutePlanInput) (RoutePlan, error)
   23: }
   24: 
   25: type BillingAdmitter interface {
   26: 	Admit(context.Context, BillingAdmissionInput) (BillingAdmissionResult, error)
   27: }
   28: 
   29: type AtomicReservation interface {
   30: 	// Reserve must create the usage reserve and increment the selected reseller
   31: 	// reserve in one atomic operation. An error must leave both states unchanged.
   32: 	Reserve(context.Context, ReservationInput) (ReservationResult, error)
   33: }
   34: 
   35: type RouteReservationTransfer interface {
   36: 	// Transfer atomically:
   37: 	//   1. verifies ExpectedUsage is still the current reserved usage record;
   38: 	//   2. removes its unused estimated upstream reserve from the previous reseller;
   39: 	//   3. adds Target.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents to the target reseller reserve;
   40: 	//   4. replaces the reserved usage routing, pricing, and estimate snapshot with
   41: 	//      the immutable Target snapshot.
   42: 	//
   43: 	// Any error must leave the usage record and both reseller balances unchanged.
   44: 	// Repeating the identical already-committed transfer is idempotent.
   45: 	Transfer(
   46: 		context.Context,
   47: 		RouteReservationTransferInput,
   48: 	) (RouteReservationTransferResult, error)
   49: }
   50: 
   51: type ForwardingStageExecutor interface {
   52: 	Execute(
   53: 		context.Context,
   54: 		PreparedRequest,
   55: 		BillingAdmissionResult,
   56: 	) (ForwardedRequest, error)
   57: }
   58: 
   59: type UsageResolver interface {
   60: 	Resolve(
   61: 		context.Context,
   62: 		UsageResolutionInput,
   63: 	) (UsageResolutionResult, error)
   64: }
   65: 
   66: type Finalizer interface {
   67: 	Commit(
   68: 		context.Context,
   69: 		FinalizationInput,
   70: 	) (FinalizationResult, error)
   71: 	MarkPricingFailed(
   72: 		context.Context,
   73: 		PricingFailureInput,
   74: 	) (FinalizationResult, error)
   75: }
   76: 
   77: type AutoCharger interface {
   78: 	Run(context.Context, AutoChargeInput) AutoChargeResult
   79: }
   80: 
   81: type Dependencies struct {
   82: 	Authenticator      Authenticator
   83: 	RequestParser      RequestParser
   84: 	CapabilityDetector CapabilityDetector
   85: 	RoutePlanner       RoutePlanner
   86: 	BillingAdmitter    BillingAdmitter
   87: 	Forwarding         ForwardingStageExecutor
   88: 	UsageResolver      UsageResolver
   89: 	Finalizer          Finalizer
   90: 	AutoCharger        AutoCharger
   91: }

    1: package llmrequest
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"errors"
    6: 	"fmt"
    7: 	"reflect"
    8: 	"testing"
    9: 
   10: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"

   12: )
   13: 
   14: type retryFailure struct {
   15: 	kind         string
   16: 	statusCode   int
   17: 	attemptState string
   18: 	retry        bool
   19: 	cause        error
   20: }
   21: 
   22: func (failure *retryFailure) Error() string                    { return failure.cause.Error() }
   23: func (failure *retryFailure) Unwrap() error                    { return failure.cause }
   24: func (failure *retryFailure) FailureKindValue() string         { return failure.kind }
   25: func (failure *retryFailure) FailureStatusCode() int           { return failure.statusCode }
   26: func (failure *retryFailure) FailureAttemptStateValue() string { return failure.attemptState }
   27: func (failure *retryFailure) FailureRouteRetryCandidate() bool { return failure.retry }
   28: 
   29: type retryTransferFunc func(
   30: 	context.Context,
   31: 	RouteReservationTransferInput,
   32: ) (RouteReservationTransferResult, error)
   33: 
   34: func (f retryTransferFunc) Transfer(
   35: 	ctx context.Context,
   36: 	input RouteReservationTransferInput,
   37: ) (RouteReservationTransferResult, error) {
   38: 	return f(ctx, input)
   39: }
   40: 
   41: func TestForwardingStageRetriesOrderedFallback(t *testing.T) {
   42: 	prepared := validForwardingPreparedRequest()
   43: 	prepared.Plan.Fallbacks = []RouteFallbackPlan{
   44: 		retryFallbackPlan(prepared, "route-2", "reseller-2"),
   45: 		retryFallbackPlan(prepared, "route-3", "reseller-3"),
   46: 	}
   47: 	var calls []string
   48: 	var attemptRoutes []string
   49: 	var reservationIDs []string
   50: 
   51: 	capacity := validForwardingCapacityManager(nil)
   52: 	capacity.acquireFunc = func(
   53: 		_ context.Context,
   54: 		input ports.RouteCapacityAcquireInput,
   55: 	) (ports.RouteCapacityReservation, error) {
   56: 		calls = append(calls, "acquire:"+input.Route.ID)
   57: 		reservationIDs = append(reservationIDs, input.ReservationID)
   58: 		return ports.RouteCapacityReservation{
   59: 			LocalRequestID: input.LocalRequestID,
   60: 			ReservationID:  input.ReservationID,
   61: 			RouteID:        input.Route.ID,
   62: 		}, nil
   63: 	}
   64: 	capacity.releaseFunc = func(
   65: 		_ context.Context,
   66: 		lease ports.RouteCapacityReservation,
   67: 	) error {
   68: 		calls = append(calls, "release:"+lease.RouteID)
   69: 		return nil
   70: 	}
   71: 
   72: 	reservation := reserveFunc(func(
   73: 		_ context.Context,
   74: 		input ReservationInput,
   75: 	) (ReservationResult, error) {
   76: 		calls = append(calls, "reserve:"+input.Route.ID)
   77: 		return validReservation(input), nil
   78: 	})
   79: 	transfer := retryTransferFunc(func(
   80: 		_ context.Context,
   81: 		input RouteReservationTransferInput,
   82: 	) (RouteReservationTransferResult, error) {
   83: 		calls = append(calls, "transfer:"+input.Target.Route.ID)
   84: 		usage := input.ExpectedUsage
   85: 		usage.SelectedRouteID = input.Target.Route.ID
   86: 		usage.SelectedResellerID = input.Target.Reseller.ID
   87: 		usage.ProviderType = input.Target.Route.ProviderType
   88: 		usage.ProviderModel = input.Target.Route.ProviderModel
   89: 		usage.BillingModel = input.Target.BillingModel
   90: 		usage.EstimatedUsage = input.Target.EstimatedUsage
   91: 		usage.EstimatedClientAmountCents = input.Target.EstimatedClientAmountCents
   92: 		usage.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents = input.Target.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents
   93: 		usage.Currency = input.Target.Currency
   94: 		return RouteReservationTransferResult{
   95: 			Usage:            usage,
   96: 			ReservedReseller: input.Target.Reseller,
   97: 		}, nil
   98: 	})
   99: 	attempts := &forwardingAttemptStoreStub{
  100: 		startFunc: func(
  101: 			_ context.Context,
  102: 			attempt domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  103: 		) (domain.ForwardingAttempt, error) {
  104: 			calls = append(calls, fmt.Sprintf(
  105: 				"start:%d:%s",
  106: 				attempt.AttemptNumber,
  107: 				attempt.RouteID,
  108: 			))
  109: 			attemptRoutes = append(attemptRoutes, attempt.RouteID)
  110: 			return attempt, nil
  111: 		},
  112: 		completeFunc: func(
  113: 			_ context.Context,
  114: 			attempt domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  115: 		) (domain.ForwardingAttempt, error) {
  116: 			calls = append(calls, fmt.Sprintf(
  117: 				"complete:%d:%s",
  118: 				attempt.AttemptNumber,
  119: 				attempt.Status,
  120: 			))
  121: 			return attempt, nil
  122: 		},
  123: 	}
  124: 	forwardCalls := 0
  125: 	forwarder := forwardingExecutorFunc(func(
  126: 		_ context.Context,
  127: 		input ForwardingExecutionInput,
  128: 	) (ForwardingExecutionResult, error) {
  129: 		calls = append(calls, "forward:"+input.Prepared.Plan.Route.ID)
  130: 		forwardCalls++
  131: 		if forwardCalls == 1 {
  132: 			return ForwardingExecutionResult{}, &retryFailure{
  133: 				kind:         "rate_limited",
  134: 				statusCode:   429,
  135: 				attemptState: string(domain.ForwardingAttemptStateResponseReceived),
  136: 				retry:        true,
  137: 				cause:        errors.New("rate limited"),
  138: 			}
  139: 		}
  140: 		return ForwardingExecutionResult{
  141: 			Response: ports.ForwardResponse{
  142: 				StatusCode: 200,
  143: 				Body:       []byte(`{"ok":true}`),
  144: 			},
  145: 		}, nil
  146: 	})
  147: 
  148: 	stage, err := NewForwardingStage(
  149: 		capacity,
  150: 		reservation,
  151: 		transfer,
  152: 		attempts,
  153: 		forwardingStageClock{now: validForwardingStageTime()},
  154: 		forwarder,
  155: 	)
  156: 	if err != nil {
  157: 		t.Fatalf("NewForwardingStage: %v", err)
  158: 	}
  159: 	result, err := stage.Execute(
  160: 		context.Background(),
  161: 		prepared,
  162: 		validForwardingAdmission(prepared),
  163: 	)
  164: 	if err != nil {
  165: 		t.Fatalf("Execute: %v", err)
  166: 	}
  167: 	if result.Reserved.Prepared.Plan.Route.ID != "route-2" ||
  168: 		result.Reserved.Reservation.Usage.SelectedRouteID != "route-2" {
  169: 		t.Fatalf("result = %+v", result)
  170: 	}
  171: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(
  172: 		attemptRoutes,
  173: 		[]string{prepared.Plan.Route.ID, "route-2"},
  174: 	) {
  175: 		t.Fatalf("attempt routes = %#v", attemptRoutes)
  176: 	}
  177: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(
  178: 		reservationIDs,
  179: 		[]string{
  180: 			prepared.LocalRequestID + ":attempt:1",
  181: 			prepared.LocalRequestID + ":attempt:2",
  182: 		},
  183: 	) {
  184: 		t.Fatalf("reservation IDs = %#v", reservationIDs)
  185: 	}
  186: 	wantCalls := []string{
  187: 		"acquire:" + prepared.Plan.Route.ID,
  188: 		"reserve:" + prepared.Plan.Route.ID,
  189: 		"start:1:" + prepared.Plan.Route.ID,
  190: 		"forward:" + prepared.Plan.Route.ID,
  191: 		"complete:1:failed",
  192: 		"release:" + prepared.Plan.Route.ID,
  193: 		"acquire:route-2",
  194: 		"transfer:route-2",
  195: 		"start:2:route-2",
  196: 		"forward:route-2",
  197: 		"complete:2:succeeded",
  198: 		"release:route-2",
  199: 	}
  200: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(calls, wantCalls) {
  201: 		t.Fatalf("calls = %#v, want %#v", calls, wantCalls)
  202: 	}
  203: }
  204: 
  205: func TestForwardingStageSkipsCapacityUnavailableCandidate(t *testing.T) {
  206: 	prepared := validForwardingPreparedRequest()
  207: 	prepared.Plan.Fallbacks = []RouteFallbackPlan{
  208: 		retryFallbackPlan(prepared, "route-2", "reseller-2"),
  209: 	}
  210: 	capacity := validForwardingCapacityManager(nil)
  211: 	acquires := 0
  212: 	capacity.acquireFunc = func(
  213: 		_ context.Context,
  214: 		input ports.RouteCapacityAcquireInput,
  215: 	) (ports.RouteCapacityReservation, error) {
  216: 		acquires++
  217: 		if acquires == 1 {
  218: 			return ports.RouteCapacityReservation{}, ports.ErrRouteCapacityUnavailable
  219: 		}
  220: 		return ports.RouteCapacityReservation{
  221: 			LocalRequestID: input.LocalRequestID,
  222: 			ReservationID:  input.ReservationID,
  223: 			RouteID:        input.Route.ID,
  224: 		}, nil
  225: 	}
  226: 	reservedRoute := ""
  227: 	stage, err := NewForwardingStage(
  228: 		capacity,
  229: 		reserveFunc(func(
  230: 			_ context.Context,
  231: 			input ReservationInput,
  232: 		) (ReservationResult, error) {
  233: 			reservedRoute = input.Route.ID
  234: 			return validReservation(input), nil
  235: 		}),
  236: 		retryTransferFunc(func(
  237: 			context.Context,
  238: 			RouteReservationTransferInput,
  239: 		) (RouteReservationTransferResult, error) {
  240: 			t.Fatal("transfer must not run before initial reserve")
  241: 			return RouteReservationTransferResult{}, nil
  242: 		}),
  243: 		&forwardingAttemptStoreStub{},
  244: 		forwardingStageClock{now: validForwardingStageTime()},
  245: 		forwardingExecutorFunc(func(
  246: 			_ context.Context,
  247: 			input ForwardingExecutionInput,
  248: 		) (ForwardingExecutionResult, error) {
  249: 			return ForwardingExecutionResult{
  250: 				Response: ports.ForwardResponse{StatusCode: 200},
  251: 			}, nil
  252: 		}),
  253: 	)
  254: 	if err != nil {
  255: 		t.Fatalf("NewForwardingStage: %v", err)
  256: 	}
  257: 	result, err := stage.Execute(
  258: 		context.Background(),
  259: 		prepared,
  260: 		validForwardingAdmission(prepared),
  261: 	)
  262: 	if err != nil {
  263: 		t.Fatalf("Execute: %v", err)
  264: 	}
  265: 	if reservedRoute != "route-2" ||
  266: 		result.Reserved.Prepared.Plan.Route.ID != "route-2" {
  267: 		t.Fatalf("reserved=%q result=%+v", reservedRoute, result)
  268: 	}
  269: }
  270: 
  271: func TestForwardingStageDoesNotRetrySentNoResponse(t *testing.T) {
  272: 	prepared := validForwardingPreparedRequest()
  273: 	prepared.Plan.Fallbacks = []RouteFallbackPlan{
  274: 		retryFallbackPlan(prepared, "route-2", "reseller-2"),
  275: 	}
  276: 	capacity := validForwardingCapacityManager(nil)
  277: 	acquires := 0
  278: 	capacity.acquireFunc = func(
  279: 		_ context.Context,
  280: 		input ports.RouteCapacityAcquireInput,
  281: 	) (ports.RouteCapacityReservation, error) {
  282: 		acquires++
  283: 		return ports.RouteCapacityReservation{
  284: 			LocalRequestID: input.LocalRequestID,
  285: 			ReservationID:  input.ReservationID,
  286: 			RouteID:        input.Route.ID,
  287: 		}, nil
  288: 	}
  289: 	forwardErr := &retryFailure{
  290: 		kind:         "unavailable",
  291: 		statusCode:   0,
  292: 		attemptState: string(domain.ForwardingAttemptStateSentNoResponse),
  293: 		retry:        true,
  294: 		cause:        errors.New("connection lost"),
  295: 	}
  296: 	stage, err := NewForwardingStage(
  297: 		capacity,
  298: 		reserveFunc(func(
  299: 			_ context.Context,
  300: 			input ReservationInput,
  301: 		) (ReservationResult, error) {
  302: 			return validReservation(input), nil
  303: 		}),
  304: 		retryTransferFunc(func(
  305: 			context.Context,
  306: 			RouteReservationTransferInput,
  307: 		) (RouteReservationTransferResult, error) {
  308: 			t.Fatal("transfer must not run")
  309: 			return RouteReservationTransferResult{}, nil
  310: 		}),
  311: 		&forwardingAttemptStoreStub{},
  312: 		forwardingStageClock{now: validForwardingStageTime()},
  313: 		forwardingExecutorFunc(func(
  314: 			context.Context,
  315: 			ForwardingExecutionInput,
  316: 		) (ForwardingExecutionResult, error) {
  317: 			return ForwardingExecutionResult{}, forwardErr
  318: 		}),
  319: 	)
  320: 	if err != nil {
  321: 		t.Fatalf("NewForwardingStage: %v", err)
  322: 	}
  323: 	_, err = stage.Execute(
  324: 		context.Background(),
  325: 		prepared,
  326: 		validForwardingAdmission(prepared),
  327: 	)
  328: 	if !errors.Is(err, forwardErr) {
  329: 		t.Fatalf("error = %v", err)
  330: 	}
  331: 	if acquires != 1 {
  332: 		t.Fatalf("acquires = %d, want 1", acquires)
  333: 	}
  334: }
  335: 
  336: func retryFallbackPlan(
  337: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  338: 	routeID string,
  339: 	resellerID string,
  340: ) RouteFallbackPlan {
  341: 	route := prepared.Plan.Route
  342: 	route.ID = routeID
  343: 	route.ResellerID = resellerID
  344: 	route.ProviderModel = "provider-" + routeID
  345: 	reseller := prepared.Plan.Reseller
  346: 	reseller.ID = resellerID
  347: 	reseller.APIKeyEnv = "KEY_" + resellerID
  348: 	return RouteFallbackPlan{
  349: 		Route:                      route,
  350: 		Reseller:                   reseller,
  351: 		Price:                      prepared.Plan.Price,
  352: 		BillingModel:               prepared.Plan.BillingModel,
  353: 		EstimatedUsage:             prepared.Plan.EstimatedUsage,
  354: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: prepared.Plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  355: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: prepared.Plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
  356: 		Currency:                   prepared.Plan.Currency,
  357: 		Confidence:                 prepared.Plan.Confidence,
  358: 	}
  359: }

    1: package llmrequest
