    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"errors"
    6: 	"fmt"
    7: 	"time"
    8: 
    9: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
   10: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/ports"
   11: )
   12: 
   13: type ForwardingExecutionInput struct {
   14: 	Prepared    PreparedRequest
   15: 	Admission   BillingAdmissionResult
   16: 	Reservation ReservationResult
   17: }
   18: 
   19: type ForwardingExecutionResult struct {
   20: 	Response ports.ForwardResponse
   21: }
   22: 
   23: type ForwardingExecutor interface {
   24: 	Forward(
   25: 		context.Context,
   26: 		ForwardingExecutionInput,
   27: 	) (ForwardingExecutionResult, error)
   28: }
   29: 
   30: type ForwardingFailure interface {
   31: 	error
   32: 	FailureKindValue() string
   33: 	FailureStatusCode() int
   34: 	FailureAttemptStateValue() string
   35: 	FailureRouteRetryCandidate() bool
   36: }
   37: 
   38: type ForwardingStage struct {
   39: 	capacity    ports.RouteCapacityManager
   40: 	reservation AtomicReservation
   41: 	transfer    RouteReservationTransfer
   42: 	attempts    ports.ForwardingAttemptStore
   43: 	clock       ports.Clock
   44: 	forwarder   ForwardingExecutor
   45: }
   46: 
   47: type ForwardedRequest struct {
   48: 	Reserved         ReservedRequest
   49: 	Response         ports.ForwardResponse
   50: 	ResolvedUsage    UsageResolutionResult
   51: 	FinalUsageRecord domain.UsageRecord
   52: 	AutoCharge       AutoChargeResult
   53: }
   54: 
   55: func NewForwardingStage(
   56: 	capacity ports.RouteCapacityManager,
   57: 	reservation AtomicReservation,
   58: 	transfer RouteReservationTransfer,
   59: 	attempts ports.ForwardingAttemptStore,
   60: 	clock ports.Clock,
   61: 	forwarder ForwardingExecutor,
   62: ) (*ForwardingStage, error) {
   63: 	if capacity == nil ||
   64: 		reservation == nil ||
   65: 		transfer == nil ||
   66: 		attempts == nil ||
   67: 		clock == nil ||
   68: 		forwarder == nil {
   69: 		return nil, ErrDependencyRequired
   70: 	}
   71: 	return &ForwardingStage{
   72: 		capacity:    capacity,
   73: 		reservation: reservation,
   74: 		transfer:    transfer,
   75: 		attempts:    attempts,
   76: 		clock:       clock,
   77: 		forwarder:   forwarder,
   78: 	}, nil
   79: }
   80: 
   81: func (s *ForwardingStage) Execute(
   82: 	ctx context.Context,
   83: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
   84: 	admission BillingAdmissionResult,
   85: ) (result ForwardedRequest, err error) {
   86: 	if s == nil || s.capacity == nil || s.reservation == nil ||
   87: 		s.transfer == nil || s.attempts == nil || s.clock == nil ||
   88: 		s.forwarder == nil {
   89: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, ErrDependencyRequired
   90: 	}
   91: 	if ctx == nil {
   92: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
   93: 			"%w: nil forwarding stage context",
   94: 			ErrInvalidInput,
   95: 		)
   96: 	}
   97: 	if err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {
   98: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, err
   99: 	}
  100: 	if err := validateBillingAdmission(prepared, admission); err != nil {
  101: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, err
  102: 	}
  103: 
  104: 	candidates := forwardingCandidates(prepared.Plan)
  105: 	var reservation ReservationResult
  106: 	reservationCreated := false
  107: 	var lastForwardErr error
  108: 	var lastCapacityErr error
  109: 
  110: 	for index, candidate := range candidates {
  111: 		attemptNumber := index + 1
  112: 		candidatePrepared := preparedForForwardingCandidate(
  113: 			prepared,
  114: 			candidate,
  115: 			candidates[index+1:],
  116: 		)
  117: 		lease, acquireErr := s.capacity.Acquire(
  118: 			ctx,
  119: 			ports.RouteCapacityAcquireInput{
  120: 				LocalRequestID: candidatePrepared.LocalRequestID,
  121: 				ReservationID: forwardingCapacityReservationID(
  122: 					candidatePrepared.LocalRequestID,
  123: 					attemptNumber,
  124: 				),
  125: 				Route:          candidatePrepared.Plan.Route,
  126: 				Reseller:       candidatePrepared.Plan.Reseller,
  127: 				EstimatedUsage: candidatePrepared.Plan.EstimatedUsage,
  128: 			},
  129: 		)
  130: 		if acquireErr != nil {
  131: 			if errors.Is(acquireErr, ports.ErrRouteCapacityUnavailable) {
  132: 				lastCapacityErr = fmt.Errorf(
  133: 					"route %q capacity unavailable: %w",
  134: 					candidatePrepared.Plan.Route.ID,
  135: 					acquireErr,
  136: 				)
  137: 				continue
  138: 			}
  139: 			return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  140: 				"acquire route capacity: %w",
  141: 				acquireErr,
  142: 			)
  143: 		}
  144: 		if err := validateForwardingCapacityLease(
  145: 			lease,
  146: 			candidatePrepared,
  147: 			attemptNumber,
  148: 		); err != nil {
  149: 			releaseErr := s.capacity.Release(
  150: 				context.WithoutCancel(ctx),
  151: 				lease,
  152: 			)
  153: 			return ForwardedRequest{}, errors.Join(err, releaseErr)
  154: 		}
  155: 
  156: 		attemptResult, attemptErr := s.executeLeasedCandidate(
  157: 			ctx,
  158: 			candidatePrepared,
  159: 			admission,
  160: 			reservation,
  161: 			reservationCreated,
  162: 			candidate,
  163: 			attemptNumber,
  164: 			lease,
  165: 		)
  166: 		if attemptResult.Reservation.Usage.LocalRequestID != "" {
  167: 			reservation = attemptResult.Reservation
  168: 			reservationCreated = true
  169: 		}
  170: 		if attemptErr == nil {
  171: 			return ForwardedRequest{
  172: 				Reserved: ReservedRequest{
  173: 					Prepared:  clonePreparedRequest(attemptResult.Prepared),
  174: 					Admission: admission,
  175: 					Reservation: cloneReservationResult(
  176: 						attemptResult.Reservation,
  177: 					),
  178: 				},
  179: 				Response: cloneForwardResponse(
  180: 					attemptResult.Execution.Response,
  181: 				),
  182: 			}, nil
  183: 		}
  184: 		lastForwardErr = attemptErr
  185: 		if !attemptResult.RetryAllowed {
  186: 			return ForwardedRequest{}, attemptErr
  187: 		}
  188: 		if err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {
  189: 			return ForwardedRequest{}, errors.Join(attemptErr, err)
  190: 		}
  191: 	}
  192: 
  193: 	switch {
  194: 	case lastForwardErr != nil && lastCapacityErr != nil:
  195: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, errors.Join(lastForwardErr, lastCapacityErr)
  196: 	case lastForwardErr != nil:
  197: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, lastForwardErr
  198: 	case lastCapacityErr != nil:
  199: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, lastCapacityErr
  200: 	default:
  201: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  202: 			"%w: empty forwarding candidate plan",
  203: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  204: 		)
  205: 	}
  206: }
  207: 
  208: type forwardingCandidate struct {
  209: 	Plan RouteFallbackPlan
  210: }
  211: 
  212: type leasedCandidateResult struct {
  213: 	Prepared     PreparedRequest
  214: 	Reservation  ReservationResult
  215: 	Execution    ForwardingExecutionResult
  216: 	RetryAllowed bool
  217: }
  218: 
  219: func (s *ForwardingStage) executeLeasedCandidate(
  220: 	ctx context.Context,
  221: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  222: 	admission BillingAdmissionResult,
  223: 	current ReservationResult,
  224: 	reservationCreated bool,
  225: 	candidate forwardingCandidate,
  226: 	attemptNumber int,
  227: 	lease ports.RouteCapacityReservation,
  228: ) (result leasedCandidateResult, err error) {
  229: 	defer func() {
  230: 		releaseErr := s.capacity.Release(
  231: 			context.WithoutCancel(ctx),
  232: 			lease,
  233: 		)
  234: 		if releaseErr != nil {
  235: 			err = errors.Join(
  236: 				err,
  237: 				fmt.Errorf("release route capacity: %w", releaseErr),
  238: 			)
  239: 			result.RetryAllowed = false
  240: 		}
  241: 	}()
  242: 
  243: 	reservation := current
  244: 	if !reservationCreated {
  245: 		created, reserveErr := s.reservation.Reserve(
  246: 			ctx,
  247: 			reservationInput(prepared),
  248: 		)
  249: 		if reserveErr != nil {
  250: 			return leasedCandidateResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
  251: 				"reserve usage and reseller balance: %w",
  252: 				reserveErr,
  253: 			)
  254: 		}
  255: 		if err := validateReservation(prepared, created); err != nil {
  256: 			return leasedCandidateResult{}, err
  257: 		}
  258: 		reservation = created
  259: 	} else {
  260: 		transferred, transferErr := s.transfer.Transfer(
  261: 			ctx,
  262: 			RouteReservationTransferInput{
  263: 				ExpectedUsage: current.Usage,
  264: 				Target:        candidate.Plan,
  265: 			},
  266: 		)
  267: 		if transferErr != nil {
  268: 			return leasedCandidateResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
  269: 				"transfer route reservation: %w",
  270: 				transferErr,
  271: 			)
  272: 		}
  273: 		var validationErr error
  274: 		reservation, validationErr = validateTransferredReservation(
  275: 			prepared,
  276: 			current,
  277: 			transferred,
  278: 		)
  279: 		if validationErr != nil {
  280: 			return leasedCandidateResult{}, validationErr
  281: 		}
  282: 	}
  283: 
  284: 	result.Prepared = clonePreparedRequest(prepared)
  285: 	result.Reservation = cloneReservationResult(reservation)
  286: 
  287: 	startedAt, err := forwardingStageNow(s.clock)
  288: 	if err != nil {
  289: 		return result, err
  290: 	}
  291: 	started := forwardingAttemptStarted(prepared, attemptNumber, startedAt)
  292: 	persistedStarted, err := s.attempts.StartAttempt(ctx, started)
  293: 	if err != nil {
  294: 		return result, fmt.Errorf("start forwarding attempt: %w", err)
  295: 	}
  296: 	if !forwardingAttemptsEqual(persistedStarted, started) {
  297: 		return result, fmt.Errorf(
  298: 			"%w: invalid started forwarding attempt",
  299: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  300: 		)
  301: 	}
  302: 
  303: 	execution, forwardErr := s.forwarder.Forward(
  304: 		ctx,
  305: 		ForwardingExecutionInput{
  306: 			Prepared:    clonePreparedRequest(prepared),
  307: 			Admission:   admission,
  308: 			Reservation: cloneReservationResult(reservation),
  309: 		},
  310: 	)
  311: 	result.Execution = execution
  312: 	completedAt, clockErr := forwardingStageNow(s.clock)
  313: 	if clockErr != nil {
  314: 		return result, errors.Join(forwardErr, clockErr)
  315: 	}
  316: 	if forwardErr == nil {
  317: 		terminal, terminalErr := succeededForwardingAttempt(
  318: 			started,
  319: 			completedAt,
  320: 			execution.Response.StatusCode,
  321: 		)
  322: 		if terminalErr != nil {
  323: 			return result, terminalErr
  324: 		}
  325: 		persisted, completionErr := s.attempts.CompleteAttempt(
  326: 			context.WithoutCancel(ctx),
  327: 			terminal,
  328: 		)
  329: 		if completionErr != nil {
  330: 			return result, fmt.Errorf(
  331: 				"complete successful forwarding attempt: %w",
  332: 				completionErr,
  333: 			)
  334: 		}
  335: 		if !forwardingAttemptsEqual(persisted, terminal) {
  336: 			return result, fmt.Errorf(
  337: 				"%w: invalid successful forwarding attempt",
  338: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  339: 			)
  340: 		}
  341: 		return result, nil
  342: 	}
  343: 
  344: 	terminal, classificationErr := failedForwardingAttempt(
  345: 		started,
  346: 		completedAt,
  347: 		forwardErr,
  348: 	)
  349: 	if classificationErr != nil {
  350: 		return result, errors.Join(forwardErr, classificationErr)
  351: 	}
  352: 	persisted, completionErr := s.attempts.CompleteAttempt(
  353: 		context.WithoutCancel(ctx),
  354: 		terminal,
  355: 	)
  356: 	if completionErr != nil {
  357: 		return result, errors.Join(
  358: 			forwardErr,
  359: 			fmt.Errorf(
  360: 				"complete failed forwarding attempt: %w",
  361: 				completionErr,
  362: 			),
  363: 		)
  364: 	}
  365: 	if !forwardingAttemptsEqual(persisted, terminal) {
  366: 		return result, errors.Join(
  367: 			forwardErr,
  368: 			fmt.Errorf(
  369: 				"%w: invalid failed forwarding attempt",
  370: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  371: 			),
  372: 		)
  373: 	}
  374: 	result.RetryAllowed = forwardingAttemptAllowsRetry(ctx, terminal)
  375: 	return result, fmt.Errorf(
  376: 		"forward route %q attempt %d: %w",
  377: 		prepared.Plan.Route.ID,
  378: 		attemptNumber,
  379: 		forwardErr,
  380: 	)
  381: }
  382: 
  383: func forwardingCandidates(plan RoutePlan) []forwardingCandidate {
  384: 	result := make([]forwardingCandidate, 0, 1+len(plan.Fallbacks))
  385: 	result = append(result, forwardingCandidate{Plan: RouteFallbackPlan{
  386: 		Route:                      plan.Route,
  387: 		Reseller:                   plan.Reseller,
  388: 		Price:                      plan.Price,
  389: 		BillingModel:               plan.BillingModel,
  390: 		EstimatedUsage:             plan.EstimatedUsage,
  391: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  392: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
  393: 		Currency:                   plan.Currency,
  394: 		Confidence:                 plan.Confidence,
  395: 	}})
  396: 	for _, fallback := range plan.Fallbacks {
  397: 		result = append(result, forwardingCandidate{
  398: 			Plan: cloneRouteFallbackPlan(fallback),
  399: 		})
  400: 	}
  401: 	return result
  402: }
  403: 
  404: func preparedForForwardingCandidate(
  405: 	base PreparedRequest,
  406: 	candidate forwardingCandidate,
  407: 	remaining []forwardingCandidate,
  408: ) PreparedRequest {
  409: 	result := clonePreparedRequest(base)
  410: 	result.Plan = RoutePlan{
  411: 		Route:                      candidate.Plan.Route,
  412: 		Reseller:                   candidate.Plan.Reseller,
  413: 		Price:                      candidate.Plan.Price,
  414: 		BillingModel:               candidate.Plan.BillingModel,
  415: 		EstimatedUsage:             candidate.Plan.EstimatedUsage,
  416: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: candidate.Plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  417: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: candidate.Plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
  418: 		Currency:                   candidate.Plan.Currency,
  419: 		Confidence:                 candidate.Plan.Confidence,
  420: 		Fallbacks:                  make([]RouteFallbackPlan, 0, len(remaining)),
  421: 	}
  422: 	for _, next := range remaining {
  423: 		result.Plan.Fallbacks = append(
  424: 			result.Plan.Fallbacks,
  425: 			cloneRouteFallbackPlan(next.Plan),
  426: 		)
  427: 	}
  428: 	return result
  429: }
  430: 
  431: func cloneRouteFallbackPlan(value RouteFallbackPlan) RouteFallbackPlan {
  432: 	return RouteFallbackPlan{
  433: 		Route:                      value.Route,
  434: 		Reseller:                   value.Reseller,
  435: 		Price:                      value.Price,
  436: 		BillingModel:               value.BillingModel,
  437: 		EstimatedUsage:             value.EstimatedUsage,
  438: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: value.EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  439: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: value.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
  440: 		Currency:                   value.Currency,
  441: 		Confidence:                 value.Confidence,
  442: 	}
  443: }
  444: 
  445: func validateForwardingCapacityLease(
  446: 	lease ports.RouteCapacityReservation,
  447: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  448: 	attemptNumber int,
  449: ) error {
  450: 	if lease.LocalRequestID != prepared.LocalRequestID ||
  451: 		lease.ReservationID != forwardingCapacityReservationID(
  452: 			prepared.LocalRequestID,
  453: 			attemptNumber,
  454: 		) ||
  455: 		lease.RouteID != prepared.Plan.Route.ID {
  456: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  457: 			"%w: invalid route capacity reservation",
  458: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  459: 		)
  460: 	}
  461: 	return nil
  462: }
  463: 
  464: func validateTransferredReservation(
  465: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  466: 	previous ReservationResult,
  467: 	transferred RouteReservationTransferResult,
  468: ) (ReservationResult, error) {
  469: 	usage := transferred.Usage
  470: 	if usage.LocalRequestID != prepared.LocalRequestID ||
  471: 		usage.Status != domain.UsageStatusReserved ||
  472: 		usage.SelectedRouteID != prepared.Plan.Route.ID ||
  473: 		usage.SelectedResellerID != prepared.Plan.Reseller.ID ||
  474: 		usage.ProviderType != prepared.Plan.Route.ProviderType ||
  475: 		usage.ProviderModel != prepared.Plan.Route.ProviderModel ||
  476: 		usage.BillingModel != prepared.Plan.BillingModel ||
  477: 		usage.EstimatedUsage != prepared.Plan.EstimatedUsage ||
  478: 		usage.EstimatedClientAmountCents != prepared.Plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents ||
  479: 		usage.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents != prepared.Plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents ||
  480: 		usage.Currency != prepared.Plan.Currency ||
  481: 		transferred.ReservedReseller.ID != prepared.Plan.Reseller.ID {
  482: 		return ReservationResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
  483: 			"%w: invalid transferred route reservation",
  484: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  485: 		)
  486: 	}
  487: 	reseller := transferred.ReservedReseller
  488: 	return ReservationResult{
  489: 		Disposition: previous.Disposition,
  490: 		Usage:       usage,
  491: 		Reseller:    &reseller,
  492: 	}, nil
  493: }
  494: 
  495: func forwardingAttemptAllowsRetry(
  496: 	ctx context.Context,
  497: 	attempt domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  498: ) bool {
  499: 	if ctx == nil || ctx.Err() != nil || !attempt.RouteRetryCandidate {
  500: 		return false
  501: 	}
  502: 	switch attempt.AttemptState {
  503: 	case domain.ForwardingAttemptStateNotSent,
  504: 		domain.ForwardingAttemptStateResponseReceived:
  505: 		return true
  506: 	case domain.ForwardingAttemptStateSentNoResponse:
  507: 		return false
  508: 	default:
  509: 		return false
  510: 	}
  511: }
  512: 
  513: func forwardingCapacityReservationID(
  514: 	localRequestID string,
  515: 	attemptNumber int,
  516: ) string {
  517: 	return fmt.Sprintf(
  518: 		"%s:attempt:%d",
  519: 		localRequestID,
  520: 		attemptNumber,
  521: 	)
  522: }
  523: 
  524: func forwardingStageNow(clock ports.Clock) (time.Time, error) {
  525: 	now := clock.Now()
  526: 	if now.IsZero() || now.Location() != time.UTC {
  527: 		return time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(
  528: 			"%w: invalid forwarding stage clock",
  529: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  530: 		)
  531: 	}
  532: 	return now, nil
  533: }
  534: 
  535: func forwardingAttemptStarted(
  536: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  537: 	attemptNumber int,
  538: 	startedAt time.Time,
  539: ) domain.ForwardingAttempt {
  540: 	route := prepared.Plan.Route
  541: 	return domain.ForwardingAttempt{
  542: 		LocalRequestID: prepared.LocalRequestID,
  543: 		AttemptNumber:  attemptNumber,
  544: 		RouteID:        route.ID,
  545: 		ResellerID:     prepared.Plan.Reseller.ID,
  546: 		APIFamily:      prepared.APIFamily,
  547: 		EndpointKind:   prepared.EndpointKind,
  548: 		ClientModel:    prepared.ClientModel,
  549: 		ProviderType:   route.ProviderType,
  550: 		ProviderModel:  route.ProviderModel,
  551: 		Status: domain.
  552: 			ForwardingAttemptStatusStarted,
  553: 		StartedAt: startedAt,
  554: 	}
  555: }
  556: 
  557: func succeededForwardingAttempt(
  558: 	started domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  559: 	completedAt time.Time,
  560: 	statusCode int,
  561: ) (domain.ForwardingAttempt, error) {
  562: 	if statusCode < 200 || statusCode > 299 ||
  563: 		completedAt.Before(started.StartedAt) {
  564: 		return domain.ForwardingAttempt{}, fmt.Errorf(
  565: 			"%w: invalid successful forwarding result",
  566: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  567: 		)
  568: 	}
  569: 	result := started
  570: 	result.Status = domain.ForwardingAttemptStatusSucceeded
  571: 	result.AttemptState =
  572: 		domain.ForwardingAttemptStateResponseReceived
  573: 	result.UpstreamStatusCode = statusCode
  574: 	result.CompletedAt = &completedAt
  575: 	return result, nil
  576: }
  577: 
  578: func failedForwardingAttempt(
  579: 	started domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  580: 	completedAt time.Time,
  581: 	forwardErr error,
  582: ) (domain.ForwardingAttempt, error) {
  583: 	var failure ForwardingFailure
  584: 	if !errors.As(forwardErr, &failure) || failure == nil {
  585: 		return domain.ForwardingAttempt{}, fmt.Errorf(
  586: 			"%w: forwarding executor returned unclassified error",
  587: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  588: 		)
  589: 	}
  590: 	attemptState := domain.ForwardingAttemptState(
  591: 		failure.FailureAttemptStateValue(),
  592: 	)
  593: 	switch attemptState {
  594: 	case domain.ForwardingAttemptStateNotSent,
  595: 		domain.ForwardingAttemptStateSentNoResponse,
  596: 		domain.ForwardingAttemptStateResponseReceived:
  597: 	default:
  598: 		return domain.ForwardingAttempt{}, fmt.Errorf(
  599: 			"%w: invalid forwarding failure attempt state",
  600: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  601: 		)
  602: 	}
  603: 	statusCode := failure.FailureStatusCode()
  604: 	if statusCode < 0 || statusCode > 599 ||
  605: 		(statusCode > 0 && statusCode < 100) ||
  606: 		failure.FailureKindValue() == "" ||
  607: 		completedAt.Before(started.StartedAt) {
  608: 		return domain.ForwardingAttempt{}, fmt.Errorf(
  609: 			"%w: invalid forwarding failure classification",
  610: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  611: 		)
  612: 	}
  613: 	result := started
  614: 	result.Status = domain.ForwardingAttemptStatusFailed
  615: 	result.AttemptState = attemptState
  616: 	result.UpstreamStatusCode = statusCode
  617: 	result.FailureKind = failure.FailureKindValue()
  618: 	result.RouteRetryCandidate =
  619: 		failure.FailureRouteRetryCandidate()
  620: 	result.CompletedAt = &completedAt
  621: 	return result, nil
  622: }
  623: 
  624: func forwardingAttemptsEqual(
  625: 	left domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  626: 	right domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  627: ) bool {
  628: 	return left.LocalRequestID == right.LocalRequestID &&
  629: 		left.AttemptNumber == right.AttemptNumber &&
  630: 		left.RouteID == right.RouteID &&
  631: 		left.ResellerID == right.ResellerID &&
  632: 		left.APIFamily == right.APIFamily &&
  633: 		left.EndpointKind == right.EndpointKind &&
  634: 		left.ClientModel == right.ClientModel &&
  635: 		left.ProviderType == right.ProviderType &&
  636: 		left.ProviderModel == right.ProviderModel &&
  637: 		left.Status == right.Status &&
  638: 		left.AttemptState == right.AttemptState &&
  639: 		left.UpstreamStatusCode == right.UpstreamStatusCode &&
  640: 		left.FailureKind == right.FailureKind &&
  641: 		left.RouteRetryCandidate == right.RouteRetryCandidate &&
  642: 		left.StartedAt.Equal(right.StartedAt) &&
  643: 		equalForwardingAttemptTimes(
  644: 			left.CompletedAt,
  645: 			right.CompletedAt,
  646: 		)
  647: }
  648: 
  649: func equalForwardingAttemptTimes(
  650: 	left *time.Time,
  651: 	right *time.Time,
  652: ) bool {
  653: 	switch {
  654: 	case left == nil && right == nil:
  655: 		return true
  656: 	case left == nil || right == nil:
  657: 		return false
  658: 	default:
  659: 		return left.Equal(*right)
  660: 	}
  661: }
  662: 
  663: func cloneForwardResponse(
  664: 	value ports.ForwardResponse,
  665: ) ports.ForwardResponse {
  666: 	return ports.ForwardResponse{
  667: 		StatusCode: value.StatusCode,
  668: 		Headers:    cloneForwardHeaders(value.Headers),
  669: 		Body:       cloneBytes(value.Body),
  670: 	}
  671: }
  672: 
  673: func cloneForwardHeaders(
  674: 	value map[string][]string,
  675: ) map[string][]string {
  676: 	if value == nil {
  677: 		return nil
  678: 	}
  679: 	result := make(map[string][]string, len(value))
  680: 	for key, values := range value {
  681: 		result[key] = append([]string(nil), values...)
  682: 	}
  683: 	return result
  684: }

   15: type forwardingCapacityManager struct {
   16: 	checkFunc   func(context.Context, ports.RouteCapacityCheckInput) (ports.RouteCapacityResult, error)
   17: 	acquireFunc func(context.Context, ports.RouteCapacityAcquireInput) (ports.RouteCapacityReservation, error)
   18: 	releaseFunc func(context.Context, ports.RouteCapacityReservation) error
   19: }

   22: 	ctx context.Context,

   24: ) (ports.RouteCapacityResult, error) {
   25: 	if manager.checkFunc == nil {

  153: 					prepared.Plan.Route.ID {

  165: 			}, nil

  181: 		t.Fatalf("Execute: %v", err)

  208: func TestForwardingStageStopsWhenCapacityAcquireFails(t *testing.T) {
  209: 	stageError := errors.New("capacity failed")
  210: 	var calls []string
  211: 	capacity := validForwardingCapacityManager(&calls)
  212: 	capacity.acquireFunc = func(
  213: 		context.Context,
  214: 		ports.RouteCapacityAcquireInput,
  215: 	) (ports.RouteCapacityReservation, error) {
  216: 		calls = append(calls, "acquire")
  217: 		return ports.RouteCapacityReservation{}, stageError
  218: 	}
  219: 
  220: 	stage := mustForwardingStage(
  221: 		t,
  222: 		capacity,
  223: 		reserveFunc(
  224: 			func(
  225: 				context.Context,
  226: 				ReservationInput,
  227: 			) (ReservationResult, error) {
  228: 				t.Fatal("reservation must not be called")
  229: 				return ReservationResult{}, nil
  230: 			},
  231: 		),
  232: 		forwardingExecutorFunc(
  233: 			func(
  234: 				context.Context,
  235: 				ForwardingExecutionInput,
  236: 			) (ForwardingExecutionResult, error) {
  237: 				t.Fatal("forwarder must not be called")
  238: 				return ForwardingExecutionResult{}, nil
  239: 			},
  240: 		),
  241: 	)
  242: 
  243: 	prepared := validForwardingPreparedRequest()
  244: 	_, err := stage.Execute(
  245: 		context.Background(),
  246: 		prepared,
  247: 		validForwardingAdmission(prepared),
  248: 	)
  249: 	if !errors.Is(err, stageError) {
  250: 		t.Fatalf("error = %v, want capacity error", err)
  251: 	}
  252: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(calls, []string{"acquire"}) {
  253: 		t.Fatalf("calls = %#v", calls)
  254: 	}
  255: }

  347: func TestForwardingStageReleaseIgnoresCallerCancellation(
  348: 	t *testing.T,
  349: ) {
  350: 	var calls []string
  351: 	ctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
  352: 	capacity := validForwardingCapacityManager(&calls)
  353: 	capacity.releaseFunc = func(
  354: 		releaseCtx context.Context,
  355: 		_ ports.RouteCapacityReservation,
  356: 	) error {
  357: 		calls = append(calls, "release")
  358: 		if releaseCtx.Err() != nil {
  359: 			t.Fatalf(
  360: 				"release context is canceled: %v",
  361: 				releaseCtx.Err(),
  362: 			)
  363: 		}
  364: 		return nil
  365: 	}
  366: 	stage := mustForwardingStage(
  367: 		t,
  368: 		capacity,
  369: 		reserveFunc(
  370: 			func(
  371: 				_ context.Context,
  372: 				input ReservationInput,
  373: 			) (ReservationResult, error) {
  374: 				calls = append(calls, "reservation")
  375: 				return validReservation(input), nil
  376: 			},
  377: 		),
  378: 		forwardingExecutorFunc(
  379: 			func(
  380: 				context.Context,
  381: 				ForwardingExecutionInput,
  382: 			) (ForwardingExecutionResult, error) {
  383: 				calls = append(calls, "forward")
  384: 				cancel()
  385: 				return ForwardingExecutionResult{},
  386: 					context.Canceled
  387: 			},
  388: 		),
  389: 	)
  390: 
  391: 	prepared := validForwardingPreparedRequest()
  392: 	_, err := stage.Execute(
  393: 		ctx,
  394: 		prepared,
  395: 		validForwardingAdmission(prepared),
  396: 	)
  397: 	if !errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {
  398: 		t.Fatalf("error = %v, want context canceled", err)
  399: 	}
  400: 	if calls[len(calls)-1] != "release" {
  401: 		t.Fatalf("calls = %#v", calls)
  402: 	}
  403: }
  404: 
  405: func TestForwardingStageJoinsReleaseFailure(t *testing.T) {
  406: 	forwardError := errors.New("forward failed")
  407: 	releaseError := errors.New("release failed")
  408: 	capacity := validForwardingCapacityManager(nil)
  409: 	capacity.releaseFunc = func(
  410: 		context.Context,
  411: 		ports.RouteCapacityReservation,
  412: 	) error {
  413: 		return releaseError
  414: 	}
  415: 
  416: 	stage := mustForwardingStage(
  417: 		t,
  418: 		capacity,
  419: 		reserveFunc(
  420: 			func(
  421: 				_ context.Context,
  422: 				input ReservationInput,
  423: 			) (ReservationResult, error) {
  424: 				return validReservation(input), nil
  425: 			},
  426: 		),
  427: 		forwardingExecutorFunc(
  428: 			func(
  429: 				context.Context,
  430: 				ForwardingExecutionInput,
  431: 			) (ForwardingExecutionResult, error) {
  432: 				return ForwardingExecutionResult{}, forwardError
  433: 			},
  434: 		),
  435: 	)
  436: 
  437: 	prepared := validForwardingPreparedRequest()
  438: 	_, err := stage.Execute(
  439: 		context.Background(),
  440: 		prepared,
  441: 		validForwardingAdmission(prepared),
  442: 	)
  443: 	if !errors.Is(err, forwardError) ||
  444: 		!errors.Is(err, releaseError) {
  445: 		t.Fatalf("joined error = %v", err)
  446: 	}
  447: }
  448: 
  449: func TestNewForwardingStageRequiresDependencies(t *testing.T) {
  450: 	validCapacity := validForwardingCapacityManager(nil)
  451: 	validAtomicReservation := reserveFunc(
  452: 		func(
  453: 			_ context.Context,
  454: 			input ReservationInput,
  455: 		) (ReservationResult, error) {
  456: 			return validReservation(input), nil
  457: 		},
  458: 	)
  459: 	validTransfer := &routeReservationTransferStub{}
  460: 	validAttemptStore := &forwardingAttemptStoreStub{}
  461: 	validClock := forwardingStageClock{
  462: 		now: validForwardingStageTime(),
  463: 	}
  464: 	validForwarder := forwardingExecutorFunc(
  465: 		func(
  466: 			context.Context,
  467: 			ForwardingExecutionInput,
  468: 		) (ForwardingExecutionResult, error) {
  469: 			return ForwardingExecutionResult{}, nil
  470: 		},
  471: 	)
  472: 
  473: 	tests := []struct {
  474: 		name        string
  475: 		capacity    ports.RouteCapacityManager
  476: 		reservation AtomicReservation
  477: 		transfer    RouteReservationTransfer
  478: 		attempts    ports.ForwardingAttemptStore
  479: 		clock       ports.Clock
  480: 		forwarder   ForwardingExecutor
  481: 	}{
  482: 		{
  483: 			name:        "capacity",
  484: 			reservation: validAtomicReservation,
  485: 			transfer:    validTransfer,
  486: 			attempts:    validAttemptStore,
  487: 			clock:       validClock,
  488: 			forwarder:   validForwarder,
  489: 		},
  490: 		{
  491: 			name:      "reservation",
  492: 			capacity:  validCapacity,
  493: 			transfer:  validTransfer,
  494: 			attempts:  validAttemptStore,
  495: 			clock:     validClock,
  496: 			forwarder: validForwarder,
  497: 		},
  498: 		{
  499: 			name:        "transfer",
  500: 			capacity:    validCapacity,
  501: 			reservation: validAtomicReservation,
  502: 			attempts:    validAttemptStore,
  503: 			clock:       validClock,
  504: 			forwarder:   validForwarder,
  505: 		},
  506: 		{
  507: 			name:        "attempts",
  508: 			capacity:    validCapacity,
  509: 			reservation: validAtomicReservation,
  510: 			transfer:    validTransfer,
  511: 			clock:       validClock,
  512: 			forwarder:   validForwarder,
  513: 		},
  514: 		{
  515: 			name:        "clock",
  516: 			capacity:    validCapacity,
  517: 			reservation: validAtomicReservation,
  518: 			transfer:    validTransfer,
  519: 			attempts:    validAttemptStore,
  520: 			forwarder:   validForwarder,
  521: 		},
  522: 		{
  523: 			name:        "forwarder",
  524: 			capacity:    validCapacity,
  525: 			reservation: validAtomicReservation,
  526: 			transfer:    validTransfer,
  527: 			attempts:    validAttemptStore,
  528: 			clock:       validClock,
  529: 		},
  530: 	}
  531: 
  532: 	for _, test := range tests {
  533: 		t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
  534: 			_, err := NewForwardingStage(
  535: 				test.capacity,
  536: 				test.reservation,
  537: 				test.transfer,
  538: 				test.attempts,
  539: 				test.clock,
  540: 				test.forwarder,
  541: 			)
  542: 			if !errors.Is(err, ErrDependencyRequired) {
  543: 				t.Fatalf(
  544: 					"error = %v, want dependency required",
  545: 					err,
  546: 				)
  547: 			}
  548: 		})
  549: 	}
  550: }
  551: 
  552: func mustForwardingStage(
  553: 	t *testing.T,
  554: 	capacity ports.RouteCapacityManager,
  555: 	reservation AtomicReservation,
  556: 	forwarder ForwardingExecutor,
  557: ) *ForwardingStage {
  558: 	t.Helper()
  559: 
  560: 	stage, err := NewForwardingStage(
  561: 		capacity,
  562: 		reservation,
  563: 		&routeReservationTransferStub{},
  564: 		&forwardingAttemptStoreStub{},
  565: 		forwardingStageClock{
  566: 			now: validForwardingStageTime(),
  567: 		},
  568: 		forwarder,
  569: 	)
  570: 	if err != nil {
  571: 		t.Fatalf("NewForwardingStage: %v", err)
  572: 	}
  573: 	return stage
  574: }
  575: 
  576: func validForwardingStageTime() time.Time {
  577: 	return time.Date(
  578: 		2026,
  579: 		time.June,
  580: 		15,
  581: 		12,
  582: 		0,
  583: 		0,
  584: 		0,
  585: 		time.UTC,
  586: 	)
  587: }
  588: 
  589: func validForwardingCapacityManager(
  590: 	calls *[]string,
  591: ) *forwardingCapacityManager {
  592: 	record := func(value string) {
  593: 		if calls != nil {
  594: 			*calls = append(*calls, value)
  595: 		}
  596: 	}
  597: 	return &forwardingCapacityManager{
  598: 		acquireFunc: func(
  599: 			_ context.Context,
  600: 			input ports.RouteCapacityAcquireInput,
  601: 		) (ports.RouteCapacityReservation, error) {
  602: 			record("acquire")
  603: 			return ports.RouteCapacityReservation{
  604: 				LocalRequestID: input.LocalRequestID,
  605: 				ReservationID:  input.ReservationID,
  606: 				RouteID:        input.Route.ID,
  607: 			}, nil
  608: 		},
  609: 		releaseFunc: func(
  610: 			_ context.Context,
  611: 			_ ports.RouteCapacityReservation,
  612: 		) error {
  613: 			record("release")
  614: 			return nil
  615: 		},
  616: 	}
  617: }
  618: 
  619: func validForwardingPreparedRequest() PreparedRequest {
  620: 	input := validInput()
  621: 	return PreparedRequest{
  622: 		LocalRequestID: input.LocalRequestID,
  623: 		IdempotencyKey: cloneStringPointer(input.IdempotencyKey),
  624: 		Principal: Principal{
  625: 			UserID:               "user-1",
  626: 			APIKeyID:             "key-1",
  627: 			BillingSubjectUserID: "billing-1",
  628: 		},
  629: 		APIFamily:             input.APIFamily,
  630: 		EndpointKind:          input.EndpointKind,
  631: 		ClientModel:           "model-1",
  632: 		RequestedCapabilities: validRoutePlan().Route.Capabilities,
  633: 		Payload:               cloneBytes(input.Payload),
  634: 		Plan:                  validRoutePlan(),
  635: 	}
  636: }
  637: 
  638: func validForwardingAdmission(
  639: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  640: ) BillingAdmissionResult {
  641: 	return validAdmission(
  642: 		BillingAdmissionInput{
  643: 			Principal: prepared.Principal,
  644: 			RequiredReserveCents: prepared.Plan.
  645: 				EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  646: 			Currency: prepared.Plan.Currency,
  647: 		},
  648: 	)
  649: }

   13: func TestServiceExecuteImageGenerationCanonicalPipeline(
   14: 	t *testing.T,
   15: ) {
   16: 	var calls []string
   17: 	record := func(value string) {
   18: 		calls = append(calls, value)
   19: 	}
   20: 
   21: 	payload := []byte(`{
   22: 		"model":"image-model",
   23: 		"prompt":"A red fox in snow",
   24: 		"n":2,
   25: 		"size":"1536x1024",
   26: 		"quality":"high"
   27: 	}`)
   28: 	input := Input{
   29: 		LocalRequestID: "llmreq_images_test",
   30: 		RawAPIKey:      "sk_test",
   31: 		APIFamily:      domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible,
   32: 		EndpointKind:   domain.EndpointImagesGeneration,
   33: 		Payload:        payload,
   34: 	}
   35: 
   36: 	dependencies := validDependencies(nil)
   37: 	dependencies.Authenticator = authenticateFunc(
   38: 		func(
   39: 			_ context.Context,
   40: 			rawAPIKey string,
   41: 		) (Principal, error) {
   42: 			record("authenticate")
   43: 			if rawAPIKey != "sk_test" {
   44: 				t.Fatalf("raw API key=%q", rawAPIKey)
   45: 			}
   46: 			return Principal{
   47: 				UserID:               "user-1",
   48: 				APIKeyID:             "key-1",
   49: 				BillingSubjectUserID: "billing-1",
   50: 			}, nil
   51: 		},
   52: 	)
   53: 	dependencies.RequestParser = parseFunc(
   54: 		func(
   55: 			_ context.Context,
   56: 			value ParseInput,
   57: 		) (ParsedRequest, error) {
   58: 			record("parse")
   59: 			if value.APIFamily != domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible ||
   60: 				value.EndpointKind !=
   61: 					domain.EndpointImagesGeneration ||
   62: 				!bytes.Equal(value.Payload, payload) {
   63: 				t.Fatalf("parse input=%+v", value)
   64: 			}
   65: 			return ParsedRequest{
   66: 				ClientModel: "image-model",
   67: 			}, nil
   68: 		},
   69: 	)
   70: 	dependencies.CapabilityDetector = detectFunc(
   71: 		func(
   72: 			_ context.Context,
   73: 			value CapabilityInput,
   74: 		) (domain.CapabilitySet, error) {
   75: 			record("capabilities")
   76: 			if value.EndpointKind !=
   77: 				domain.EndpointImagesGeneration ||
   78: 				value.ClientModel != "image-model" ||
   79: 				!bytes.Equal(value.Payload, payload) {
   80: 				t.Fatalf("capability input=%+v", value)
   81: 			}
   82: 			return domain.CapabilitySet{
   83: 				ImagesGeneration: true,
   84: 			}, nil
   85: 		},
   86: 	)
   87: 	dependencies.RoutePlanner = planFunc(
   88: 		func(
   89: 			_ context.Context,
   90: 			value RoutePlanInput,
   91: 		) (RoutePlan, error) {
   92: 			record("route")
   93: 			if value.EndpointKind !=
   94: 				domain.EndpointImagesGeneration ||
   95: 				value.ClientModel != "image-model" ||
   96: 				!value.RequestedCapabilities.ImagesGeneration ||
   97: 				value.RequestedCapabilities.Chat ||
   98: 				value.RequestedCapabilities.Embeddings {
   99: 				t.Fatalf("route input=%+v", value)
  100: 			}
  101: 
  102: 			plan := validRoutePlan()
  103: 			plan.Route.EndpointKind =
  104: 				domain.EndpointImagesGeneration
  105: 			plan.Route.ClientModel = "image-model"
  106: 			plan.Route.ProviderModel =
  107: 				"provider-image-model"
  108: 			plan.BillingModel = "openai:image-model"
  109: 			plan.EstimatedUsage = domain.TokenUsage{
  110: 				ImageGenerationUnits: 2,
  111: 			}
  112: 			plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents = 30
  113: 			plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents = 20
  114: 			return plan, nil
  115: 		},
  116: 	)
  117: 	dependencies.BillingAdmitter = admitFunc(
  118: 		func(
  119: 			_ context.Context,
  120: 			value BillingAdmissionInput,
  121: 		) (BillingAdmissionResult, error) {
  122: 			record("admission")
  123: 			if value.Principal.UserID != "user-1" ||
  124: 				value.RequiredReserveCents != 30 ||
  125: 				value.Currency != "RUB" {
  126: 				t.Fatalf("admission input=%+v", value)
  127: 			}
  128: 			return BillingAdmissionResult{
  129: 				Allowed:               true,
  130: 				RemoteBalanceCents:    1000,
  131: 				PendingAmountCents:    100,
  132: 				EffectiveBalanceCents: 900,
  133: 				RequiredReserveCents:  30,
  134: 				Currency:              "RUB",
  135: 			}, nil
  136: 		},
  137: 	)
  138: 	dependencies.Forwarding = forwardingStageFunc(
  139: 		func(
  140: 			_ context.Context,
  141: 			prepared PreparedRequest,
  142: 			admission BillingAdmissionResult,
  143: 		) (ForwardedRequest, error) {
  144: 			record("forwarding")
  145: 			if prepared.EndpointKind !=
  146: 				domain.EndpointImagesGeneration ||
  147: 				!prepared.RequestedCapabilities.ImagesGeneration ||
  148: 				prepared.Plan.Route.EndpointKind !=
  149: 					domain.EndpointImagesGeneration ||
  150: 				admission.RequiredReserveCents != 30 {
  151: 				t.Fatalf(
  152: 					"prepared=%+v admission=%+v",
  153: 					prepared,
  154: 					admission,
  155: 				)
  156: 			}
  157: 
  158: 			reservation := validReservation(
  159: 				reservationInput(prepared),
  160: 			)
  161: 			return ForwardedRequest{
  162: 				Reserved: ReservedRequest{
  163: 					Prepared:    prepared,
  164: 					Admission:   admission,
  165: 					Reservation: reservation,
  166: 				},
  167: 				Response: ports.ForwardResponse{
  168: 					StatusCode: 200,
  169: 					Body: []byte(`{
  170: 						"created":1710000000,
  171: 						"data":[
  172: 							{"url":"https://example.test/1.png"},
  173: 							{"b64_json":"AAAA"}
  174: 						]
  175: 					}`),
  176: 				},
  177: 			}, nil
  178: 		},
  179: 	)
  180: 	dependencies.UsageResolver = usageResolverFunc(
  181: 		func(
  182: 			_ context.Context,
  183: 			value UsageResolutionInput,
  184: 		) (UsageResolutionResult, error) {
  185: 			record("usage")
  186: 			if value.Reserved.Prepared.EndpointKind !=
  187: 				domain.EndpointImagesGeneration ||
  188: 				value.Response.StatusCode != 200 {
  189: 				t.Fatalf("usage input=%+v", value)
  190: 			}
  191: 			return UsageResolutionResult{
  192: 				Usage: domain.TokenUsage{
  193: 					ImageGenerationUnits: 2,
  194: 				},
  195: 				Completeness:      "detailed",
  196: 				UpstreamCostCents: 20,
  197: 				ClientAmountCents: 30,
  198: 				Currency:          "RUB",
  199: 			}, nil
  200: 		},
  201: 	)
  202: 	dependencies.Finalizer = finalizerFunc{
  203: 		commit: func(
  204: 			_ context.Context,
  205: 			value FinalizationInput,
  206: 		) (FinalizationResult, error) {
  207: 			record("finalize")
  208: 			if value.ResolvedUsage.Usage.
  209: 				ImageGenerationUnits != 2 ||
  210: 				value.ResolvedUsage.Usage.InputTokens != 0 ||
  211: 				value.ResolvedUsage.Usage.OutputTokens != 0 ||
  212: 				value.ResolvedUsage.ClientAmountCents != 30 {
  213: 				t.Fatalf("finalization input=%+v", value)
  214: 			}
  215: 			return FinalizationResult{
  216: 				Usage: domain.UsageRecord{
  217: 					LocalRequestID: value.Reserved.
  218: 						Prepared.LocalRequestID,
  219: 					UserID: value.Reserved.Prepared.
  220: 						Principal.UserID,
  221: 					ProviderType: domain.ProviderOpenAI,
  222: 					ClientModel:  "image-model",
  223: 					BillingModel: "openai:image-model",
  224: 					Currency:     "RUB",
  225: 					Usage: domain.TokenUsage{
  226: 						ImageGenerationUnits: 2,
  227: 					},
  228: 					UsageCompleteness:    "detailed",
  229: 					ClientAmountCents:    30,
  230: 					RemainingAmountCents: 30,
  231: 					Status: domain.
  232: 						UsageStatusBillable,
  233: 				},
  234: 			}, nil
  235: 		},
  236: 		pricingFailed: func(
  237: 			context.Context,
  238: 			PricingFailureInput,
  239: 		) (FinalizationResult, error) {
  240: 			t.Fatal("pricing-failure finalizer called")
  241: 			return FinalizationResult{}, nil
  242: 		},
  243: 	}
  244: 	dependencies.AutoCharger = autoChargerFunc(
  245: 		func(
  246: 			_ context.Context,
  247: 			value AutoChargeInput,
  248: 		) AutoChargeResult {
  249: 			record("autocharge")
  250: 			if value.Principal.BillingSubjectUserID != "billing-1" ||
  251: 				value.FinalUsageRecord.Status !=
  252: 					domain.UsageStatusBillable ||
  253: 				value.FinalUsageRecord.
  254: 					ClientAmountCents != 30 ||
  255: 				value.FinalUsageRecord.Usage.
  256: 					ImageGenerationUnits != 2 {
  257: 				t.Fatalf("auto-charge input=%+v", value)
  258: 			}
  259: 			balance := int64(970)
  260: 			return AutoChargeResult{
  261: 				Status: AutoChargeStatusProcessed,
  262: 				ProcessedBatchIDs: []string{
  263: 					"billchg_images",
  264: 				},
  265: 				ChargedAmountCents:  30,
  266: 				BillingBalanceCents: &balance,
  267: 			}
  268: 		},
  269: 	)
  270: 
  271: 	service, err := NewService(dependencies)
  272: 	if err != nil {
  273: 		t.Fatalf("NewService: %v", err)
  274: 	}
  275: 	result, err := service.Execute(
  276: 		context.Background(),
  277: 		input,
  278: 	)
  279: 	if err != nil {
  280: 		t.Fatalf("Execute: %v", err)
  281: 	}
  282: 
  283: 	wantCalls := []string{
  284: 		"authenticate",
  285: 		"parse",
  286: 		"capabilities",
  287: 		"route",
  288: 		"admission",
  289: 		"forwarding",
  290: 		"usage",
  291: 		"finalize",
  292: 		"autocharge",
  293: 	}
  294: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(calls, wantCalls) {
  295: 		t.Fatalf("calls=%#v want=%#v", calls, wantCalls)
  296: 	}
  297: 
  298: 	if result.Reserved.Prepared.EndpointKind !=
  299: 		domain.EndpointImagesGeneration ||
  300: 		!result.Reserved.Prepared.
  301: 			RequestedCapabilities.ImagesGeneration ||
  302: 		result.ResolvedUsage.Usage.
  303: 			ImageGenerationUnits != 2 ||
  304: 		result.ResolvedUsage.Usage.InputTokens != 0 ||
  305: 		result.ResolvedUsage.Usage.OutputTokens != 0 ||
  306: 		result.FinalUsageRecord.Status !=
  307: 			domain.UsageStatusBillable ||
  308: 		result.FinalUsageRecord.ClientAmountCents != 30 ||
  309: 		result.AutoCharge.Status !=
  310: 			AutoChargeStatusProcessed ||
  311: 		result.AutoCharge.ChargedAmountCents != 30 ||
  312: 		result.AutoCharge.BillingBalanceCents == nil ||
  313: 		*result.AutoCharge.BillingBalanceCents != 970 ||
  314: 		len(result.Response.Body) == 0 {
  315: 		t.Fatalf("result=%+v", result)
  316: 	}
  317: }

   13: type RouteCandidatePreflightInput struct {
   14: 	Route    domain.Route
   15: 	Reseller domain.Reseller
   16: 	Price    *domain.RoutePrice
   17: 
   18: 	RequestedCapabilities domain.CapabilitySet
   19: 	Payload               []byte
   20: }

   22: type RouteCandidatePreflightResult struct {
   23: 	SecretAvailable bool
   24: 	CostAvailable   bool
   25: 
   26: 	EstimatedUsage domain.TokenUsage

   28: 	EstimatedClientAmountCents int64
   29: 	EstimatedUpstreamCostCents int64

   33: 
   34: 	ForwardingAdapterAvailable    bool

   59: 	RequestedCapabilities domain.CapabilitySet

   75: type RepositoryRoutePlanner struct {
   76: 	routes      ports.RouteRepository
   77: 	resellers   ports.ResellerQueryRepository
   78: 	prices      ports.RoutePriceRepository
   79: 	preflighter RouteCandidatePreflighter
   80: 	selector    RouteCandidateSelector
   81: }
   82: 
   83: var _ RoutePlanner = (*RepositoryRoutePlanner)(nil)
   84: 
   85: func NewRepositoryRoutePlanner(
   86: 	routes ports.RouteRepository,
   87: 	resellers ports.ResellerQueryRepository,
   88: 	prices ports.RoutePriceRepository,
   89: 	preflighter RouteCandidatePreflighter,
   90: 	selector RouteCandidateSelector,
   91: ) (*RepositoryRoutePlanner, error) {
   92: 	if routes == nil ||
   93: 		resellers == nil ||
   94: 		prices == nil ||
   95: 		preflighter == nil ||
   96: 		selector == nil {
   97: 		return nil, ErrDependencyRequired
   98: 	}
   99: 	return &RepositoryRoutePlanner{
  100: 		routes:      routes,
  101: 		resellers:   resellers,
  102: 		prices:      prices,
  103: 		preflighter: preflighter,
  104: 		selector:    selector,
  105: 	}, nil
  106: }
  107: 
  108: func (p *RepositoryRoutePlanner) Plan(
  109: 	ctx context.Context,
  110: 	input RoutePlanInput,
  111: ) (RoutePlan, error) {
  112: 	if p == nil ||
  113: 		p.routes == nil ||
  114: 		p.resellers == nil ||
  115: 		p.prices == nil ||
  116: 		p.preflighter == nil ||
  117: 		p.selector == nil {
  118: 		return RoutePlan{}, ErrDependencyRequired
  119: 	}
  120: 	if ctx == nil {
  121: 		return RoutePlan{}, fmt.Errorf(
  122: 			"%w: nil route planner context",
  123: 			ErrInvalidInput,
  124: 		)
  125: 	}
  126: 	if err := validateRoutePlanInput(input); err != nil {
  127: 		return RoutePlan{}, err
  128: 	}
  129: 
  130: 	routes, err := p.routes.FindRoutes(
  131: 		ctx,
  132: 		ports.RouteQuery{
  133: 			APIFamily:    input.APIFamily,
  134: 			EndpointKind: input.EndpointKind,
  135: 			ClientModel:  input.ClientModel,
  136: 		},
  137: 	)
  138: 	if err != nil {
  139: 		return RoutePlan{}, fmt.Errorf(
  140: 			"find route candidates: %w",
  141: 			err,
  142: 		)
  143: 	}
  144: 	if len(routes) == 0 {
  145: 		return RoutePlan{}, ErrUnknownModel
  146: 	}
  147: 
  148: 	canonicalRoutes, resellerIDs, routeIDs, err :=
  149: 		canonicalRouteCandidates(input, routes)
  150: 	if err != nil {
  151: 		return RoutePlan{}, err
  152: 	}
  153: 
  154: 	resellers, err := p.resellers.FindByIDs(ctx, resellerIDs)
  155: 	if err != nil {
  156: 		return RoutePlan{}, fmt.Errorf(
  157: 			"find candidate resellers: %w",
  158: 			err,
  159: 		)
  160: 	}
  161: 	prices, err := p.prices.FindByRouteIDs(ctx, routeIDs)
  162: 	if err != nil {
  163: 		return RoutePlan{}, fmt.Errorf(
  164: 			"find candidate route prices: %w",
  165: 			err,
  166: 		)
  167: 	}
  168: 
  169: 	candidates := make(
  170: 		[]RouteSelectionCandidate,
  171: 		0,
  172: 		len(canonicalRoutes),
  173: 	)
  174: 	for _, route := range canonicalRoutes {
  175: 		reseller, exists := resellers[route.ResellerID]
  176: 		if !exists {
  177: 			return RoutePlan{}, fmt.Errorf(
  178: 				"%w: reseller %q missing for route %q",
  179: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  180: 				route.ResellerID,
  181: 				route.ID,
  182: 			)
  183: 		}
  184: 		if reseller.ID != route.ResellerID ||
  185: 			reseller.ProviderType != route.ProviderType {
  186: 			return RoutePlan{}, fmt.Errorf(
  187: 				"%w: reseller identity mismatch for route %q",
  188: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  189: 				route.ID,
  190: 			)
  191: 		}
  192: 
  193: 		var price *domain.RoutePrice
  194: 		if value, exists := prices[route.ID]; exists {
  195: 			priceCopy := value
  196: 			price = &priceCopy
  197: 		}
  198: 
  199: 		preflight, err := p.preflighter.Evaluate(
  200: 			ctx,
  201: 			RouteCandidatePreflightInput{
  202: 				Route:                 route,
  203: 				Reseller:              reseller,
  204: 				Price:                 cloneRoutePricePointer(price),
  205: 				RequestedCapabilities: input.RequestedCapabilities,
  206: 				Payload:               cloneBytes(input.Payload),
  207: 			},
  208: 		)
  209: 		if err != nil {
  210: 			return RoutePlan{}, fmt.Errorf(
  211: 				"evaluate route %q preflight: %w",
  212: 				route.ID,
  213: 				err,
  214: 			)
  215: 		}
  216: 
  217: 		candidates = append(
  218: 			candidates,
  219: 			RouteSelectionCandidate{
  220: 				Route:     route,
  221: 				Reseller:  reseller,
  222: 				Price:     cloneRoutePricePointer(price),
  223: 				Preflight: preflight,
  224: 			},
  225: 		)
  226: 	}
  227: 
  228: 	selection, err := p.selector.Select(
  229: 		ctx,
  230: 		RouteSelectionInput{
  231: 			APIFamily:             input.APIFamily,
  232: 			EndpointKind:          input.EndpointKind,
  233: 			ClientModel:           input.ClientModel,
  234: 			RequestedCapabilities: input.RequestedCapabilities,
  235: 			Candidates:            cloneRouteSelectionCandidates(candidates),
  236: 		},
  237: 	)
  238: 	if err != nil {
  239: 		return RoutePlan{}, fmt.Errorf(
  240: 			"select route candidate: %w",
  241: 			err,
  242: 		)
  243: 	}
  244: 
  245: 	selected, err := selectedRouteCandidate(
  246: 		candidates,
  247: 		selection.SelectedRouteID,
  248: 	)
  249: 	if err != nil {
  250: 		return RoutePlan{}, err
  251: 	}
  252: 	if err := validateSelectedRouteCandidate(selected); err != nil {
  253: 		return RoutePlan{}, err
  254: 	}
  255: 	fallbackCandidates, err := selectedRouteFallbacks(
  256: 		candidates,
  257: 		selection.SelectedRouteID,
  258: 		selection.FallbackRouteIDs,
  259: 	)
  260: 	if err != nil {
  261: 		return RoutePlan{}, err
  262: 	}
  263: 	fallbacks := make(
  264: 		[]RouteFallbackPlan,
  265: 		len(fallbackCandidates),
  266: 	)
  267: 	for index, candidate := range fallbackCandidates {
  268: 		if err := validateSelectedRouteCandidate(candidate); err != nil {
  269: 			return RoutePlan{}, err
  270: 		}
  271: 		fallbacks[index] = routeFallbackPlan(candidate)
  272: 	}
  273: 
  274: 	return RoutePlan{
  275: 		Route:          selected.Route,
  276: 		Reseller:       selected.Reseller,
  277: 		Price:          *selected.Price,
  278: 		BillingModel:   billingModel(selected.Route),
  279: 		EstimatedUsage: selected.Preflight.EstimatedUsage,
  280: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: selected.Preflight.
  281: 			EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  282: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: selected.Preflight.
  283: 			EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
  284: 		Currency:   selected.Preflight.Currency,
  285: 		Confidence: selected.Preflight.Confidence,
  286: 		Fallbacks:  fallbacks,
  287: 	}, nil
  288: }
  289: 
  290: func validateRoutePlanInput(input RoutePlanInput) error {
  291: 	if strings.TrimSpace(input.Principal.UserID) == "" ||
  292: 		strings.TrimSpace(input.Principal.APIKeyID) == "" ||
  293: 		strings.TrimSpace(
  294: 			input.Principal.BillingSubjectUserID,
  295: 		) == "" ||
  296: 		input.APIFamily == "" ||
  297: 		input.EndpointKind == "" ||
  298: 		strings.TrimSpace(input.ClientModel) == "" ||
  299: 		input.Payload == nil {
  300: 		return ErrInvalidInput
  301: 	}
  302: 	return nil
  303: }
  304: 
  305: func canonicalRouteCandidates(
  306: 	input RoutePlanInput,
  307: 	routes []domain.Route,
  308: ) ([]domain.Route, []string, []string, error) {
  309: 	canonical := append([]domain.Route(nil), routes...)
  310: 	sort.Slice(canonical, func(left, right int) bool {
  311: 		return canonical[left].ID < canonical[right].ID
  312: 	})
  313: 
  314: 	resellerSet := make(map[string]struct{}, len(canonical))
  315: 	routeSet := make(map[string]struct{}, len(canonical))
  316: 	resellerIDs := make([]string, 0, len(canonical))
  317: 	routeIDs := make([]string, 0, len(canonical))
  318: 
  319: 	for _, route := range canonical {
  320: 		if strings.TrimSpace(route.ID) == "" ||
  321: 			strings.TrimSpace(route.ResellerID) == "" ||
  322: 			route.APIFamily != input.APIFamily ||
  323: 			route.EndpointKind != input.EndpointKind ||
  324: 			route.ClientModel != input.ClientModel {
  325: 			return nil, nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(
  326: 				"%w: invalid route repository result",
  327: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  328: 			)
  329: 		}
  330: 		if _, exists := routeSet[route.ID]; exists {
  331: 			return nil, nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(
  332: 				"%w: duplicate route id %q",
  333: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  334: 				route.ID,
  335: 			)
  336: 		}
  337: 		routeSet[route.ID] = struct{}{}
  338: 		routeIDs = append(routeIDs, route.ID)
  339: 
  340: 		if _, exists := resellerSet[route.ResellerID]; !exists {
  341: 			resellerSet[route.ResellerID] = struct{}{}
  342: 			resellerIDs = append(resellerIDs, route.ResellerID)
  343: 		}
  344: 	}
  345: 	sort.Strings(resellerIDs)
  346: 	return canonical, resellerIDs, routeIDs, nil
  347: }
  348: 
  349: func selectedRouteCandidate(
  350: 	candidates []RouteSelectionCandidate,
  351: 	selectedRouteID string,
  352: ) (RouteSelectionCandidate, error) {
  353: 	if strings.TrimSpace(selectedRouteID) == "" {
  354: 		return RouteSelectionCandidate{}, fmt.Errorf(
  355: 			"%w: selector returned blank route id",
  356: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  357: 		)
  358: 	}
  359: 
  360: 	var selected *RouteSelectionCandidate
  361: 	for index := range candidates {
  362: 		if candidates[index].Route.ID != selectedRouteID {
  363: 			continue
  364: 		}
  365: 		if selected != nil {
  366: 			return RouteSelectionCandidate{}, fmt.Errorf(
  367: 				"%w: selected route id %q is ambiguous",
  368: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  369: 				selectedRouteID,
  370: 			)
  371: 		}
  372: 		value := candidates[index]
  373: 		selected = &value
  374: 	}
  375: 	if selected == nil {
  376: 		return RouteSelectionCandidate{}, fmt.Errorf(
  377: 			"%w: selector returned unknown route id %q",
  378: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  379: 			selectedRouteID,
  380: 		)
  381: 	}
  382: 	return *selected, nil
  383: }
  384: 
  385: func selectedRouteFallbacks(
  386: 	candidates []RouteSelectionCandidate,
  387: 	selectedRouteID string,
  388: 	fallbackRouteIDs []string,
  389: ) ([]RouteSelectionCandidate, error) {
  390: 	result := make(
  391: 		[]RouteSelectionCandidate,
  392: 		0,
  393: 		len(fallbackRouteIDs),
  394: 	)
  395: 	seen := map[string]struct{}{selectedRouteID: {}}
  396: 	byID := make(
  397: 		map[string]RouteSelectionCandidate,
  398: 		len(candidates),
  399: 	)
  400: 	for _, candidate := range candidates {
  401: 		byID[candidate.Route.ID] = candidate
  402: 	}
  403: 	for _, routeID := range fallbackRouteIDs {
  404: 		if strings.TrimSpace(routeID) == "" {
  405: 			return nil, fmt.Errorf(
  406: 				"%w: selector returned blank fallback route id",
  407: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  408: 			)
  409: 		}
  410: 		if _, exists := seen[routeID]; exists {
  411: 			return nil, fmt.Errorf(
  412: 				"%w: selector returned duplicate fallback route id %q",
  413: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  414: 				routeID,
  415: 			)
  416: 		}
  417: 		candidate, exists := byID[routeID]
  418: 		if !exists {
  419: 			return nil, fmt.Errorf(
  420: 				"%w: selector returned unknown fallback route id %q",
  421: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  422: 				routeID,
  423: 			)
  424: 		}
  425: 		seen[routeID] = struct{}{}
  426: 		result = append(result, candidate)
  427: 	}
  428: 	return result, nil
  429: }
  430: 
  431: func routeFallbackPlan(
  432: 	candidate RouteSelectionCandidate,
  433: ) RouteFallbackPlan {
  434: 	return RouteFallbackPlan{
  435: 		Route:          candidate.Route,
  436: 		Reseller:       candidate.Reseller,
  437: 		Price:          *candidate.Price,
  438: 		BillingModel:   billingModel(candidate.Route),
  439: 		EstimatedUsage: candidate.Preflight.EstimatedUsage,
  440: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: candidate.Preflight.
  441: 			EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  442: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: candidate.Preflight.
  443: 			EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
  444: 		Currency:   candidate.Preflight.Currency,
  445: 		Confidence: candidate.Preflight.Confidence,
  446: 	}
  447: }
  448: 
  449: func validateSelectedRouteCandidate(
  450: 	selected RouteSelectionCandidate,
  451: ) error {
  452: 	preflight := selected.Preflight
  453: 	if selected.Price == nil ||
  454: 		selected.Price.RouteID != selected.Route.ID ||
  455: 		!preflight.SecretAvailable ||
  456: 		!preflight.CostAvailable ||
  457: 		!preflight.ForwardingAdapterAvailable ||
  458: 		!preflight.RateLimitAllowed ||
  459: 		!preflight.ConcurrencyAllowed ||
  460: 		!preflight.ModelIdentifierRewriteAllowed ||
  461: 		preflight.EstimatedClientAmountCents < 0 ||
  462: 		preflight.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents < 0 ||
  463: 		preflight.Currency != "RUB" ||
  464: 		strings.TrimSpace(preflight.Confidence) == "" ||
  465: 		!nonNegativeUsage(preflight.EstimatedUsage) {
  466: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  467: 			"%w: selector returned ineligible route %q",
  468: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  469: 			selected.Route.ID,
  470: 		)
  471: 	}
  472: 	return nil
  473: }
  474: 
  475: func billingModel(route domain.Route) string {
  476: 	return string(route.ProviderType) + ":" + route.ProviderModel
  477: }
  478: 
  479: func cloneRoutePricePointer(
  480: 	value *domain.RoutePrice,
  481: ) *domain.RoutePrice {
  482: 	if value == nil {
  483: 		return nil
  484: 	}
  485: 	copyValue := *value
  486: 	return &copyValue
  487: }
  488: 
  489: func cloneRouteSelectionCandidates(
  490: 	values []RouteSelectionCandidate,
  491: ) []RouteSelectionCandidate {
  492: 	result := make([]RouteSelectionCandidate, len(values))
  493: 	for index, value := range values {
  494: 		result[index] = value
  495: 		result[index].Price = cloneRoutePricePointer(value.Price)
  496: 	}
  497: 	return result
  498: }

   74: func TestRepositoryRoutePlannerBuildsDeterministicCandidateSet(
   75: 	t *testing.T,
   76: ) {
   77: 	input := validRoutePlanInput()
   78: 	routes := []domain.Route{
   79: 		validPlannerRoute("route-b", "reseller-b"),
   80: 		validPlannerRoute("route-a", "reseller-a"),
   81: 	}
   82: 	resellers := map[string]domain.Reseller{
   83: 		"reseller-a": validPlannerReseller("reseller-a"),
   84: 		"reseller-b": validPlannerReseller("reseller-b"),
   85: 	}
   86: 	prices := map[string]domain.RoutePrice{
   87: 		"route-a": validPlannerPrice("route-a"),
   88: 		"route-b": validPlannerPrice("route-b"),
   89: 	}
   90: 
   91: 	var gotResellerIDs []string
   92: 	var gotRouteIDs []string
   93: 	var preflightOrder []string
   94: 	var selectorInput RouteSelectionInput
   95: 
   96: 	planner := mustRepositoryRoutePlanner(
   97: 		t,
   98: 		routeRepositoryFunc(
   99: 			func(
  100: 				_ context.Context,
  101: 				query ports.RouteQuery,
  102: 			) ([]domain.Route, error) {
  103: 				if query.APIFamily != input.APIFamily ||
  104: 					query.EndpointKind != input.EndpointKind ||
  105: 					query.ClientModel != input.ClientModel {
  106: 					t.Fatalf("query = %+v", query)
  107: 				}
  108: 				return routes, nil
  109: 			},
  110: 		),
  111: 		resellerRepositoryFunc(
  112: 			func(
  113: 				_ context.Context,
  114: 				ids []string,
  115: 			) (map[string]domain.Reseller, error) {
  116: 				gotResellerIDs = append([]string(nil), ids...)
  117: 				return resellers, nil
  118: 			},
  119: 		),
  120: 		routePriceRepositoryFunc(
  121: 			func(
  122: 				_ context.Context,
  123: 				ids []string,
  124: 			) (map[string]domain.RoutePrice, error) {
  125: 				gotRouteIDs = append([]string(nil), ids...)
  126: 				return prices, nil
  127: 			},
  128: 		),
  129: 		routeCandidatePreflightFunc(
  130: 			func(
  131: 				_ context.Context,
  132: 				value RouteCandidatePreflightInput,
  133: 			) (RouteCandidatePreflightResult, error) {
  134: 				preflightOrder = append(
  135: 					preflightOrder,
  136: 					value.Route.ID,
  137: 				)
  138: 				if !bytes.Equal(value.Payload, input.Payload) {
  139: 					t.Fatalf(
  140: 						"preflight payload = %q, want %q",
  141: 						value.Payload,
  142: 						input.Payload,
  143: 					)
  144: 				}
  145: 				value.Payload[0] = 'X'
  146: 				return validPlannerPreflight(value.Route.ID), nil
  147: 			},
  148: 		),
  149: 		routeCandidateSelectorFunc(
  150: 			func(
  151: 				_ context.Context,
  152: 				value RouteSelectionInput,
  153: 			) (RouteSelectionResult, error) {
  154: 				selectorInput = value
  155: 				return RouteSelectionResult{
  156: 					SelectedRouteID:  "route-b",
  157: 					FallbackRouteIDs: []string{"route-a"},
  158: 				}, nil
  159: 			},
  160: 		),
  161: 	)
  162: 
  163: 	plan, err := planner.Plan(context.Background(), input)
  164: 	if err != nil {
  165: 		t.Fatalf("Plan: %v", err)
  166: 	}
  167: 
  168: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(
  169: 		gotResellerIDs,
  170: 		[]string{"reseller-a", "reseller-b"},
  171: 	) {
  172: 		t.Fatalf("reseller ids = %#v", gotResellerIDs)
  173: 	}
  174: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(
  175: 		gotRouteIDs,
  176: 		[]string{"route-a", "route-b"},
  177: 	) {
  178: 		t.Fatalf("route ids = %#v", gotRouteIDs)
  179: 	}
  180: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(
  181: 		preflightOrder,
  182: 		[]string{"route-a", "route-b"},
  183: 	) {
  184: 		t.Fatalf("preflight order = %#v", preflightOrder)
  185: 	}
  186: 	if len(selectorInput.Candidates) != 2 ||
  187: 		selectorInput.Candidates[0].Route.ID != "route-a" ||
  188: 		selectorInput.Candidates[1].Route.ID != "route-b" {
  189: 		t.Fatalf("selector input = %+v", selectorInput)
  190: 	}
  191: 	if !bytes.Equal(input.Payload, []byte(`{"model":"model-1"}`)) {
  192: 		t.Fatalf("caller payload mutated: %q", input.Payload)
  193: 	}
  194: 	if plan.Route.ID != "route-b" ||
  195: 		plan.Reseller.ID != "reseller-b" ||
  196: 		plan.Price.RouteID != "route-b" ||
  197: 		plan.BillingModel != "openai:provider-route-b" ||
  198: 		plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents != 20 {
  199: 		t.Fatalf("plan = %+v", plan)
  200: 	}
  201: 	if len(plan.Fallbacks) != 1 ||
  202: 		plan.Fallbacks[0].Route.ID != "route-a" ||
  203: 		plan.Fallbacks[0].Reseller.ID != "reseller-a" ||
  204: 		plan.Fallbacks[0].Price.RouteID != "route-a" ||
  205: 		plan.Fallbacks[0].BillingModel !=
  206: 			"openai:provider-route-a" ||
  207: 		plan.Fallbacks[0].EstimatedUpstreamCostCents != 10 {
  208: 		t.Fatalf("fallbacks = %+v", plan.Fallbacks)
  209: 	}
  210: }

  466: func TestRepositoryRoutePlannerStopsAtDependencyError(t *testing.T) {
  467: 	dependencyError := errors.New("dependency failed")
  468: 	input := validRoutePlanInput()
  469: 	route := validPlannerRoute("route-a", "reseller-a")
  470: 
  471: 	tests := []struct {
  472: 		name    string
  473: 		planner *RepositoryRoutePlanner
  474: 	}{
  475: 		{
  476: 			name: "routes",
  477: 			planner: mustRepositoryRoutePlanner(
  478: 				t,
  479: 				routeRepositoryFunc(
  480: 					func(
  481: 						context.Context,
  482: 						ports.RouteQuery,
  483: 					) ([]domain.Route, error) {
  484: 						return nil, dependencyError
  485: 					},
  486: 				),
  487: 				unusedResellerRepository(t),
  488: 				unusedRoutePriceRepository(t),
  489: 				unusedRouteCandidatePreflighter(t),
  490: 				unusedRouteCandidateSelector(t),
  491: 			),
  492: 		},
  493: 		{
  494: 			name: "resellers",
  495: 			planner: mustRepositoryRoutePlanner(
  496: 				t,
  497: 				routeRepositoryFunc(
  498: 					func(
  499: 						context.Context,
  500: 						ports.RouteQuery,
  501: 					) ([]domain.Route, error) {
  502: 						return []domain.Route{route}, nil
  503: 					},
  504: 				),
  505: 				resellerRepositoryFunc(
  506: 					func(
  507: 						context.Context,
  508: 						[]string,
  509: 					) (map[string]domain.Reseller, error) {
  510: 						return nil, dependencyError
  511: 					},
  512: 				),
  513: 				unusedRoutePriceRepository(t),
  514: 				unusedRouteCandidatePreflighter(t),
  515: 				unusedRouteCandidateSelector(t),
  516: 			),
  517: 		},
  518: 	}
  519: 
  520: 	for _, test := range tests {
  521: 		t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
  522: 			_, err := test.planner.Plan(
  523: 				context.Background(),
  524: 				input,
  525: 			)
  526: 			if !errors.Is(err, dependencyError) {
  527: 				t.Fatalf(
  528: 					"error = %v, want dependency error",
  529: 					err,
  530: 				)
  531: 			}
  532: 		})
  533: 	}
  534: }

  588: func mustRepositoryRoutePlanner(
  589: 	t *testing.T,
  590: 	routes ports.RouteRepository,
  591: 	resellers ports.ResellerQueryRepository,
  592: 	prices ports.RoutePriceRepository,
  593: 	preflighter RouteCandidatePreflighter,
  594: 	selector RouteCandidateSelector,
  595: ) *RepositoryRoutePlanner {
  596: 	t.Helper()
  597: 
  598: 	planner, err := NewRepositoryRoutePlanner(
  599: 		routes,
  600: 		resellers,
  601: 		prices,
  602: 		preflighter,
  603: 		selector,
  604: 	)
  605: 	if err != nil {
  606: 		t.Fatalf("NewRepositoryRoutePlanner: %v", err)
  607: 	}
  608: 	return planner
  609: }
  610: 
  611: func validRoutePlanInput() RoutePlanInput {
  612: 	return RoutePlanInput{
  613: 		Principal: Principal{
  614: 			UserID:               "user-1",
  615: 			APIKeyID:             "key-1",
  616: 			BillingSubjectUserID: "billing-1",
  617: 		},
  618: 		APIFamily:    domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible,

    8: 
    9: func TestRouteReservationTransferInputCarriesExactSnapshots(
   10: 	t *testing.T,
   11: ) {
   12: 	expected := domain.UsageRecord{
   13: 		LocalRequestID:             "llmreq-1",
   14: 		SelectedRouteID:            "route-primary",
   15: 		SelectedResellerID:         "reseller-primary",
   16: 		ProviderType:               domain.ProviderOpenAI,
   17: 		ProviderModel:              "provider-primary",
   18: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: 17,
   19: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: 23,
   20: 		Currency:                   "RUB",
   21: 		Status:                     domain.UsageStatusReserved,
   22: 	}
   23: 	target := RouteFallbackPlan{
   24: 		Route: domain.Route{
   25: 			ID:            "route-fallback",
   26: 			ResellerID:    "reseller-fallback",
   27: 			ProviderType:  domain.ProviderOpenRouter,
   28: 			ProviderModel: "provider-fallback",
   29: 		},
   30: 		Reseller: domain.Reseller{
   31: 			ID:           "reseller-fallback",
   32: 			ProviderType: domain.ProviderOpenRouter,
   33: 		},
   34: 		BillingModel:               "billing-model",
   35: 		EstimatedUsage:             domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 7},
   36: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: 29,
   37: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: 19,
   38: 		Currency:                   "RUB",
   39: 		Confidence:                 "exact",
   40: 	}
   41: 
   42: 	input := RouteReservationTransferInput{
   43: 		ExpectedUsage: expected,
   44: 		Target:        target,
   45: 	}
   46: 
   47: 	if input.ExpectedUsage.LocalRequestID != "llmreq-1" ||
   48: 		input.ExpectedUsage.SelectedRouteID != "route-primary" ||
   49: 		input.ExpectedUsage.SelectedResellerID != "reseller-primary" ||
   50: 		input.Target.Route.ID != "route-fallback" ||
   51: 		input.Target.Reseller.ID != "reseller-fallback" ||
   52: 		input.Target.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents != 19 {
   53: 		t.Fatalf("transfer input = %+v", input)
   54: 	}
   55: }
