FILE: internal/application/llmrequest/service.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: 25b3c737ee4484ea28b0d52be2af46ce0bb0003a
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package llmrequest
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"errors"
    6: 	"fmt"
    7: 	"strings"
    8: 	"time"
    9: 	"unicode"
   10: 
   11: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
   12: )
   13: 
   14: const localRequestIDPrefix = "llmreq_"
   15: 
   16: type Service struct {
   17: 	authenticator      Authenticator
   18: 	requestParser      RequestParser
   19: 	capabilityDetector CapabilityDetector
   20: 	routePlanner       RoutePlanner
   21: 	billingAdmitter    BillingAdmitter
   22: 	forwarding         ForwardingStageExecutor
   23: 	usageResolver      UsageResolver
   24: 	finalizer          Finalizer
   25: 	autoCharger        AutoCharger
   26: }
   27: 
   28: func NewService(dependencies Dependencies) (*Service, error) {
   29: 	if dependencies.Authenticator == nil ||
   30: 		dependencies.RequestParser == nil ||
   31: 		dependencies.CapabilityDetector == nil ||
   32: 		dependencies.RoutePlanner == nil ||
   33: 		dependencies.BillingAdmitter == nil ||
   34: 		dependencies.Forwarding == nil ||
   35: 		dependencies.UsageResolver == nil ||
   36: 		dependencies.Finalizer == nil ||
   37: 		dependencies.AutoCharger == nil {
   38: 		return nil, ErrDependencyRequired
   39: 	}
   40: 
   41: 	return &Service{
   42: 		authenticator:      dependencies.Authenticator,
   43: 		requestParser:      dependencies.RequestParser,
   44: 		capabilityDetector: dependencies.CapabilityDetector,
   45: 		routePlanner:       dependencies.RoutePlanner,
   46: 		billingAdmitter:    dependencies.BillingAdmitter,
   47: 		forwarding:         dependencies.Forwarding,
   48: 		usageResolver:      dependencies.UsageResolver,
   49: 		finalizer:          dependencies.Finalizer,
   50: 		autoCharger:        dependencies.AutoCharger,
   51: 	}, nil
   52: }
   53: 
   54: func (s *Service) Execute(
   55: 	ctx context.Context,
   56: 	input Input,
   57: ) (ForwardedRequest, error) {
   58: 	if s == nil ||
   59: 		s.authenticator == nil ||
   60: 		s.requestParser == nil ||
   61: 		s.capabilityDetector == nil ||
   62: 		s.routePlanner == nil ||
   63: 		s.billingAdmitter == nil ||
   64: 		s.forwarding == nil ||
   65: 		s.usageResolver == nil ||
   66: 		s.finalizer == nil ||
   67: 		s.autoCharger == nil {
   68: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, ErrDependencyRequired
   69: 	}
   70: 	if ctx == nil {
   71: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
   72: 			"%w: nil context",
   73: 			ErrInvalidInput,
   74: 		)
   75: 	}
   76: 
   77: 	prepared, err := s.prepare(ctx, input)
   78: 	if err != nil {
   79: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, err
   80: 	}
   81: 
   82: 	admission, err := s.billingAdmitter.Admit(
   83: 		ctx,
   84: 		BillingAdmissionInput{
   85: 			Principal:            prepared.Principal,
   86: 			RequiredReserveCents: prepared.Plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents,
   87: 			Currency:             prepared.Plan.Currency,
   88: 		},
   89: 	)
   90: 	if err != nil {
   91: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
   92: 			"admit billing reserve: %w",
   93: 			err,
   94: 		)
   95: 	}
   96: 	if err := validateBillingAdmission(prepared, admission); err != nil {
   97: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, err
   98: 	}
   99: 
  100: 	forwarded, err := s.forwarding.Execute(
  101: 		ctx,
  102: 		clonePreparedRequest(prepared),
  103: 		admission,
  104: 	)
  105: 	if err != nil {
  106: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  107: 			"execute forwarding stage: %w",
  108: 			err,
  109: 		)
  110: 	}
  111: 
  112: 	resolved, err := s.usageResolver.Resolve(
  113: 		ctx,
  114: 		UsageResolutionInput{
  115: 			Reserved: forwarded.Reserved,
  116: 			Response: cloneForwardResponse(
  117: 				forwarded.Response,
  118: 			),
  119: 		},
  120: 	)
  121: 	if err != nil {
  122: 		failureErr := s.markPricingFailed(
  123: 			ctx,
  124: 			forwarded.Reserved,
  125: 			"usage_resolution_failed",
  126: 		)
  127: 		if failureErr != nil {
  128: 			return ForwardedRequest{}, errors.Join(
  129: 				fmt.Errorf("resolve final usage: %w", err),
  130: 				failureErr,
  131: 			)
  132: 		}
  133: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  134: 			"resolve final usage: %w",
  135: 			err,
  136: 		)
  137: 	}
  138: 	if err := validateUsageResolution(
  139: 		forwarded,
  140: 		resolved,
  141: 	); err != nil {
  142: 		failureErr := s.markPricingFailed(
  143: 			ctx,
  144: 			forwarded.Reserved,
  145: 			"usage_resolution_invalid",
  146: 		)
  147: 		if failureErr != nil {
  148: 			return ForwardedRequest{}, errors.Join(
  149: 				err,
  150: 				failureErr,
  151: 			)
  152: 		}
  153: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, err
  154: 	}
  155: 
  156: 	finalized, err := s.finalizer.Commit(
  157: 		ctx,
  158: 		FinalizationInput{
  159: 			Reserved:      forwarded.Reserved,
  160: 			ResolvedUsage: resolved,
  161: 		},
  162: 	)
  163: 	if err != nil {
  164: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  165: 			"finalize billable usage: %w",
  166: 			err,
  167: 		)
  168: 	}
  169: 	if finalized.Usage.Status != domain.UsageStatusBillable ||
  170: 		finalized.Usage.LocalRequestID !=
  171: 			forwarded.Reserved.Prepared.LocalRequestID {
  172: 		return ForwardedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  173: 			"%w: invalid finalization result",
  174: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  175: 		)
  176: 	}
  177: 
  178: 	forwarded.ResolvedUsage = resolved
  179: 	forwarded.FinalUsageRecord = finalized.Usage
  180: 	forwarded.AutoCharge = cloneAutoChargeResult(
  181: 		s.autoCharger.Run(
  182: 			ctx,
  183: 			AutoChargeInput{
  184: 				Principal: forwarded.Reserved.
  185: 					Prepared.Principal,
  186: 				FinalUsageRecord: finalized.Usage,
  187: 			},
  188: 		),
  189: 	)
  190: 	return forwarded, nil
  191: }
  192: 
  193: func cloneAutoChargeResult(
  194: 	value AutoChargeResult,
  195: ) AutoChargeResult {
  196: 	result := value
  197: 	result.ProcessedBatchIDs = append(
  198: 		[]string(nil),
  199: 		value.ProcessedBatchIDs...,
  200: 	)
  201: 	if value.BillingBalanceCents != nil {
  202: 		copied := *value.BillingBalanceCents
  203: 		result.BillingBalanceCents = &copied
  204: 	}
  205: 	switch result.Status {
  206: 	case AutoChargeStatusDeferred,
  207: 		AutoChargeStatusProcessed,
  208: 		AutoChargeStatusFailed:
  209: 	default:
  210: 		result = AutoChargeResult{
  211: 			Status: AutoChargeStatusFailed,
  212: 		}
  213: 	}
  214: 	if result.ChargedAmountCents < 0 {
  215: 		result = AutoChargeResult{
  216: 			Status: AutoChargeStatusFailed,
  217: 		}
  218: 	}
  219: 	return result
  220: }
  221: 
  222: func (s *Service) markPricingFailed(
  223: 	ctx context.Context,
  224: 	reserved ReservedRequest,
  225: 	reason string,
  226: ) error {
  227: 	finalized, err := s.finalizer.MarkPricingFailed(
  228: 		ctx,
  229: 		PricingFailureInput{
  230: 			Reserved:      reserved,
  231: 			FailureReason: reason,
  232: 		},
  233: 	)
  234: 	if err != nil {
  235: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  236: 			"finalize pricing failure: %w",
  237: 			err,
  238: 		)
  239: 	}
  240: 	if finalized.Usage.Status !=
  241: 		domain.UsageStatusPricingFailed ||
  242: 		finalized.Usage.LocalRequestID !=
  243: 			reserved.Prepared.LocalRequestID {
  244: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  245: 			"%w: invalid pricing failure result",
  246: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  247: 		)
  248: 	}
  249: 	return nil
  250: }
  251: 
  252: func validateUsageResolution(
  253: 	forwarded ForwardedRequest,
  254: 	resolved UsageResolutionResult,
  255: ) error {
  256: 	if resolved.Completeness == "" ||
  257: 		resolved.UpstreamCostCents < 0 ||
  258: 		resolved.ClientAmountCents < 0 ||
  259: 		resolved.Currency != forwarded.Reserved.Prepared.Plan.Currency ||
  260: 		!nonNegativeUsage(resolved.Usage) {
  261: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  262: 			"%w: invalid usage resolution",
  263: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  264: 		)
  265: 	}
  266: 	return nil
  267: }
  268: 
  269: func (s *Service) prepare(
  270: 	ctx context.Context,
  271: 	input Input,
  272: ) (PreparedRequest, error) {
  273: 	if err := validateInput(input); err != nil {
  274: 		return PreparedRequest{}, err
  275: 	}
  276: 
  277: 	originalPayload := cloneBytes(input.Payload)
  278: 
  279: 	principal, err := s.authenticator.Authenticate(
  280: 		ctx,
  281: 		input.RawAPIKey,
  282: 	)
  283: 	if err != nil {
  284: 		return PreparedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  285: 			"authenticate request: %w",
  286: 			err,
  287: 		)
  288: 	}
  289: 	if err := validatePrincipal(principal); err != nil {
  290: 		return PreparedRequest{}, err
  291: 	}
  292: 
  293: 	parsed, err := s.requestParser.Parse(
  294: 		ctx,
  295: 		ParseInput{
  296: 			APIFamily:    input.APIFamily,
  297: 			EndpointKind: input.EndpointKind,
  298: 			Payload:      cloneBytes(originalPayload),
  299: 		},
  300: 	)
  301: 	if err != nil {
  302: 		return PreparedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  303: 			"parse request: %w",
  304: 			err,
  305: 		)
  306: 	}
  307: 	if strings.TrimSpace(parsed.ClientModel) == "" {
  308: 		return PreparedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  309: 			"%w: parser returned blank client model",
  310: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  311: 		)
  312: 	}
  313: 
  314: 	requestedCapabilities, err := s.capabilityDetector.Detect(
  315: 		ctx,
  316: 		CapabilityInput{
  317: 			APIFamily:    input.APIFamily,
  318: 			EndpointKind: input.EndpointKind,
  319: 			ClientModel:  parsed.ClientModel,
  320: 			Payload:      cloneBytes(originalPayload),
  321: 		},
  322: 	)
  323: 	if err != nil {
  324: 		return PreparedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  325: 			"detect requested capabilities: %w",
  326: 			err,
  327: 		)
  328: 	}
  329: 
  330: 	plan, err := s.routePlanner.Plan(
  331: 		ctx,
  332: 		RoutePlanInput{
  333: 			Principal:             principal,
  334: 			APIFamily:             input.APIFamily,
  335: 			EndpointKind:          input.EndpointKind,
  336: 			ClientModel:           parsed.ClientModel,
  337: 			RequestedCapabilities: requestedCapabilities,
  338: 			Payload:               cloneBytes(originalPayload),
  339: 		},
  340: 	)
  341: 	if err != nil {
  342: 		return PreparedRequest{}, fmt.Errorf(
  343: 			"plan route: %w",
  344: 			err,
  345: 		)
  346: 	}
  347: 	if err := validateRoutePlan(
  348: 		input,
  349: 		parsed,
  350: 		plan,
  351: 	); err != nil {
  352: 		return PreparedRequest{}, err
  353: 	}
  354: 
  355: 	return PreparedRequest{
  356: 		LocalRequestID:        input.LocalRequestID,
  357: 		IdempotencyKey:        cloneStringPointer(input.IdempotencyKey),
  358: 		Principal:             principal,
  359: 		APIFamily:             input.APIFamily,
  360: 		EndpointKind:          input.EndpointKind,
  361: 		ClientModel:           parsed.ClientModel,
  362: 		RequestedCapabilities: requestedCapabilities,
  363: 		Payload:               cloneBytes(originalPayload),
  364: 		Plan:                  plan,
  365: 	}, nil
  366: }
  367: 
  368: func validateInput(input Input) error {
  369: 	if !validLocalRequestID(input.LocalRequestID) ||
  370: 		strings.TrimSpace(input.RawAPIKey) == "" ||
  371: 		input.APIFamily == "" ||
  372: 		input.EndpointKind == "" ||
  373: 		input.Payload == nil {
  374: 		return ErrInvalidInput
  375: 	}
  376: 	if input.IdempotencyKey != nil &&
  377: 		strings.TrimSpace(*input.IdempotencyKey) == "" {
  378: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  379: 			"%w: blank idempotency key",
  380: 			ErrInvalidInput,
  381: 		)
  382: 	}
  383: 	return nil
  384: }
  385: 
  386: func validatePrincipal(value Principal) error {
  387: 	if strings.TrimSpace(value.UserID) == "" ||
  388: 		strings.TrimSpace(value.APIKeyID) == "" ||
  389: 		strings.TrimSpace(value.BillingSubjectUserID) == "" {
  390: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  391: 			"%w: invalid authentication principal",
  392: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  393: 		)
  394: 	}
  395: 	return nil
  396: }
  397: 
  398: func validateRoutePlan(
  399: 	input Input,
  400: 	parsed ParsedRequest,
  401: 	plan RoutePlan,
  402: ) error {
  403: 	route := plan.Route
  404: 	reseller := plan.Reseller
  405: 	price := plan.Price
  406: 
  407: 	if strings.TrimSpace(route.ID) == "" ||
  408: 		strings.TrimSpace(route.ResellerID) == "" ||
  409: 		strings.TrimSpace(route.ClientModel) == "" ||
  410: 		strings.TrimSpace(route.ProviderModel) == "" ||
  411: 		strings.TrimSpace(reseller.ID) == "" ||
  412: 		strings.TrimSpace(price.RouteID) == "" ||
  413: 		strings.TrimSpace(plan.BillingModel) == "" ||
  414: 		route.APIFamily != input.APIFamily ||
  415: 		route.EndpointKind != input.EndpointKind ||
  416: 		route.ClientModel != parsed.ClientModel ||
  417: 		route.ResellerID != reseller.ID ||
  418: 		route.ProviderType == "" ||
  419: 		route.ProviderType != reseller.ProviderType ||
  420: 		price.RouteID != route.ID ||
  421: 		!route.Enabled ||
  422: 		!reseller.Enabled ||
  423: 		!price.Enabled ||
  424: 		price.Currency != "RUB" ||
  425: 		plan.Currency != "RUB" ||
  426: 		plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents < 0 ||
  427: 		plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents < 0 ||
  428: 		strings.TrimSpace(plan.Confidence) == "" ||
  429: 		!nonNegativeUsage(plan.EstimatedUsage) {
  430: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  431: 			"%w: invalid route plan",
  432: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  433: 		)
  434: 	}
  435: 	return nil
  436: }
  437: 
  438: func validateBillingAdmission(
  439: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  440: 	admission BillingAdmissionResult,
  441: ) error {
  442: 	if !admission.Allowed ||
  443: 		admission.Currency != prepared.Plan.Currency ||
  444: 		admission.RequiredReserveCents !=
  445: 			prepared.Plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents ||
  446: 		admission.RemoteBalanceCents < 0 ||
  447: 		admission.PendingAmountCents < 0 ||
  448: 		admission.RemoteBalanceCents <
  449: 			admission.PendingAmountCents ||
  450: 		admission.EffectiveBalanceCents !=
  451: 			admission.RemoteBalanceCents-
  452: 				admission.PendingAmountCents ||
  453: 		admission.EffectiveBalanceCents <
  454: 			admission.RequiredReserveCents {
  455: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  456: 			"%w: invalid billing admission",
  457: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  458: 		)
  459: 	}
  460: 	return nil
  461: }
  462: 
  463: func reservationInput(
  464: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  465: ) ReservationInput {
  466: 	return ReservationInput{
  467: 		LocalRequestID: prepared.LocalRequestID,
  468: 		IdempotencyKey: cloneStringPointer(
  469: 			prepared.IdempotencyKey,
  470: 		),
  471: 		Principal:      prepared.Principal,
  472: 		APIFamily:      prepared.APIFamily,
  473: 		EndpointKind:   prepared.EndpointKind,
  474: 		ClientModel:    prepared.ClientModel,
  475: 		BillingModel:   prepared.Plan.BillingModel,
  476: 		Route:          prepared.Plan.Route,
  477: 		Reseller:       prepared.Plan.Reseller,
  478: 		EstimatedUsage: prepared.Plan.EstimatedUsage,
  479: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: prepared.Plan.
  480: 			EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  481: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: prepared.Plan.
  482: 			EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
  483: 		Currency: prepared.Plan.Currency,
  484: 	}
  485: }
  486: 
  487: func validateReservation(
  488: 	prepared PreparedRequest,
  489: 	result ReservationResult,
  490: ) error {
  491: 	usage := result.Usage
  492: 	expectedIdempotencyKey := ""
  493: 	if prepared.IdempotencyKey != nil {
  494: 		expectedIdempotencyKey = *prepared.IdempotencyKey
  495: 	}
  496: 
  497: 	if result.Disposition != ReservationDispositionCreated &&
  498: 		result.Disposition !=
  499: 			ReservationDispositionAlreadyReserved ||
  500: 		usage.LocalRequestID != prepared.LocalRequestID ||
  501: 		usage.IdempotencyKey != expectedIdempotencyKey ||
  502: 		usage.UserID != prepared.Principal.UserID ||
  503: 		usage.APIKeyID != prepared.Principal.APIKeyID ||
  504: 		usage.APIFamily != prepared.APIFamily ||
  505: 		usage.EndpointKind != prepared.EndpointKind ||
  506: 		usage.ClientModel != prepared.ClientModel ||
  507: 		usage.BillingModel != prepared.Plan.BillingModel ||
  508: 		usage.SelectedRouteID != prepared.Plan.Route.ID ||
  509: 		usage.SelectedResellerID != prepared.Plan.Reseller.ID ||
  510: 		usage.ProviderType != prepared.Plan.Route.ProviderType ||
  511: 		usage.ProviderModel != prepared.Plan.Route.ProviderModel ||
  512: 		usage.EstimatedUsage != prepared.Plan.EstimatedUsage ||
  513: 		usage.EstimatedClientAmountCents !=
  514: 			prepared.Plan.EstimatedClientAmountCents ||
  515: 		usage.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents !=
  516: 			prepared.Plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents ||
  517: 		usage.Currency != prepared.Plan.Currency ||
  518: 		usage.UsageCompleteness != "missing" ||
  519: 		usage.Status != domain.UsageStatusReserved ||
  520: 		usage.Usage != (domain.TokenUsage{}) ||
  521: 		usage.ClientAmountCents != 0 ||
  522: 		usage.ChargedAmountCents != 0 ||
  523: 		usage.RemainingAmountCents != 0 ||
  524: 		usage.ActualUpstreamCostCents != 0 ||
  525: 		usage.ReservedAt == nil ||
  526: 		usage.ReleasedAt != nil ||
  527: 		usage.BillableAt != nil ||
  528: 		usage.ChargedAt != nil ||
  529: 		usage.FailedAt != nil ||
  530: 		usage.CreatedAt.IsZero() ||
  531: 		usage.UpdatedAt.IsZero() ||
  532: 		usage.CreatedAt.Location() != time.UTC ||
  533: 		usage.ReservedAt.Location() != time.UTC ||
  534: 		usage.UpdatedAt.Location() != time.UTC ||
  535: 		!usage.CreatedAt.Equal(*usage.ReservedAt) ||
  536: 		!usage.UpdatedAt.Equal(*usage.ReservedAt) ||
  537: 		strings.TrimSpace(usage.FailureReason) != "" ||
  538: 		strings.TrimSpace(usage.BillingChargeRequestID) != "" {
  539: 		return fmt.Errorf(
  540: 			"%w: invalid atomic reservation",
  541: 			ErrStageContractViolation,
  542: 		)
  543: 	}
  544: 
  545: 	switch result.Disposition {
  546: 	case ReservationDispositionCreated:
  547: 		if result.Reseller == nil ||
  548: 			result.Reseller.ID != prepared.Plan.Reseller.ID ||
  549: 			result.Reseller.ProviderType !=
  550: 				prepared.Plan.Reseller.ProviderType ||
  551: 			result.Reseller.ReservedCents <
  552: 				prepared.Plan.EstimatedUpstreamCostCents {
  553: 			return fmt.Errorf(
  554: 				"%w: invalid created reseller reserve",
  555: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  556: 			)
  557: 		}
  558: 	case ReservationDispositionAlreadyReserved:
  559: 		if result.Reseller != nil {
  560: 			return fmt.Errorf(
  561: 				"%w: replay returned mutable reseller snapshot",
  562: 				ErrStageContractViolation,
  563: 			)
  564: 		}
  565: 	}
  566: 	return nil
  567: }
  568: 
  569: func validLocalRequestID(value string) bool {
  570: 	if !strings.HasPrefix(value, localRequestIDPrefix) ||
  571: 		len(value) == len(localRequestIDPrefix) {
  572: 		return false
  573: 	}
  574: 	for _, current := range value {
  575: 		if unicode.IsControl(current) ||
  576: 			unicode.IsSpace(current) {
  577: 			return false
  578: 		}
  579: 	}
  580: 	return true
  581: }
  582: 
  583: func nonNegativeUsage(value domain.TokenUsage) bool {
  584: 	return value.InputTokens >= 0 &&
  585: 		value.CachedInputTokens >= 0 &&
  586: 		value.OutputTokens >= 0 &&
  587: 		value.ReasoningTokens >= 0 &&
  588: 		value.ImageInputTokens >= 0 &&
  589: 		value.AudioInputTokens >= 0 &&
  590: 		value.AudioOutputTokens >= 0 &&
  591: 		value.FileInputTokens >= 0 &&
  592: 		value.VideoInputTokens >= 0 &&
  593: 		value.ImageGenerationUnits >= 0
  594: }
  595: 
  596: func clonePreparedRequest(
  597: 	value PreparedRequest,
  598: ) PreparedRequest {
  599: 	result := value
  600: 	result.IdempotencyKey = cloneStringPointer(
  601: 		value.IdempotencyKey,
  602: 	)
  603: 	result.Payload = cloneBytes(value.Payload)
  604: 	result.Plan.Fallbacks = cloneRouteFallbackPlans(
  605: 		value.Plan.Fallbacks,
  606: 	)
  607: 	return result
  608: }
  609: 
  610: func cloneRouteFallbackPlans(
  611: 	values []RouteFallbackPlan,
  612: ) []RouteFallbackPlan {
  613: 	if values == nil {
  614: 		return nil
  615: 	}
  616: 	return append([]RouteFallbackPlan(nil), values...)
  617: }
  618: 
  619: func cloneReservationResult(
  620: 	value ReservationResult,
  621: ) ReservationResult {
  622: 	result := value
  623: 	result.Usage.ReservedAt = cloneTimePointer(
  624: 		value.Usage.ReservedAt,
  625: 	)
  626: 	result.Usage.ReleasedAt = cloneTimePointer(
  627: 		value.Usage.ReleasedAt,
  628: 	)
  629: 	result.Usage.BillableAt = cloneTimePointer(
  630: 		value.Usage.BillableAt,
  631: 	)
  632: 	result.Usage.ChargedAt = cloneTimePointer(
  633: 		value.Usage.ChargedAt,
  634: 	)
  635: 	result.Usage.FailedAt = cloneTimePointer(
  636: 		value.Usage.FailedAt,
  637: 	)
  638: 	if value.Reseller != nil {
  639: 		reseller := *value.Reseller
  640: 		reseller.DisabledAt = cloneTimePointer(
  641: 			value.Reseller.DisabledAt,
  642: 		)
  643: 		result.Reseller = &reseller
  644: 	}
  645: 	return result
  646: }
  647: 
  648: func cloneBytes(value []byte) []byte {
  649: 	if value == nil {
  650: 		return nil
  651: 	}
  652: 	return append([]byte(nil), value...)
  653: }
  654: 
  655: func cloneStringPointer(value *string) *string {
  656: 	if value == nil {
  657: 		return nil
  658: 	}
  659: 	copyValue := *value
  660: 	return &copyValue
  661: }
  662: 
  663: func cloneTimePointer(value *time.Time) *time.Time {
  664: 	if value == nil {
  665: 		return nil
  666: 	}
  667: 	copyValue := *value
  668: 	return &copyValue
  669: }

  235: func TestServiceExecuteExecutesCanonicalOrder(t *testing.T) {
  236: 	var calls []string
  237: 	service := mustService(t, validDependencies(&calls))
  238: 	input := validInput()
  239: 
  240: 	reserved, err := service.Execute(
  241: 		context.Background(),
  242: 		input,
  243: 	)
  244: 	if err != nil {
  245: 		t.Fatalf("Execute: %v", err)
  246: 	}
  247: 
  248: 	wantCalls := []string{
  249: 		"authenticate",
  250: 		"parse",
  251: 		"capabilities",
  252: 		"route",
  253: 		"admission",
  254: 		"forwarding",
  255: 		"usage",
  256: 		"finalize",
  257: 		"autocharge",
  258: 	}
  259: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(calls, wantCalls) {
  260: 		t.Fatalf("calls = %#v, want %#v", calls, wantCalls)
  261: 	}
  262: 	if reserved.Reserved.Prepared.LocalRequestID !=
  263: 		input.LocalRequestID ||
  264: 		reserved.Reserved.Prepared.Principal.UserID != "user-1" ||
  265: 		reserved.Reserved.Prepared.ClientModel != "model-1" ||
  266: 		!reserved.Reserved.Prepared.RequestedCapabilities.Chat ||
  267: 		reserved.Reserved.Prepared.Plan.Route.ID != "route-1" ||
  268: 		!bytes.Equal(
  269: 			reserved.Reserved.Prepared.Payload,
  270: 			input.Payload,
  271: 		) ||
  272: 		!reserved.Reserved.Admission.Allowed ||
  273: 		reserved.Reserved.Reservation.Disposition !=
  274: 			ReservationDispositionCreated ||
  275: 		reserved.Reserved.Reservation.Usage.Status !=
  276: 			domain.UsageStatusReserved ||
  277: 		reserved.Response.StatusCode != 200 ||
  278: 		reserved.ResolvedUsage.Completeness != "detailed" ||
  279: 		reserved.ResolvedUsage.ClientAmountCents != 15 ||
  280: 		reserved.FinalUsageRecord.Status !=
  281: 			domain.UsageStatusBillable ||
  282: 		reserved.AutoCharge.Status !=
  283: 			AutoChargeStatusDeferred {
  284: 		t.Fatalf("forwarded = %+v", reserved)
  285: 	}
  286: }

  387: 					test.wantCalls,

  389: 			}
  390: 		})
  391: 	}
  392: }
  393: 
  394: func TestServiceExecuteDoesNotCallForwardingWhenAdmissionDenied(
  395: 	t *testing.T,
  396: ) {
  397: 	var calls []string
  398: 	dependencies := validDependencies(&calls)
  399: 	dependencies.BillingAdmitter = admitFunc(
  400: 		func(
  401: 			_ context.Context,
  402: 			input BillingAdmissionInput,
  403: 		) (BillingAdmissionResult, error) {
  404: 			calls = append(calls, "admission")
  405: 			result := validAdmission(input)
  406: 			result.Allowed = false
  407: 			return result, nil
  408: 		},
  409: 	)
  410: 
  411: 	service := mustService(t, dependencies)
  412: 	_, err := service.Execute(
  413: 		context.Background(),
  414: 		validInput(),
  415: 	)
  416: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrStageContractViolation) {
  417: 		t.Fatalf(
  418: 			"error = %v, want stage contract violation",
  419: 			err,
  420: 		)
  421: 	}
  422: 	wantCalls := []string{
  423: 		"authenticate",
  424: 		"parse",
  425: 		"capabilities",
  426: 		"route",
  427: 		"admission",
  428: 	}
  429: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(calls, wantCalls) {
  430: 		t.Fatalf("calls = %#v, want %#v", calls, wantCalls)
  431: 	}
  432: }

  434: func TestServiceExecuteIsolatesPayloadBetweenStages(t *testing.T) {
  435: 	input := validInput()
  436: 	original := append([]byte(nil), input.Payload...)
  437: 
  438: 	dependencies := validDependencies(nil)
  439: 	dependencies.RequestParser = parseFunc(
  440: 		func(
  441: 			_ context.Context,
  442: 			value ParseInput,
  443: 		) (ParsedRequest, error) {
  444: 			value.Payload[0] = 'X'
  445: 			return ParsedRequest{
  446: 				ClientModel: "model-1",
  447: 			}, nil
  448: 		},
  449: 	)
  450: 	dependencies.CapabilityDetector = detectFunc(
  451: 		func(
  452: 			_ context.Context,
  453: 			value CapabilityInput,
  454: 		) (domain.CapabilitySet, error) {
  455: 			if !bytes.Equal(value.Payload, original) {
  456: 				t.Fatalf(
  457: 					"capability payload = %q, want %q",
  458: 					value.Payload,
  459: 					original,
  460: 				)
  461: 			}
  462: 			value.Payload[0] = 'Y'
  463: 			return domain.CapabilitySet{Chat: true}, nil
  464: 		},
  465: 	)
  466: 	dependencies.RoutePlanner = planFunc(
  467: 		func(
  468: 			_ context.Context,
  469: 			value RoutePlanInput,
  470: 		) (RoutePlan, error) {
  471: 			if !bytes.Equal(value.Payload, original) {
  472: 				t.Fatalf(
  473: 					"route payload = %q, want %q",
  474: 					value.Payload,
  475: 					original,
  476: 				)
  477: 			}
  478: 			value.Payload[0] = 'Z'
  479: 			return validRoutePlan(), nil
  480: 		},
  481: 	)
  482: 
  483: 	service := mustService(t, dependencies)
  484: 	reserved, err := service.Execute(
  485: 		context.Background(),
  486: 		input,
  487: 	)
  488: 	if err != nil {
  489: 		t.Fatalf("Execute: %v", err)
  490: 	}
  491: 	if !bytes.Equal(input.Payload, original) {
  492: 		t.Fatalf(
  493: 			"caller payload = %q, want %q",
  494: 			input.Payload,
  495: 			original,
  496: 		)
  497: 	}
  498: 	if !bytes.Equal(
  499: 		reserved.Reserved.Prepared.Payload,
  500: 		original,
  501: 	) {
  502: 		t.Fatalf(
  503: 			"prepared payload = %q, want %q",
  504: 			reserved.Reserved.Prepared.Payload,
  505: 			original,
  506: 		)
  507: 	}
  508: }

  510: func TestServiceExecuteRejectsInvalidRoutePlan(t *testing.T) {

  518: 			plan.BillingModel = ""

  520: 		},
  521: 	)
  522: 
  523: 	service := mustService(t, dependencies)
  524: 	_, err := service.Execute(
  525: 		context.Background(),
  526: 		validInput(),
  527: 	)
  528: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrStageContractViolation) {
  529: 		t.Fatalf(
  530: 			"error = %v, want stage contract violation",
  531: 			err,
  532: 		)
  533: 	}

  535: 
  536: func validDependencies(
  537: 	calls *[]string,
  538: ) Dependencies {
  539: 	record := func(value string) {
  540: 		if calls != nil {
  541: 			*calls = append(*calls, value)
  542: 		}
  543: 	}
  544: 
  545: 	return Dependencies{
  546: 		Authenticator: authenticateFunc(
  547: 			func(
  548: 				_ context.Context,
  549: 				rawAPIKey string,
  550: 			) (Principal, error) {
  551: 				record("authenticate")
  552: 				if rawAPIKey != "sk_test" {
  553: 					return Principal{}, errors.New(
  554: 						"unexpected API key",
  555: 					)
  556: 				}
  557: 				return Principal{
  558: 					UserID:               "user-1",
  559: 					APIKeyID:             "key-1",
  560: 					BillingSubjectUserID: "billing-1",
  561: 				}, nil
  562: 			},
  563: 		),
  564: 		RequestParser: parseFunc(
  565: 			func(
  566: 				_ context.Context,
  567: 				input ParseInput,
  568: 			) (ParsedRequest, error) {
  569: 				record("parse")
  570: 				if input.APIFamily !=
  571: 					domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible ||
  572: 					input.EndpointKind != domain.EndpointChat {
  573: 					return ParsedRequest{}, errors.New(
  574: 						"unexpected parse input",
  575: 					)
  576: 				}
  577: 				return ParsedRequest{
  578: 					ClientModel: "model-1",
  579: 				}, nil
  580: 			},
  581: 		),
  582: 		CapabilityDetector: detectFunc(
  583: 			func(
  584: 				_ context.Context,
  585: 				input CapabilityInput,
  586: 			) (domain.CapabilitySet, error) {
  587: 				record("capabilities")
  588: 				if input.ClientModel != "model-1" {
  589: 					return domain.CapabilitySet{},
  590: 						errors.New(
  591: 							"unexpected capability input",
  592: 						)
  593: 				}
  594: 				return domain.CapabilitySet{
  595: 					Chat: true,
  596: 				}, nil
  597: 			},
  598: 		),
  599: 		RoutePlanner: planFunc(
  600: 			func(
  601: 				_ context.Context,
  602: 				input RoutePlanInput,
  603: 			) (RoutePlan, error) {
  604: 				record("route")
  605: 				if input.Principal.UserID != "user-1" ||
  606: 					input.ClientModel != "model-1" ||
  607: 					!input.RequestedCapabilities.Chat {
  608: 					return RoutePlan{}, errors.New(
  609: 						"unexpected route input",
  610: 					)
  611: 				}
  612: 				return validRoutePlan(), nil
  613: 			},
  614: 		),
  615: 		BillingAdmitter: admitFunc(
  616: 			func(
  617: 				_ context.Context,
  618: 				input BillingAdmissionInput,
  619: 			) (BillingAdmissionResult, error) {
  620: 				record("admission")
  621: 				if input.Principal.UserID != "user-1" ||
  622: 					input.RequiredReserveCents != 20 ||
  623: 					input.Currency != "RUB" {
  624: 					return BillingAdmissionResult{},
  625: 						errors.New(
  626: 							"unexpected admission input",
  627: 						)
  628: 				}
  629: 				return validAdmission(input), nil
  630: 			},
  631: 		),
  632: 		Forwarding: forwardingStageFunc(
  633: 			func(
  634: 				_ context.Context,
  635: 				prepared PreparedRequest,
  636: 				admission BillingAdmissionResult,
  637: 			) (ForwardedRequest, error) {
  638: 				record("forwarding")
  639: 				if prepared.LocalRequestID != "llmreq_test" ||
  640: 					prepared.Principal.UserID != "user-1" ||
  641: 					prepared.Plan.Route.ID != "route-1" ||
  642: 					!admission.Allowed {
  643: 					return ForwardedRequest{},
  644: 						errors.New(
  645: 							"unexpected forwarding input",
  646: 						)
  647: 				}
  648: 				reservation := validReservation(
  649: 					reservationInput(prepared),
  650: 				)
  651: 				return ForwardedRequest{
  652: 					Reserved: ReservedRequest{
  653: 						Prepared:    prepared,
  654: 						Admission:   admission,
  655: 						Reservation: reservation,
  656: 					},
  657: 					Response: ports.ForwardResponse{
  658: 						StatusCode: 200,
  659: 						Body:       []byte(`{"ok":true}`),
  660: 					},
  661: 				}, nil
  662: 			},
  663: 		),
  664: 		UsageResolver: usageResolverFunc(
  665: 			func(
  666: 				_ context.Context,
  667: 				input UsageResolutionInput,
  668: 			) (UsageResolutionResult, error) {
  669: 				record("usage")
  670: 				if input.Reserved.Prepared.LocalRequestID !=
  671: 					"llmreq_test" ||
  672: 					input.Response.StatusCode != 200 {
  673: 					return UsageResolutionResult{},
  674: 						errors.New(
  675: 							"unexpected usage input",
  676: 						)
  677: 				}
  678: 				return UsageResolutionResult{
  679: 					Usage: domain.TokenUsage{
  680: 						InputTokens:  10,
  681: 						OutputTokens: 5,
  682: 					},
  683: 					Completeness:      "detailed",
  684: 					UpstreamCostCents: 10,
  685: 					ClientAmountCents: 15,
  686: 					Currency:          "RUB",
  687: 				}, nil
  688: 			},
  689: 		),
  690: 		Finalizer: finalizerFunc{
  691: 			commit: func(
  692: 				_ context.Context,
  693: 				input FinalizationInput,
  694: 			) (FinalizationResult, error) {
  695: 				record("finalize")
  696: 				return FinalizationResult{
  697: 					Usage: domain.UsageRecord{
  698: 						LocalRequestID: input.Reserved.
  699: 							Prepared.LocalRequestID,
  700: 						UserID: input.Reserved.Prepared.
  701: 							Principal.UserID,
  702: 						Currency: "RUB",
  703: 						Status: domain.
  704: 							UsageStatusBillable,
  705: 					},
  706: 				}, nil
  707: 			},
  708: 			pricingFailed: func(
  709: 				_ context.Context,
  710: 				input PricingFailureInput,
  711: 			) (FinalizationResult, error) {
  712: 				record("pricing_failed")
  713: 				return FinalizationResult{
  714: 					Usage: domain.UsageRecord{
  715: 						LocalRequestID: input.Reserved.
  716: 							Prepared.LocalRequestID,
  717: 						Status: domain.
  718: 							UsageStatusPricingFailed,
  719: 					},
  720: 				}, nil
  721: 			},
  722: 		},
  723: 		AutoCharger: autoChargerFunc(
  724: 			func(
  725: 				_ context.Context,
  726: 				input AutoChargeInput,
  727: 			) AutoChargeResult {
  728: 				record("autocharge")
  729: 				if input.FinalUsageRecord.Status !=
  730: 					domain.UsageStatusBillable {
  731: 					return AutoChargeResult{
  732: 						Status: AutoChargeStatusFailed,
  733: 					}
  734: 				}
  735: 				return AutoChargeResult{
  736: 					Status: AutoChargeStatusDeferred,
  737: 				}
  738: 			},
  739: 		),
  740: 	}
  741: }
  742: 
  743: func failingDependencies(
  744: 	value Dependencies,
  745: 	calls *[]string,
  746: 	stage string,
  747: 	stageError error,
  748: ) Dependencies {
  749: 	record := func() {
  750: 		*calls = append(*calls, stage)
  751: 	}
  752: 
  753: 	switch stage {
  754: 	case "authenticate":
  755: 		value.Authenticator = authenticateFunc(
  756: 			func(
  757: 				context.Context,
  758: 				string,
  759: 			) (Principal, error) {
  760: 				record()
  761: 				return Principal{}, stageError
  762: 			},
  763: 		)
  764: 	case "parse":
  765: 		value.RequestParser = parseFunc(
  766: 			func(
  767: 				context.Context,
  768: 				ParseInput,
  769: 			) (ParsedRequest, error) {
  770: 				record()
  771: 				return ParsedRequest{}, stageError
  772: 			},
  773: 		)
  774: 	case "capabilities":
  775: 		value.CapabilityDetector = detectFunc(
  776: 			func(
  777: 				context.Context,
  778: 				CapabilityInput,
  779: 			) (domain.CapabilitySet, error) {
  780: 				record()
  781: 				return domain.CapabilitySet{}, stageError
  782: 			},
  783: 		)
  784: 	case "route":
  785: 		value.RoutePlanner = planFunc(
  786: 			func(
  787: 				context.Context,
  788: 				RoutePlanInput,
  789: 			) (RoutePlan, error) {
  790: 				record()
  791: 				return RoutePlan{}, stageError
  792: 			},
  793: 		)
  794: 	case "admission":
  795: 		value.BillingAdmitter = admitFunc(
  796: 			func(
  797: 				context.Context,
  798: 				BillingAdmissionInput,
  799: 			) (BillingAdmissionResult, error) {
  800: 				record()
  801: 				return BillingAdmissionResult{}, stageError
  802: 			},
  803: 		)
  804: 	case "forwarding":
  805: 		value.Forwarding = forwardingStageFunc(
  806: 			func(
  807: 				context.Context,
  808: 				PreparedRequest,
  809: 				BillingAdmissionResult,
  810: 			) (ForwardedRequest, error) {
  811: 				record()
  812: 				return ForwardedRequest{}, stageError
  813: 			},
  814: 		)
  815: 	case "usage":
  816: 		value.UsageResolver = usageResolverFunc(
  817: 			func(
  818: 				context.Context,
  819: 				UsageResolutionInput,
  820: 			) (UsageResolutionResult, error) {
  821: 				record()
  822: 				return UsageResolutionResult{}, stageError
  823: 			},
  824: 		)
  825: 	default:
  826: 		panic("unknown stage")
  827: 	}
  828: 	return value
  829: }
  830: 
  831: func validInput() Input {
  832: 	idempotencyKey := "idem-1"
  833: 	return Input{
  834: 		LocalRequestID: "llmreq_test",
  835: 		RawAPIKey:      "sk_test",
  836: 		IdempotencyKey: &idempotencyKey,
  837: 		APIFamily:      domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible,
  838: 		EndpointKind:   domain.EndpointChat,
  839: 		Payload:        []byte(`{"model":"model-1"}`),
  840: 	}
  841: }
  842: 
  843: func validRoutePlan() RoutePlan {
  844: 	return RoutePlan{
  845: 		Route: domain.Route{
  846: 			ID:            "route-1",
  847: 			ResellerID:    "reseller-1",
  848: 			ProviderType:  domain.ProviderOpenAI,
  849: 			APIFamily:     domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible,
  850: 			EndpointKind:  domain.EndpointChat,
  851: 			ClientModel:   "model-1",
  852: 			ProviderModel: "model-1",
  853: 			Enabled:       true,
  854: 		},
  855: 		Reseller: domain.Reseller{
  856: 			ID:           "reseller-1",
  857: 			ProviderType: domain.ProviderOpenAI,
  858: 			Enabled:      true,
  859: 		},
  860: 		Price: domain.RoutePrice{
  861: 			RouteID:  "route-1",
  862: 			Currency: "RUB",
  863: 			Enabled:  true,
  864: 		},
  865: 		BillingModel: "openai:model-1",
  866: 		EstimatedUsage: domain.TokenUsage{
  867: 			InputTokens:  10,
  868: 			OutputTokens: 5,
  869: 		},
  870: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: 20,
  871: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: 10,
  872: 		Currency:                   "RUB",
  873: 		Confidence:                 "conservative",
  874: 	}
  875: }
  876: 
  877: func validAdmission(
  878: 	input BillingAdmissionInput,
  879: ) BillingAdmissionResult {
  880: 	return BillingAdmissionResult{
  881: 		Allowed:               true,
  882: 		RemoteBalanceCents:    1000,
  883: 		PendingAmountCents:    100,
  884: 		EffectiveBalanceCents: 900,
  885: 		RequiredReserveCents:  input.RequiredReserveCents,
  886: 		Currency:              input.Currency,
  887: 	}
  888: }
  889: 
  890: func validReservation(
  891: 	input ReservationInput,
  892: ) ReservationResult {
  893: 	reservedAt := time.Date(
  894: 		2026,
  895: 		time.June,
  896: 		14,
  897: 		12,
  898: 		0,
  899: 		0,
  900: 		0,
  901: 		time.UTC,
  902: 	)
  903: 	idempotencyKey := ""
  904: 	if input.IdempotencyKey != nil {
  905: 		idempotencyKey = *input.IdempotencyKey
  906: 	}
  907: 	reseller := input.Reseller
  908: 	reseller.ReservedCents = 10
  909: 	return ReservationResult{
  910: 		Disposition: ReservationDispositionCreated,
  911: 		Usage: domain.UsageRecord{
  912: 			LocalRequestID:     input.LocalRequestID,
  913: 			IdempotencyKey:     idempotencyKey,
  914: 			UserID:             input.Principal.UserID,
  915: 			APIKeyID:           input.Principal.APIKeyID,
  916: 			APIFamily:          input.APIFamily,
  917: 			EndpointKind:       input.EndpointKind,
  918: 			ClientModel:        input.ClientModel,
  919: 			BillingModel:       input.BillingModel,
  920: 			SelectedRouteID:    input.Route.ID,
  921: 			SelectedResellerID: input.Reseller.ID,
  922: 			ProviderType:       input.Route.ProviderType,
  923: 			ProviderModel:      input.Route.ProviderModel,
  924: 			EstimatedUsage:     input.EstimatedUsage,
  925: 			EstimatedClientAmountCents: input.
  926: 				EstimatedClientAmountCents,
  927: 			EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: input.
  928: 				EstimatedUpstreamCostCents,
  929: 			Currency:          input.Currency,
  930: 			UsageCompleteness: "missing",
  931: 			Status:            domain.UsageStatusReserved,
  932: 			CreatedAt:         reservedAt,
  933: 			ReservedAt:        &reservedAt,
  934: 			UpdatedAt:         reservedAt,
  935: 		},
  936: 		Reseller: &reseller,
  937: 	}
  938: }
  939: 
  940: func mustService(
  941: 	t *testing.T,
  942: 	dependencies Dependencies,
  943: ) *Service {
  944: 	t.Helper()
  945: 
  946: 	service, err := NewService(dependencies)
  947: 	if err != nil {
  948: 		t.Fatalf("NewService: %v", err)
  949: 	}
  950: 	return service
  951: }

    1: package llmrequest

    7: 
    8: type Input struct {
    9: 	LocalRequestID string
   10: 	RawAPIKey      string
   11: 	IdempotencyKey *string
   12: 
   13: 	APIFamily    domain.APIFamily
   14: 	EndpointKind domain.EndpointKind
   15: 
   16: 	Payload []byte
   17: }
   18: 
   19: type Principal struct {
   20: 	UserID               string
   21: 	APIKeyID             string
   22: 	BillingSubjectUserID string
   23: }
   24: 
   25: type ParseInput struct {
   26: 	APIFamily    domain.APIFamily
   27: 	EndpointKind domain.EndpointKind
   28: 	Payload      []byte
   29: }
   30: 
   31: type ParsedRequest struct {
   32: 	ClientModel string
   33: }
   34: 
   35: type CapabilityInput struct {
   36: 	APIFamily    domain.APIFamily
   37: 	EndpointKind domain.EndpointKind
   38: 	ClientModel  string
   39: 	Payload      []byte
   40: }
   41: 
   42: type RoutePlanInput struct {
   43: 	Principal Principal
   44: 
   45: 	APIFamily             domain.APIFamily
   46: 	EndpointKind          domain.EndpointKind
   47: 	ClientModel           string
   48: 	RequestedCapabilities domain.CapabilitySet
   49: 	Payload               []byte
   50: }
   51: 
   52: type RouteFallbackPlan struct {
   53: 	Route    domain.Route
   54: 	Reseller domain.Reseller
   55: 	Price    domain.RoutePrice
   56: 
   57: 	BillingModel   string
   58: 	EstimatedUsage domain.TokenUsage
   59: 
   60: 	EstimatedClientAmountCents int64
   61: 	EstimatedUpstreamCostCents int64
   62: 
   63: 	Currency   string
   64: 	Confidence string
   65: }
   66: 
   67: type RoutePlan struct {
   68: 	Route    domain.Route
   69: 	Reseller domain.Reseller
   70: 	Price    domain.RoutePrice
   71: 
   72: 	BillingModel   string
   73: 	EstimatedUsage domain.TokenUsage
   74: 
   75: 	EstimatedClientAmountCents int64
   76: 	EstimatedUpstreamCostCents int64
   77: 
   78: 	Currency   string
   79: 	Confidence string
   80: 
   81: 	Fallbacks []RouteFallbackPlan
   82: }
   83: 
   84: type PreparedRequest struct {
   85: 	LocalRequestID string
   86: 	IdempotencyKey *string
   87: 
   88: 	Principal Principal
   89: 
   90: 	APIFamily             domain.APIFamily
   91: 	EndpointKind          domain.EndpointKind
   92: 	ClientModel           string
   93: 	RequestedCapabilities domain.CapabilitySet
   94: 
   95: 	Payload []byte
   96: 	Plan    RoutePlan
   97: }
   98: 
   99: type BillingAdmissionInput struct {
  100: 	Principal Principal
  101: 
  102: 	RequiredReserveCents int64
  103: 	Currency             string
  104: }
  105: 
  106: type BillingAdmissionResult struct {
  107: 	Allowed bool
  108: 
  109: 	RemoteBalanceCents    int64
  110: 	PendingAmountCents    int64
  111: 	EffectiveBalanceCents int64
  112: 	RequiredReserveCents  int64
  113: 	Currency              string
  114: }
  115: 
  116: type ReservationInput struct {
  117: 	LocalRequestID string
  118: 	IdempotencyKey *string
  119: 
  120: 	Principal Principal
  121: 
  122: 	APIFamily    domain.APIFamily
  123: 	EndpointKind domain.EndpointKind
  124: 	ClientModel  string
  125: 	BillingModel string
  126: 
  127: 	Route    domain.Route
  128: 	Reseller domain.Reseller
  129: 
  130: 	EstimatedUsage domain.TokenUsage
  131: 
  132: 	EstimatedClientAmountCents int64
  133: 	EstimatedUpstreamCostCents int64
  134: 	Currency                   string
  135: }
  136: 
  137: type RouteReservationTransferInput struct {
  138: 	// ExpectedUsage is the exact currently persisted reserved usage snapshot.
  139: 	// The transfer must fail rather than overwrite a different committed state.
  140: 	ExpectedUsage domain.UsageRecord
  141: 
  142: 	// Target is the immutable fallback snapshot selected during the original
  143: 	// routing decision. The transfer must not re-query or re-price the route.
  144: 	Target RouteFallbackPlan
  145: }
  146: 
  147: type RouteReservationTransferResult struct {
  148: 	// Usage is the exact committed reserved usage snapshot after the transfer.
  149: 	Usage domain.UsageRecord
  150: 
  151: 	// ReleasedReseller is the committed previous reseller balance snapshot after
  152: 	// its unused estimated upstream reserve has been removed.
  153: 	ReleasedReseller domain.Reseller
  154: 
  155: 	// ReservedReseller is the committed target reseller balance snapshot after
  156: 	// the target estimated upstream reserve has been added.
  157: 	ReservedReseller domain.Reseller
  158: }
  159: 
  160: type ReservationDisposition string
  161: 
  162: const (
  163: 	ReservationDispositionCreated         ReservationDisposition = "created"
  164: 	ReservationDispositionAlreadyReserved ReservationDisposition = "already_reserved"
  165: )
  166: 
  167: type ReservationResult struct {
  168: 	Disposition ReservationDisposition
  169: 	Usage       domain.UsageRecord
  170: 	Reseller    *domain.Reseller
  171: }
  172: 
  173: type ReservedRequest struct {
  174: 	Prepared    PreparedRequest
  175: 	Admission   BillingAdmissionResult
  176: 	Reservation ReservationResult
  177: }
  178: 
  179: type UsageResolutionInput struct {
  180: 	Reserved ReservedRequest
  181: 	Response ports.ForwardResponse
  182: }
  183: 
  184: type UsageResolutionResult struct {
  185: 	Usage        domain.TokenUsage
  186: 	Completeness string
  187: 	Estimated    bool
  188: 
  189: 	UpstreamCostCents int64
  190: 	ClientAmountCents int64
  191: 	Currency          string
  192: 
  193: 	ProviderRequestID     string
  194: 	ProviderResponseModel string
  195: }
  196: 
  197: type FinalizationInput struct {
  198: 	Reserved      ReservedRequest
  199: 	ResolvedUsage UsageResolutionResult
  200: }
  201: 
  202: type PricingFailureInput struct {
  203: 	Reserved      ReservedRequest
  204: 	FailureReason string
  205: }
  206: 
  207: type FinalizationResult struct {
  208: 	Usage domain.UsageRecord
  209: }
  210: 
  211: type AutoChargeStatus string
  212: 
  213: const (
  214: 	AutoChargeStatusDeferred  AutoChargeStatus = "deferred"
  215: 	AutoChargeStatusProcessed AutoChargeStatus = "processed"
  216: 	AutoChargeStatusFailed    AutoChargeStatus = "failed"
  217: )
  218: 
  219: type AutoChargeInput struct {
  220: 	Principal        Principal
  221: 	FinalUsageRecord domain.UsageRecord
  222: }
  223: 
  224: type AutoChargeResult struct {
  225: 	Status AutoChargeStatus
  226: 
  227: 	ProcessedBatchIDs  []string
  228: 	ChargedAmountCents int64
  229: 
  230: 	BillingBalanceCents *int64
  231: }

   23: type Dependencies struct {
   24: 	Routes         ports.ModelCatalogRouteRepository
   25: 	Resellers      ports.ResellerQueryRepository
   26: 	Prices         ports.RoutePriceRepository
   27: 	Secrets        ports.SecretPresenceChecker
   28: 	AdapterSupport ports.ForwardingAdapterSupport
   29: 	RewriteSupport ports.ModelIdentifierRewriteSupport
   30: 	Clock          ports.Clock
   31: 	Currency       string
   32: }
   33: 
   34: type Service struct {
   35: 	deps Dependencies
   36: }
   37: 
   38: type routeGroup struct {
   39: 	kind   domain.EndpointKind
   40: 	routes []domain.Route
   41: }

   43: type catalogCandidate struct {
   44: 	route         domain.Route
   45: 	pricing       Pricing
   46: 	referenceCost int64

   49: func NewService(deps Dependencies) (*Service, error) {
   50: 	if deps.Routes == nil ||
   51: 		deps.Resellers == nil ||
   52: 		deps.Prices == nil ||
   53: 		deps.Secrets == nil ||
   54: 		deps.AdapterSupport == nil ||
   55: 		deps.RewriteSupport == nil ||
   56: 		deps.Clock == nil ||
   57: 		!validOpaque(deps.Currency) {
   58: 		return nil, ErrInvalidInput
   59: 	}
   60: 	return &Service{deps: deps}, nil
   61: }
   62: 
   63: func (s *Service) List(
   64: 	ctx context.Context,
   65: 	apiFamily domain.APIFamily,
   66: ) (Catalog, error) {
   67: 	if ctx == nil ||
   68: 		s == nil ||
   69: 		!validAPIFamily(apiFamily) {
   70: 		return Catalog{}, ErrInvalidInput
   71: 	}
   72: 	if err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {
   73: 		return Catalog{}, err
   74: 	}
   75: 
   76: 	now := s.deps.Clock.Now()
   77: 	if now.IsZero() {
   78: 		return Catalog{}, ErrCatalogUnavailable
   79: 	}
   80: 	now = now.UTC()
   81: 
   82: 	routes, err := s.deps.Routes.ListModelCatalogRoutes(
   83: 		ctx,
   84: 		apiFamily,
   85: 	)
   86: 	if err != nil {
   87: 		return Catalog{}, mapDependencyError(err)
   88: 	}
   89: 
   90: 	groups, routeIDs, resellerIDs, err :=
   91: 		groupCatalogRoutes(routes, apiFamily)
   92: 	if err != nil {
   93: 		return Catalog{}, err
   94: 	}
   95: 
   96: 	resellers, err := s.deps.Resellers.FindByIDs(
   97: 		ctx,
   98: 		resellerIDs,
   99: 	)
  100: 	if err != nil {
  101: 		return Catalog{}, mapDependencyError(err)
  102: 	}
  103: 	if err := validateReturnedResellers(
  104: 		resellers,
  105: 		resellerIDs,
  106: 	); err != nil {
  107: 		return Catalog{}, err
  108: 	}
  109: 
  110: 	prices, err := s.deps.Prices.FindByRouteIDs(
  111: 		ctx,
  112: 		routeIDs,
  113: 	)
  114: 	if err != nil {
  115: 		return Catalog{}, mapDependencyError(err)
  116: 	}
  117: 	if err := validateReturnedPrices(
  118: 		prices,
  119: 		routeIDs,
  120: 	); err != nil {
  121: 		return Catalog{}, err
  122: 	}
  123: 
  124: 	modelIDs := make([]string, 0, len(groups))
  125: 	for modelID := range groups {
  126: 		modelIDs = append(modelIDs, modelID)
  127: 	}
  128: 	sort.Strings(modelIDs)
  129: 
  130: 	secretPresence := make(map[string]bool)
  131: 	result := Catalog{
  132: 		Object: catalogObject,
  133: 		Data:   make([]Model, 0, len(modelIDs)),
  134: 	}
  135: 
  136: 	for _, modelID := range modelIDs {
  137: 		group := groups[modelID]
  138: 		model, err := s.buildModel(
  139: 			ctx,
  140: 			modelID,
  141: 			group,
  142: 			resellers,
  143: 			prices,
  144: 			secretPresence,
  145: 			now,
  146: 		)
  147: 		if err != nil {
  148: 			return Catalog{}, err
  149: 		}
  150: 		result.Data = append(result.Data, model)
  151: 	}
  152: 	return result, nil
  153: }
  154: 
  155: func groupCatalogRoutes(
  156: 	routes []domain.Route,
  157: 	apiFamily domain.APIFamily,
  158: ) (
  159: 	map[string]routeGroup,
  160: 	[]string,
  161: 	[]string,
  162: 	error,
  163: ) {
  164: 	groups := make(map[string]routeGroup)
  165: 	routeIDs := make([]string, 0, len(routes))
  166: 	resellerIDs := make([]string, 0, len(routes))
  167: 	seenRoutes := make(map[string]struct{}, len(routes))
  168: 	seenResellers := make(map[string]struct{})
  169: 
  170: 	for _, route := range routes {
  171: 		if err := validateRouteRecord(
  172: 			route,
  173: 			apiFamily,
  174: 		); err != nil {
  175: 			return nil, nil, nil, err
  176: 		}
  177: 		if _, exists := seenRoutes[route.ID]; exists {
  178: 			return nil, nil, nil, ErrCatalogUnavailable
  179: 		}
  180: 		seenRoutes[route.ID] = struct{}{}
  181: 		routeIDs = append(routeIDs, route.ID)
  182: 
  183: 		if _, exists := seenResellers[route.ResellerID]; !exists {
  184: 			seenResellers[route.ResellerID] = struct{}{}
  185: 			resellerIDs = append(
  186: 				resellerIDs,
  187: 				route.ResellerID,
  188: 			)
  189: 		}
  190: 
  191: 		group, exists := groups[route.ClientModel]
  192: 		if exists && group.kind != route.EndpointKind {
  193: 			return nil, nil, nil, ErrCatalogUnavailable
  194: 		}
  195: 		group.kind = route.EndpointKind
  196: 		group.routes = append(group.routes, route)
  197: 		groups[route.ClientModel] = group
  198: 	}
  199: 
  200: 	sort.Strings(routeIDs)
  201: 	sort.Strings(resellerIDs)
  202: 	return groups, routeIDs, resellerIDs, nil
  203: }
  204: 
  205: func (s *Service) buildModel(
  206: 	ctx context.Context,
  207: 	modelID string,
  208: 	group routeGroup,
  209: 	resellers map[string]domain.Reseller,
  210: 	prices map[string]domain.RoutePrice,
  211: 	secretPresence map[string]bool,
  212: 	now time.Time,
  213: ) (Model, error) {
  214: 	candidates := make(
  215: 		[]catalogCandidate,
  216: 		0,
  217: 		len(group.routes),
  218: 	)
  219: 
  220: 	for _, route := range group.routes {
  221: 		reseller, exists := resellers[route.ResellerID]
  222: 		if !exists {
  223: 			return Model{}, ErrCatalogUnavailable
  224: 		}
  225: 		if err := validateResellerRecord(
  226: 			reseller,
  227: 			route,
  228: 		); err != nil {
  229: 			return Model{}, err
  230: 		}
  231: 
  232: 		price, hasPrice := prices[route.ID]
  233: 		if hasPrice {
  234: 			if err := validatePriceRecord(
  235: 				price,
  236: 				route.ID,
  237: 			); err != nil {
  238: 				return Model{}, err
  239: 			}
  240: 		}
  241: 
  242: 		if !hasPrice ||
  243: 			!catalogRouteStaticallyAvailable(
  244: 				route,
  245: 				reseller,
  246: 				price,
  247: 				s.deps.Currency,
  248: 				now,
  249: 			) ||
  250: 			!s.routeConfigurationSupported(route) {
  251: 			continue
  252: 		}
  253: 
  254: 		exists, known := secretPresence[reseller.APIKeyEnv]
  255: 		if !known {
  256: 			var err error
  257: 			exists, err = s.deps.Secrets.Exists(
  258: 				ctx,
  259: 				reseller.APIKeyEnv,
  260: 			)
  261: 			if err != nil {
  262: 				return Model{}, mapDependencyError(err)
  263: 			}
  264: 			secretPresence[reseller.APIKeyEnv] = exists
  265: 		}
  266: 		if !exists {
  267: 			continue
  268: 		}
  269: 
  270: 		pricing, err := publicPricing(price)
  271: 		if err != nil {
  272: 			return Model{}, err
  273: 		}
  274: 		referenceCost, ok := catalogReferenceCost(
  275: 			route.EndpointKind,
  276: 			pricing,
  277: 		)
  278: 		if !ok {
  279: 			continue
  280: 		}
  281: 		candidates = append(
  282: 			candidates,
  283: 			catalogCandidate{
  284: 				route:         route,
  285: 				pricing:       pricing,
  286: 				referenceCost: referenceCost,
  287: 			},
  288: 		)
  289: 	}
  290: 
  291: 	model := Model{
  292: 		ID:           modelID,
  293: 		Object:       modelObject,
  294: 		OwnedBy:      modelOwner,
  295: 		Type:         string(group.kind),
  296: 		Active:       false,
  297: 		Pricing:      nil,
  298: 		Capabilities: domain.CapabilitySet{},
  299: 	}
  300: 	if len(candidates) == 0 {
  301: 		return model, nil
  302: 	}
  303: 
  304: 	sort.Slice(candidates, func(i, j int) bool {
  305: 		left := candidates[i]
  306: 		right := candidates[j]
  307: 		if left.referenceCost != right.referenceCost {
  308: 			return left.referenceCost < right.referenceCost
  309: 		}
  310: 		if left.route.Priority != right.route.Priority {
  311: 			return left.route.Priority < right.route.Priority
  312: 		}
  313: 		return left.route.ID < right.route.ID
  314: 	})
  315: 
  316: 	selectedPricing := candidates[0].pricing
  317: 	model.Active = true
  318: 	model.Pricing = &selectedPricing
  319: 	for _, candidate := range candidates {
  320: 		model.Capabilities = unionCapabilities(
  321: 			model.Capabilities,
  322: 			candidate.route.Capabilities,
  323: 		)
  324: 	}
  325: 	return model, nil
  326: }
  327: 
  328: func (s *Service) routeConfigurationSupported(
  329: 	route domain.Route,
  330: ) bool {
  331: 	if !s.deps.AdapterSupport.SupportsForwardingAdapter(
  332: 		route.APIFamily,
  333: 		route.ProviderType,
  334: 		route.EndpointKind,
  335: 	) {
  336: 		return false
  337: 	}
  338: 	if !endpointCapabilityPresent(route) {
  339: 		return false
  340: 	}
  341: 
  342: 	switch route.ModelRewritePolicy {
  343: 	case domain.ModelRewritePolicyNone:
  344: 		return route.ProviderModel == route.ClientModel
  345: 	case domain.ModelRewritePolicyProviderModel:
  346: 		return route.ProviderModel != "" &&
  347: 			s.deps.RewriteSupport.
  348: 				SupportsModelIdentifierRewrite(
  349: 					route.APIFamily,
  350: 					route.ProviderType,
  351: 				)
  352: 	default:
  353: 		return false
  354: 	}
  355: }
  356: 
  357: func catalogRouteStaticallyAvailable(
  358: 	route domain.Route,
  359: 	reseller domain.Reseller,
  360: 	price domain.RoutePrice,
  361: 	currency string,
  362: 	now time.Time,
  363: ) bool {
  364: 	if !route.Enabled ||
  365: 		route.DisabledAt != nil ||
  366: 		!reseller.Enabled ||
  367: 		reseller.DisabledAt != nil ||
  368: 		!price.Enabled ||
  369: 		price.Currency != currency {
  370: 		return false
  371: 	}
  372: 	if route.CooldownUntil != nil &&
  373: 		route.CooldownUntil.After(now) {
  374: 		return false
  375: 	}
  376: 	return positiveAvailableBalance(reseller)
  377: }
  378: 
  379: func positiveAvailableBalance(
  380: 	reseller domain.Reseller,
  381: ) bool {
  382: 	available := big.NewInt(reseller.BalanceCents)
  383: 	available.Sub(
  384: 		available,
  385: 		big.NewInt(reseller.ReservedCents),
  386: 	)
  387: 	available.Sub(
  388: 		available,
  389: 		big.NewInt(reseller.MinimumBalanceCents),
  390: 	)
  391: 	return available.Sign() > 0
  392: }
  393: 
  394: func publicPricing(
  395: 	price domain.RoutePrice,
  396: ) (Pricing, error) {
  397: 	values := []int64{
  398: 		price.InputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  399: 		price.CachedInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  400: 		price.OutputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  401: 		price.ReasoningOutputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  402: 		price.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  403: 		price.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  404: 		price.AudioOutputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  405: 		price.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  406: 		price.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  407: 		price.ImageGenerationPricePerUnitCents,
  408: 	}
  409: 	markedUp := make([]int64, len(values))
  410: 	for index, value := range values {
  411: 		result, err := applyMarkup(
  412: 			value,
  413: 			price.MarkupCoefficient,
  414: 		)
  415: 		if err != nil {
  416: 			return Pricing{}, err
  417: 		}
  418: 		markedUp[index] = result
  419: 	}
  420: 
  421: 	return Pricing{
  422: 		Currency:                             price.Currency,
  423: 		InputPricePer1MTokensCents:           markedUp[0],
  424: 		CachedInputPricePer1MTokensCents:     markedUp[1],
  425: 		OutputPricePer1MTokensCents:          markedUp[2],
  426: 		ReasoningOutputPricePer1MTokensCents: markedUp[3],
  427: 		ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents:      markedUp[4],
  428: 		AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents:      markedUp[5],
  429: 		AudioOutputPricePer1MTokensCents:     markedUp[6],
  430: 		FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents:       markedUp[7],
  431: 		VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents:      markedUp[8],
  432: 		ImageGenerationPricePerUnitCents:     markedUp[9],
  433: 		ImageGenerationUnitKind:              price.ImageGenerationUnitKind,
  434: 	}, nil
  435: }
  436: 
  437: func applyMarkup(
  438: 	value int64,
  439: 	markup float64,
  440: ) (int64, error) {
  441: 	if value < 0 ||
  442: 		markup <= 0 ||
  443: 		math.IsNaN(markup) ||
  444: 		math.IsInf(markup, 0) {
  445: 		return 0, ErrCatalogUnavailable
  446: 	}
  447: 	if value == 0 {
  448: 		return 0, nil
  449: 	}
  450: 
  451: 	canonicalMarkup := strconv.FormatFloat(
  452: 		markup,
  453: 		'g',
  454: 		-1,
  455: 		64,
  456: 	)
  457: 	ratio, ok := new(big.Rat).SetString(
  458: 		canonicalMarkup,
  459: 	)
  460: 	if !ok || ratio.Sign() <= 0 {
  461: 		return 0, ErrCatalogUnavailable
  462: 	}
  463: 
  464: 	numerator := new(big.Int).Mul(
  465: 		big.NewInt(value),
  466: 		ratio.Num(),
  467: 	)
  468: 	quotient := new(big.Int)
  469: 	remainder := new(big.Int)
  470: 	quotient.QuoRem(
  471: 		numerator,
  472: 		ratio.Denom(),
  473: 		remainder,
  474: 	)
  475: 	if remainder.Sign() > 0 {
  476: 		quotient.Add(quotient, big.NewInt(1))
  477: 	}
  478: 	if !quotient.IsInt64() {
  479: 		return 0, ErrCatalogUnavailable
  480: 	}
  481: 	return quotient.Int64(), nil
  482: }
  483: 
  484: func catalogReferenceCost(
  485: 	kind domain.EndpointKind,
  486: 	pricing Pricing,
  487: ) (int64, bool) {
  488: 	switch kind {
  489: 	case domain.EndpointChat:
  490: 		if pricing.InputPricePer1MTokensCents <= 0 ||
  491: 			pricing.OutputPricePer1MTokensCents <= 0 {
  492: 			return 0, false
  493: 		}
  494: 		total, ok := safeAdd(
  495: 			pricing.InputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  496: 			pricing.OutputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  497: 		)
  498: 		return total, ok
  499: 
  500: 	case domain.EndpointEmbeddings:
  501: 		if pricing.InputPricePer1MTokensCents <= 0 {
  502: 			return 0, false
  503: 		}
  504: 		return pricing.InputPricePer1MTokensCents, true
  505: 
  506: 	case domain.EndpointImagesGeneration:
  507: 		if pricing.ImageGenerationPricePerUnitCents <= 0 ||
  508: 			pricing.ImageGenerationUnitKind !=
  509: 				domain.ImageGenerationUnitKindGeneratedImage {
  510: 			return 0, false
  511: 		}
  512: 		return pricing.ImageGenerationPricePerUnitCents, true
  513: 
  514: 	default:
  515: 		return 0, false
  516: 	}
  517: }
  518: 
  519: func safeAdd(left, right int64) (int64, bool) {
  520: 	if left < 0 || right < 0 ||
  521: 		left > math.MaxInt64-right {
  522: 		return 0, false
  523: 	}
  524: 	return left + right, true
  525: }
  526: 
  527: func endpointCapabilityPresent(
  528: 	route domain.Route,
  529: ) bool {
  530: 	switch route.EndpointKind {
  531: 	case domain.EndpointChat:
  532: 		return route.Capabilities.Chat
  533: 	case domain.EndpointEmbeddings:
  534: 		return route.Capabilities.Embeddings
  535: 	case domain.EndpointImagesGeneration:
  536: 		return route.Capabilities.ImagesGeneration
  537: 	default:
  538: 		return false
  539: 	}
  540: }
  541: 
  542: func unionCapabilities(
  543: 	left domain.CapabilitySet,
  544: 	right domain.CapabilitySet,
  545: ) domain.CapabilitySet {
  546: 	return domain.CapabilitySet{
  547: 		Chat: left.Chat || right.Chat,
  548: 		Embeddings: left.Embeddings ||
  549: 			right.Embeddings,
  550: 		ImagesGeneration: left.ImagesGeneration ||
  551: 			right.ImagesGeneration,
  552: 		Tools: left.Tools || right.Tools,
  553: 		ToolChoice: left.ToolChoice ||
  554: 			right.ToolChoice,
  555: 		ResponseFormat: left.ResponseFormat ||
  556: 			right.ResponseFormat,
  557: 		JSONSchema: left.JSONSchema ||
  558: 			right.JSONSchema,
  559: 		ImageInput: left.ImageInput ||
  560: 			right.ImageInput,
  561: 		AudioInput: left.AudioInput ||
  562: 			right.AudioInput,
  563: 		FileInput: left.FileInput ||
  564: 			right.FileInput,
  565: 		VideoInput: left.VideoInput ||
  566: 			right.VideoInput,
  567: 		Reasoning: left.Reasoning ||
  568: 			right.Reasoning,
  569: 	}
  570: }
  571: 
  572: func validateRouteRecord(
  573: 	route domain.Route,
  574: 	apiFamily domain.APIFamily,
  575: ) error {
  576: 	if !validOpaque(route.ID) ||
  577: 		!validOpaque(route.ResellerID) ||
  578: 		!validOpaque(route.ClientModel) ||
  579: 		!validOpaque(route.ProviderModel) ||
  580: 		!validProviderType(route.ProviderType) ||
  581: 		route.APIFamily != apiFamily ||
  582: 		!validEndpointKind(route.EndpointKind) ||
  583: 		!validRewritePolicy(route.ModelRewritePolicy) ||
  584: 		route.Priority < 0 ||
  585: 		route.RequestsPerMinute < 0 ||
  586: 		route.TokensPerMinute < 0 ||
  587: 		route.ConcurrentRequests < 0 ||
  588: 		route.DefaultMaxOutputTokens < 0 ||
  589: 		route.Enabled != (route.DisabledAt == nil) ||
  590: 		!validOptionalUTC(route.DisabledAt) ||
  591: 		!validOptionalUTC(route.CooldownUntil) ||
  592: 		!validCooldownState(route) {
  593: 		return ErrCatalogUnavailable
  594: 	}
  595: 	return nil
  596: }
  597: 
  598: func validateResellerRecord(
  599: 	reseller domain.Reseller,
  600: 	route domain.Route,
  601: ) error {
  602: 	if reseller.ID != route.ResellerID ||
  603: 		!validOpaque(reseller.ID) ||
  604: 		!validOpaque(reseller.BaseURL) ||
  605: 		!validOpaque(reseller.APIKeyEnv) ||
  606: 		!validProviderType(reseller.ProviderType) ||
  607: 		reseller.ProviderType != route.ProviderType ||
  608: 		reseller.ReservedCents < 0 ||
  609: 		reseller.MinimumBalanceCents < 0 ||
  610: 		reseller.Enabled != (reseller.DisabledAt == nil) ||
  611: 		!validOptionalUTC(reseller.DisabledAt) {
  612: 		return ErrCatalogUnavailable
  613: 	}
  614: 	return nil
  615: }
  616: 
  617: func validatePriceRecord(
  618: 	price domain.RoutePrice,
  619: 	routeID string,
  620: ) error {
  621: 	values := []int64{
  622: 		price.InputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  623: 		price.CachedInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  624: 		price.OutputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  625: 		price.ReasoningOutputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  626: 		price.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  627: 		price.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  628: 		price.AudioOutputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  629: 		price.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  630: 		price.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents,
  631: 		price.ImageGenerationPricePerUnitCents,
  632: 	}
  633: 	for _, value := range values {
  634: 		if value < 0 {
  635: 			return ErrCatalogUnavailable
  636: 		}
  637: 	}
  638: 
  639: 	if price.RouteID != routeID ||
  640: 		!validOpaque(price.RouteID) ||
  641: 		!validOpaque(price.Currency) ||
  642: 		price.MarkupCoefficient <= 0 ||
  643: 		math.IsNaN(price.MarkupCoefficient) ||
  644: 		math.IsInf(price.MarkupCoefficient, 0) ||
  645: 		!validImageGenerationUnitKind(
  646: 			price.ImageGenerationUnitKind,
  647: 		) {
  648: 		return ErrCatalogUnavailable
  649: 	}
  650: 	return nil
  651: }
  652: 
  653: func validateReturnedResellers(
  654: 	values map[string]domain.Reseller,
  655: 	requested []string,
  656: ) error {
  657: 	allowed := make(map[string]struct{}, len(requested))
  658: 	for _, id := range requested {
  659: 		allowed[id] = struct{}{}
  660: 	}
  661: 	for id := range values {
  662: 		if _, exists := allowed[id]; !exists {
  663: 			return ErrCatalogUnavailable
  664: 		}
  665: 	}
  666: 	return nil
  667: }
  668: 
  669: func validateReturnedPrices(
  670: 	values map[string]domain.RoutePrice,
  671: 	requested []string,
  672: ) error {
  673: 	allowed := make(map[string]struct{}, len(requested))
  674: 	for _, id := range requested {
  675: 		allowed[id] = struct{}{}
  676: 	}
  677: 	for id := range values {
  678: 		if _, exists := allowed[id]; !exists {
  679: 			return ErrCatalogUnavailable
  680: 		}
  681: 	}
  682: 	return nil
  683: }
  684: 
  685: func validOpaque(value string) bool {
  686: 	return value != "" &&
  687: 		value == strings.TrimSpace(value)
  688: }
  689: 
  690: func validAPIFamily(value domain.APIFamily) bool {
  691: 	switch value {
  692: 	case domain.APIFamilyOpenAICompatible,
  693: 		domain.APIFamilyGeminiNative,
  694: 		domain.APIFamilyAnthropicNative,
  695: 		domain.APIFamilyOllamaNative:
  696: 		return true
  697: 	default:
  698: 		return false
  699: 	}
  700: }
  701: 
  702: func validProviderType(value domain.ProviderType) bool {
  703: 	switch value {
  704: 	case domain.ProviderOpenAI,
  705: 		domain.ProviderOpenRouter,
  706: 		domain.ProviderTogether,
  707: 		domain.ProviderGroq,
  708: 		domain.ProviderOllama,
  709: 		domain.ProviderLMStudio,
  710: 		domain.ProviderVLLM,
  711: 		domain.ProviderGemini,
  712: 		domain.ProviderAnthropic,
  713: 		domain.ProviderHydra:
  714: 		return true
  715: 	default:
  716: 		return false
  717: 	}
  718: }
  719: 
  720: func validEndpointKind(value domain.EndpointKind) bool {
  721: 	switch value {
  722: 	case domain.EndpointChat,
  723: 		domain.EndpointEmbeddings,
  724: 		domain.EndpointImagesGeneration:
  725: 		return true
  726: 	default:
  727: 		return false
  728: 	}
  729: }
  730: 
  731: func validRewritePolicy(
  732: 	value domain.ModelRewritePolicy,
  733: ) bool {
  734: 	switch value {
  735: 	case domain.ModelRewritePolicyNone,
  736: 		domain.ModelRewritePolicyProviderModel:
  737: 		return true
  738: 	default:
  739: 		return false
  740: 	}
  741: }
  742: 
  743: func validImageGenerationUnitKind(
  744: 	value domain.ImageGenerationUnitKind,
  745: ) bool {
  746: 	switch value {
  747: 	case domain.ImageGenerationUnitKindNone,
  748: 		domain.ImageGenerationUnitKindGeneratedImage:
  749: 		return true
  750: 	default:
  751: 		return false
  752: 	}
  753: }
  754: 
  755: func validOptionalUTC(value *time.Time) bool {
  756: 	return value == nil ||
  757: 		(!value.IsZero() && value.Location() == time.UTC)
  758: }
  759: 
  760: func validCooldownState(route domain.Route) bool {
  761: 	if route.CooldownUntil == nil {
  762: 		return route.CooldownReason == ""
  763: 	}
  764: 	return validOpaque(route.CooldownReason)
  765: }
  766: 
  767: func mapDependencyError(err error) error {
  768: 	if err == nil {
  769: 		return nil
  770: 	}
  771: 	if errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) ||
  772: 		errors.Is(err, context.DeadlineExceeded) {
  773: 		return err
  774: 	}
  775: 	return ErrCatalogUnavailable
  776: }

  299: 	}

  303: 		catalog.Data[0].ID != "aaa-inactive" ||
  304: 		catalog.Data[1].ID != "gpt-test" {
  305: 		t.Fatalf("catalog = %+v", catalog)
  306: 	}
  307: 
  308: 	inactive := catalog.Data[0]
  309: 	if inactive.Active ||
  310: 		inactive.Pricing != nil ||
  311: 		inactive.Capabilities !=
  312: 			(domain.CapabilitySet{}) {
  313: 		t.Fatalf("inactive model = %+v", inactive)
  314: 	}
  315:

  317: 	if !active.Active ||
  318: 		active.Object != "model" ||
  319: 		active.OwnedBy != "tokenio" ||
  320: 		active.Type != "chat" ||
  321: 		active.Pricing == nil ||

  323: 		active.Pricing.OutputPricePer1MTokensCents != 300 ||
  324: 		!active.Capabilities.Chat ||
  325: 		!active.Capabilities.Tools ||
  326: 		!active.Capabilities.ImageInput {
  327: 		t.Fatalf("active model = %+v", active)
  328: 	}
  329: 
  330: 	if secrets.calls["EXPENSIVE_KEY"] != 1 ||
  331: 		secrets.calls["SELECTED_KEY"] != 1 ||
  332: 		secrets.calls["INACTIVE_KEY"] != 0 {
  333: 		t.Fatalf("secret calls = %+v", secrets.calls)
  334: 	}
  335: 
  336: 	encoded, err := json.Marshal(catalog)
  337: 	if err != nil {
  338: 		t.Fatalf("Marshal: %v", err)
  339: 	}
  340: 	response := string(encoded)
  341: 	for _, forbidden := range []string{
  342: 		"route_id",
  343: 		"reseller_id",
  344: 		"provider_model",
  345: 		"provider_type",
  346: 		"api_key_env",
  347: 		"markup_coefficient",
  348: 		"cooldown_reason",
  349: 		"priority",
  350: 	} {
  351: 		if strings.Contains(response, forbidden) {
  352: 			t.Fatalf(
  353: 				"catalog leaked %q: %s",
  354: 				forbidden,
  355: 				response,
  356: 			)
  357: 		}
  358: 	}

  431: 		pricing.InputPricePer1MTokensCents != 200 ||

  681: func TestApplyMarkupIsCeilingAndRejectsOverflow(
  682: 	t *testing.T,
  683: ) {

  685: 	if err != nil || value != 152 {
  686: 		t.Fatalf("value=%d error=%v", value, err)
  687: 	}
  688: 
  689: 	decimalValue, err := applyMarkup(100, 1.1)
  690: 	if err != nil || decimalValue != 110 {
  691: 		t.Fatalf(
  692: 			"decimal value=%d error=%v",
  693: 			decimalValue,
  694: 			err,
  695: 		)
  696: 	}
  697: 
  698: 	_, err = applyMarkup(math.MaxInt64, 2)
  699: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrCatalogUnavailable) {
  700: 		t.Fatalf(
  701: 			"overflow error = %v",
  702: 			err,
  703: 		)
  704: 	}
  705: }
