   12: const microCentsPerCent int64 = 1_000_000
   13: 
   14: var maxInt64Big = big.NewInt(math.MaxInt64)
   15: 
   16: type Calculator struct {
   17: 	tokenSafetyFactor *big.Rat
   18: 	costSafetyFactor  *big.Rat
   19: }
   20: 
   21: type ActualCalculationInput struct {
   22: 	Usage      domain.TokenUsage
   23: 	Price      domain.RoutePrice
   24: 	InputMode  InputPricingMode
   25: 	Modalities InputModalities
   26: }
   27: 
   28: type EstimateCalculationInput struct {
   29: 	Usage      domain.TokenUsage
   30: 	Price      domain.RoutePrice
   31: 	InputMode  InputPricingMode
   32: 	Modalities InputModalities
   33: }
   34: 
   35: type MixedCalculationInput struct {
   36: 	ActualUsage    domain.TokenUsage
   37: 	EstimatedUsage domain.TokenUsage
   38: 	Price          domain.RoutePrice
   39: 
   40: 	ActualInputMode    InputPricingMode
   41: 	EstimatedInputMode InputPricingMode
   42: 	Modalities         InputModalities
   43: }
   44: 
   45: type CalculationResult struct {
   46: 	Usage domain.TokenUsage
   47: 
   48: 	UpstreamCostCents int64
   49: 	ClientAmountCents int64
   50: 	Currency          string
   51: 
   52: 	Estimated bool
   53: }
   54: 
   55: func NewCalculator(tokenSafetyFactor float64, costSafetyFactor float64) (*Calculator, error) {
   56: 	token, err := positiveFiniteRat(tokenSafetyFactor, "token safety factor")
   57: 	if err != nil {
   58: 		return nil, err
   59: 	}
   60: 	cost, err := positiveFiniteRat(costSafetyFactor, "cost safety factor")
   61: 	if err != nil {
   62: 		return nil, err
   63: 	}
   64: 	return &Calculator{tokenSafetyFactor: token, costSafetyFactor: cost}, nil
   65: }
   66: 
   67: func (c *Calculator) CalculateActual(input ActualCalculationInput) (CalculationResult, error) {
   68: 	if c == nil {
   69: 		return CalculationResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil calculator", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   70: 	}
   71: 	return c.calculate(input.Usage, input.Price, input.InputMode, input.Modalities, false)
   72: }
   73: 
   74: func (c *Calculator) CalculateEstimate(input EstimateCalculationInput) (CalculationResult, error) {
   75: 	if c == nil {
   76: 		return CalculationResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil calculator", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   77: 	}
   78: 	usage, err := applyTokenSafetyFactor(input.Usage, c.tokenSafetyFactor)
   79: 	if err != nil {
   80: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
   81: 	}
   82: 	return c.calculate(usage, input.Price, input.InputMode, input.Modalities, true)
   83: }
   84: 
   85: func (c *Calculator) CalculateMixed(
   86: 	input MixedCalculationInput,
   87: ) (CalculationResult, error) {
   88: 	if c == nil {
   89: 		return CalculationResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
   90: 			"%w: nil calculator",
   91: 			ErrInvalidPricingInput,
   92: 		)
   93: 	}
   94: 	if err := ValidateUsage(input.ActualUsage); err != nil {
   95: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
   96: 	}
   97: 	if err := ValidateUsage(input.EstimatedUsage); err != nil {
   98: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
   99: 	}
  100: 	if err := ValidateRoutePrice(input.Price); err != nil {
  101: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  102: 	}
  103: 	estimatedUsage, err := applyTokenSafetyFactor(
  104: 		input.EstimatedUsage,
  105: 		c.tokenSafetyFactor,
  106: 	)
  107: 	if err != nil {
  108: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  109: 	}
  110: 	actualRaw, err := rawCostBasis(
  111: 		input.ActualUsage,
  112: 		input.Price,
  113: 		input.ActualInputMode,
  114: 		input.Modalities,
  115: 	)
  116: 	if err != nil {
  117: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  118: 	}
  119: 	estimatedRaw, err := rawCostBasis(
  120: 		estimatedUsage,
  121: 		input.Price,
  122: 		input.EstimatedInputMode,
  123: 		input.Modalities,
  124: 	)
  125: 	if err != nil {
  126: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  127: 	}
  128: 	usage, err := addUsage(input.ActualUsage, estimatedUsage)
  129: 	if err != nil {
  130: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  131: 	}
  132: 	markup, err := markupRat(input.Price.MarkupCoefficient)
  133: 	if err != nil {
  134: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  135: 	}
  136: 	totalRaw := new(big.Rat).SetInt64(actualRaw)
  137: 	totalRaw.Add(
  138: 		totalRaw,
  139: 		new(big.Rat).Mul(
  140: 			new(big.Rat).SetInt64(estimatedRaw),
  141: 			c.costSafetyFactor,
  142: 		),
  143: 	)
  144: 	upstream, err := ceilRawRatCents(totalRaw)
  145: 	if err != nil {
  146: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  147: 	}
  148: 	client, err := ceilRawRatCents(
  149: 		new(big.Rat).Mul(totalRaw, markup),
  150: 	)
  151: 	if err != nil {
  152: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  153: 	}
  154: 	return CalculationResult{
  155: 		Usage:             usage,
  156: 		UpstreamCostCents: upstream,
  157: 		ClientAmountCents: client,
  158: 		Currency:          input.Price.Currency,
  159: 		Estimated:         true,
  160: 	}, nil
  161: }
  162: 
  163: func (c *Calculator) calculate(usage domain.TokenUsage, price domain.RoutePrice, mode InputPricingMode, modalities InputModalities, estimated bool) (CalculationResult, error) {
  164: 	if err := ValidateUsage(usage); err != nil {
  165: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  166: 	}
  167: 	if err := ValidateRoutePrice(price); err != nil {
  168: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  169: 	}
  170: 	raw, err := rawCostBasis(usage, price, mode, modalities)
  171: 	if err != nil {
  172: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  173: 	}
  174: 	markup, err := markupRat(price.MarkupCoefficient)
  175: 	if err != nil {
  176: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  177: 	}
  178: 	costFactor := big.NewRat(1, 1)
  179: 	if estimated {
  180: 		costFactor = c.costSafetyFactor
  181: 	}
  182: 	upstream, err := ceilRawCents(raw, costFactor)
  183: 	if err != nil {
  184: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  185: 	}
  186: 	clientFactor := new(big.Rat).Mul(costFactor, markup)
  187: 	client, err := ceilRawCents(raw, clientFactor)
  188: 	if err != nil {
  189: 		return CalculationResult{}, err
  190: 	}
  191: 	return CalculationResult{Usage: usage, UpstreamCostCents: upstream, ClientAmountCents: client, Currency: price.Currency, Estimated: estimated}, nil
  192: }
  193: 
  194: func ValidateRoutePrice(price domain.RoutePrice) error {
  195: 	if price.RouteID == "" {
  196: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: route id is empty", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
  197: 	}
  198: 	if price.Currency != "RUB" {
  199: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: %q", ErrUnsupportedCurrency, price.Currency)
  200: 	}
  201: 	fields := []struct {
  202: 		name  string
  203: 		value int64
  204: 	}{
  205: 		{"input price", price.InputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  206: 		{"cached input price", price.CachedInputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  207: 		{"output price", price.OutputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  208: 		{"reasoning price", price.ReasoningOutputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  209: 		{"image input price", price.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  210: 		{"audio input price", price.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  211: 		{"audio output price", price.AudioOutputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  212: 		{"file input price", price.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  213: 		{"video input price", price.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents},
  214: 		{"image generation price", price.ImageGenerationPricePerUnitCents},
  215: 	}
  216: 	for _, field := range fields {
  217: 		if field.value < 0 {
  218: 			return fmt.Errorf("%w: %s is negative", ErrInvalidPricingInput, field.name)
  219: 		}
  220: 	}
  221: 	if math.IsNaN(price.MarkupCoefficient) || math.IsInf(price.MarkupCoefficient, 0) || price.MarkupCoefficient <= 0 {
  222: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: invalid markup coefficient", ErrInvalidMarkup)
  223: 	}
  224: 	return nil
  225: }
  226: 
  227: func rawCostBasis(usage domain.TokenUsage, price domain.RoutePrice, mode InputPricingMode, modalities InputModalities) (int64, error) {
  228: 	var total int64
  229: 	addToken := func(count, unitPrice int64, name string) error {
  230: 		if count > 0 && unitPrice == 0 {
  231: 			return fmt.Errorf("%w: %s", ErrMissingPrice, name)
  232: 		}
  233: 		component, err := checkedMul(count, unitPrice)
  234: 		if err != nil {
  235: 			return err
  236: 		}
  237: 		total, err = checkedAdd(total, component)
  238: 		return err
  239: 	}
  240: 	if mode == "" {
  241: 		mode = InputPricingModeDetailed
  242: 	}
  243: 	switch mode {
  244: 	case InputPricingModeDetailed:
  245: 		if err := addToken(usage.InputTokens, price.InputPricePer1MTokensCents, "input tokens"); err != nil {
  246: 			return 0, err
  247: 		}
  248: 		if err := addToken(usage.CachedInputTokens, price.CachedInputPricePer1MTokensCents, "cached input tokens"); err != nil {
  249: 			return 0, err
  250: 		}
  251: 		if err := addToken(usage.ImageInputTokens, price.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents, "image input tokens"); err != nil {
  252: 			return 0, err
  253: 		}
  254: 		if err := addToken(usage.AudioInputTokens, price.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents, "audio input tokens"); err != nil {
  255: 			return 0, err
  256: 		}
  257: 		if err := addToken(usage.FileInputTokens, price.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents, "file input tokens"); err != nil {
  258: 			return 0, err
  259: 		}
  260: 		if err := addToken(usage.VideoInputTokens, price.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents, "video input tokens"); err != nil {
  261: 			return 0, err
  262: 		}
  263: 	case InputPricingModeAggregateMax:
  264: 		if usage.CachedInputTokens != 0 || usage.ImageInputTokens != 0 || usage.AudioInputTokens != 0 || usage.FileInputTokens != 0 || usage.VideoInputTokens != 0 {
  265: 			return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: aggregate input includes breakdown tokens", ErrInvalidUsage)
  266: 		}
  267: 		inputPrice, err := aggregateInputPrice(usage.InputTokens, price, modalities)
  268: 		if err != nil {
  269: 			return 0, err
  270: 		}
  271: 		if err := addToken(usage.InputTokens, inputPrice, "aggregate input tokens"); err != nil {
  272: 			return 0, err
  273: 		}
  274: 	default:
  275: 		return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: input pricing mode", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
  276: 	}
  277: 	if err := addToken(usage.OutputTokens, price.OutputPricePer1MTokensCents, "output tokens"); err != nil {
  278: 		return 0, err
  279: 	}
  280: 	if err := addToken(usage.ReasoningTokens, price.ReasoningOutputPricePer1MTokensCents, "reasoning tokens"); err != nil {
  281: 		return 0, err
  282: 	}
  283: 	if err := addToken(usage.AudioOutputTokens, price.AudioOutputPricePer1MTokensCents, "audio output tokens"); err != nil {
  284: 		return 0, err
  285: 	}
  286: 	if usage.ImageGenerationUnits > 0 {
  287: 		if price.ImageGenerationPricePerUnitCents <= 0 || price.ImageGenerationUnitKind != domain.ImageGenerationUnitKindGeneratedImage {
  288: 			return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: image generation units require generated_image unit price", ErrInvalidImageGenerationPricing)
  289: 		}
  290: 		unitsPrice, err := checkedMul(usage.ImageGenerationUnits, price.ImageGenerationPricePerUnitCents)
  291: 		if err != nil {
  292: 			return 0, err
  293: 		}
  294: 		component, err := checkedMul(unitsPrice, microCentsPerCent)
  295: 		if err != nil {
  296: 			return 0, err
  297: 		}
  298: 		total, err = checkedAdd(total, component)
  299: 		if err != nil {
  300: 			return 0, err
  301: 		}
  302: 	}
  303: 	return total, nil
  304: }
  305: 
  306: func aggregateInputPrice(inputTokens int64, price domain.RoutePrice, modalities InputModalities) (int64, error) {
  307: 	if inputTokens > 0 && price.InputPricePer1MTokensCents == 0 {
  308: 		return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: aggregate text input tokens", ErrMissingPrice)
  309: 	}
  310: 	max := price.InputPricePer1MTokensCents
  311: 	if modalities.Image {
  312: 		if price.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents == 0 {
  313: 			return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: aggregate image input tokens", ErrMissingPrice)
  314: 		}
  315: 		if price.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents > max {
  316: 			max = price.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents
  317: 		}
  318: 	}
  319: 	if modalities.Audio {
  320: 		if price.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents == 0 {
  321: 			return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: aggregate audio input tokens", ErrMissingPrice)
  322: 		}
  323: 		if price.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents > max {
  324: 			max = price.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents
  325: 		}
  326: 	}
  327: 	if modalities.File {
  328: 		if price.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents == 0 {
  329: 			return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: aggregate file input tokens", ErrMissingPrice)
  330: 		}
  331: 		if price.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents > max {
  332: 			max = price.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents
  333: 		}
  334: 	}
  335: 	if modalities.Video {
  336: 		if price.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents == 0 {
  337: 			return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: aggregate video input tokens", ErrMissingPrice)
  338: 		}
  339: 		if price.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents > max {
  340: 			max = price.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents
  341: 		}
  342: 	}
  343: 	return max, nil
  344: }
  345: 
  346: func checkedMul(a, b int64) (int64, error) {
  347: 	if a < 0 || b < 0 {
  348: 		return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: negative operand", ErrAmountOverflow)
  349: 	}
  350: 	product := new(big.Int).Mul(big.NewInt(a), big.NewInt(b))
  351: 	if product.Cmp(maxInt64Big) > 0 {
  352: 		return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: multiplication", ErrAmountOverflow)
  353: 	}
  354: 	return product.Int64(), nil
  355: }
  356: 
  357: func checkedAdd(a, b int64) (int64, error) {
  358: 	sum := new(big.Int).Add(big.NewInt(a), big.NewInt(b))
  359: 	if sum.Cmp(maxInt64Big) > 0 {
  360: 		return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: sum", ErrAmountOverflow)
  361: 	}
  362: 	return sum.Int64(), nil
  363: }
  364: 
  365: func ceilRawCents(raw int64, factor *big.Rat) (int64, error) {
  366: 	if raw == 0 {
  367: 		return 0, nil
  368: 	}
  369: 	r := new(big.Rat).SetInt64(raw)
  370: 	r.Mul(r, factor)
  371: 	return ceilRawRatCents(r)
  372: }
  373: 
  374: func ceilRawRatCents(raw *big.Rat) (int64, error) {
  375: 	if raw == nil || raw.Sign() == 0 {
  376: 		return 0, nil
  377: 	}
  378: 	r := new(big.Rat).Quo(
  379: 		new(big.Rat).Set(raw),
  380: 		big.NewRat(microCentsPerCent, 1),
  381: 	)
  382: 	value := ceilRat(r)
  383: 	if value.Cmp(maxInt64Big) > 0 {
  384: 		return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: final amount", ErrAmountOverflow)
  385: 	}
  386: 	return value.Int64(), nil
  387: }
  388: 
  389: func ceilRat(r *big.Rat) *big.Int {
  390: 	n := new(big.Int).Set(r.Num())
  391: 	d := new(big.Int).Set(r.Denom())
  392: 	q, rem := new(big.Int).QuoRem(n, d, new(big.Int))
  393: 	if rem.Sign() > 0 {
  394: 		q.Add(q, big.NewInt(1))
  395: 	}
  396: 	return q
  397: }
  398: 
  399: func positiveFiniteRat(value float64, name string) (*big.Rat, error) {
  400: 	if value <= 0 || math.IsNaN(value) || math.IsInf(value, 0) {
  401: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w: %s", ErrInvalidPricingInput, name)
  402: 	}
  403: 	return floatToRat(value)
  404: }
  405: 
  406: func markupRat(value float64) (*big.Rat, error) {
  407: 	if value <= 0 || math.IsNaN(value) || math.IsInf(value, 0) {
  408: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w: markup coefficient", ErrInvalidMarkup)
  409: 	}
  410: 	return floatToRat(value)
  411: }
  412: 
  413: func floatToRat(value float64) (*big.Rat, error) {
  414: 	text := strconv.FormatFloat(value, 'f', -1, 64)
  415: 	rat, ok := new(big.Rat).SetString(text)
  416: 	if !ok {
  417: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w: decimal coefficient", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
  418: 	}
  419: 	return rat, nil
  420: }
  421: 
  422: func addUsage(
  423: 	left domain.TokenUsage,
  424: 	right domain.TokenUsage,
  425: ) (domain.TokenUsage, error) {
  426: 	out := left
  427: 	var err error
  428: 	if out.InputTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.InputTokens, right.InputTokens); err != nil {
  429: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  430: 	}
  431: 	if out.CachedInputTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.CachedInputTokens, right.CachedInputTokens); err != nil {
  432: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  433: 	}
  434: 	if out.OutputTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.OutputTokens, right.OutputTokens); err != nil {
  435: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  436: 	}
  437: 	if out.ReasoningTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.ReasoningTokens, right.ReasoningTokens); err != nil {
  438: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  439: 	}
  440: 	if out.ImageInputTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.ImageInputTokens, right.ImageInputTokens); err != nil {
  441: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  442: 	}
  443: 	if out.AudioInputTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.AudioInputTokens, right.AudioInputTokens); err != nil {
  444: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  445: 	}
  446: 	if out.AudioOutputTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.AudioOutputTokens, right.AudioOutputTokens); err != nil {
  447: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  448: 	}
  449: 	if out.FileInputTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.FileInputTokens, right.FileInputTokens); err != nil {
  450: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  451: 	}
  452: 	if out.VideoInputTokens, err = checkedAdd(left.VideoInputTokens, right.VideoInputTokens); err != nil {
  453: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  454: 	}
  455: 	if out.ImageGenerationUnits, err = checkedAdd(left.ImageGenerationUnits, right.ImageGenerationUnits); err != nil {
  456: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  457: 	}
  458: 	return out, nil
  459: }
  460: 
  461: func applyTokenSafetyFactor(usage domain.TokenUsage, factor *big.Rat) (domain.TokenUsage, error) {
  462: 	var err error
  463: 	out := usage
  464: 	if out.InputTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.InputTokens, factor); err != nil {
  465: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  466: 	}
  467: 	if out.CachedInputTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.CachedInputTokens, factor); err != nil {
  468: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  469: 	}
  470: 	if out.OutputTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.OutputTokens, factor); err != nil {
  471: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  472: 	}
  473: 	if out.ReasoningTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.ReasoningTokens, factor); err != nil {
  474: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  475: 	}
  476: 	if out.ImageInputTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.ImageInputTokens, factor); err != nil {
  477: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  478: 	}
  479: 	if out.AudioInputTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.AudioInputTokens, factor); err != nil {
  480: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  481: 	}
  482: 	if out.AudioOutputTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.AudioOutputTokens, factor); err != nil {
  483: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  484: 	}
  485: 	if out.FileInputTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.FileInputTokens, factor); err != nil {
  486: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  487: 	}
  488: 	if out.VideoInputTokens, err = ceilMulRat(usage.VideoInputTokens, factor); err != nil {
  489: 		return domain.TokenUsage{}, err
  490: 	}
  491: 	return out, nil
  492: }
  493: 
  494: func ceilMulRat(value int64, factor *big.Rat) (int64, error) {
  495: 	if value < 0 {
  496: 		return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: token safety factor negative usage", ErrInvalidUsage)
  497: 	}
  498: 	if value == 0 {
  499: 		return 0, nil
  500: 	}
  501: 	r := new(big.Rat).Mul(new(big.Rat).SetInt64(value), factor)
  502: 	ceil := ceilRat(r)
  503: 	if ceil.Cmp(maxInt64Big) > 0 {
  504: 		return 0, fmt.Errorf("%w: token estimate", ErrAmountOverflow)
  505: 	}
  506: 	return ceil.Int64(), nil
  507: }

  172: 		}
  173: 	}

  176: func TestAggregateMaxMode(t *testing.T) {
  177: 	p := testPrice()
  178: 	p.MarkupCoefficient = 1
  179: 	p.InputPricePer1MTokensCents = 100
  180: 	p.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 200
  181: 	p.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 300
  182: 	p.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 400
  183: 	p.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 500
  184: 	cases := []struct {
  185: 		name string
  186: 		m    InputModalities
  187: 		want int64
  188: 	}{{"text", InputModalities{}, 1}, {"image", InputModalities{Image: true}, 2}, {"audio", InputModalities{Audio: true}, 3}, {"file", InputModalities{File: true}, 4}, {"video", InputModalities{Video: true}, 5}, {"audio file", InputModalities{Audio: true, File: true}, 4}, {"absent expensive ignored", InputModalities{Audio: true}, 3}}
  189: 	for _, tt := range cases {
  190: 		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
  191: 			got, err := newTestCalculator(t).CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 10_000}, Price: p, InputMode: InputPricingModeAggregateMax, Modalities: tt.m})
  192: 			if err != nil {
  193: 				t.Fatal(err)
  194: 			}
  195: 			if got.UpstreamCostCents != tt.want {
  196: 				t.Fatalf("got %d want %d", got.UpstreamCostCents, tt.want)
  197: 			}
  198: 		})
  199: 	}
  200: 	for _, usage := range []domain.TokenUsage{{InputTokens: 1, ImageInputTokens: 1}, {InputTokens: 1, CachedInputTokens: 1}} {
  201: 		_, err := newTestCalculator(t).CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: usage, Price: p, InputMode: InputPricingModeAggregateMax})
  202: 		if !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidUsage) {
  203: 			t.Fatalf("err = %v, want ErrInvalidUsage", err)
  204: 		}
  205: 	}
  206: 	got := actual(t, domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 10_000, ImageInputTokens: 10_000}, p)
  207: 	if got.UpstreamCostCents != 3 {
  208: 		t.Fatalf("detailed mode got %d", got.UpstreamCostCents)
  209: 	}
  210: }
  211: 
  212: func TestAggregateMaxModeRequiresPresentModalityPrices(t *testing.T) {
  213: 	p := testPrice()
  214: 	p.MarkupCoefficient = 1
  215: 	p.InputPricePer1MTokensCents = 100
  216: 	p.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 200
  217: 	p.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 300
  218: 	p.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 400
  219: 	p.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 500
  220: 
  221: 	cases := []struct {
  222: 		name     string
  223: 		mutate   func(*domain.RoutePrice)
  224: 		modality InputModalities
  225: 	}{
  226: 		{"text input", func(price *domain.RoutePrice) { price.InputPricePer1MTokensCents = 0 }, InputModalities{}},
  227: 		{"image present", func(price *domain.RoutePrice) { price.ImageInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 0 }, InputModalities{Image: true}},
  228: 		{"audio present", func(price *domain.RoutePrice) { price.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 0 }, InputModalities{Audio: true}},
  229: 		{"file present", func(price *domain.RoutePrice) { price.FileInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 0 }, InputModalities{File: true}},
  230: 		{"video present", func(price *domain.RoutePrice) { price.VideoInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 0 }, InputModalities{Video: true}},
  231: 	}
  232: 	for _, tt := range cases {
  233: 		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
  234: 			price := p
  235: 			tt.mutate(&price)
  236: 			_, err := newTestCalculator(t).CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{
  237: 				Usage:      domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 10_000},
  238: 				Price:      price,
  239: 				InputMode:  InputPricingModeAggregateMax,
  240: 				Modalities: tt.modality,
  241: 			})
  242: 			if !errors.Is(err, ErrMissingPrice) {
  243: 				t.Fatalf("err = %v, want ErrMissingPrice", err)
  244: 			}
  245: 		})
  246: 	}
  247: 
  248: 	absentZeroPrice := p
  249: 	absentZeroPrice.AudioInputPricePer1MTokensCents = 0
  250: 	got, err := newTestCalculator(t).CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{
  251: 		Usage:      domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 10_000},
  252: 		Price:      absentZeroPrice,
  253: 		InputMode:  InputPricingModeAggregateMax,
  254: 		Modalities: InputModalities{File: true},
  255: 	})
  256: 	if err != nil {
  257: 		t.Fatalf("absent zero-priced modality should not be required: %v", err)
  258: 	}
  259: 	if got.UpstreamCostCents != 4 {
  260: 		t.Fatalf("got %d want 4", got.UpstreamCostCents)
  261: 	}
  262: }
  263: 
  264: func TestSafetyFactorsAndOverflow(t *testing.T) {
  265: 	c := newTestCalculator(t)
  266: 	p := testPrice()
  267: 	p.MarkupCoefficient = 2
  268: 	usage := domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 4, CachedInputTokens: 4, OutputTokens: 4, ReasoningTokens: 4, ImageInputTokens: 4, AudioInputTokens: 4, AudioOutputTokens: 4, FileInputTokens: 4, VideoInputTokens: 4, ImageGenerationUnits: 4}
  269: 	original := usage
  270: 	got, err := c.CalculateEstimate(EstimateCalculationInput{Usage: usage, Price: p, InputMode: InputPricingModeDetailed})
  271: 	if err != nil {
  272: 		t.Fatal(err)
  273: 	}
  274: 	wantUsage := domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 5, CachedInputTokens: 5, OutputTokens: 5, ReasoningTokens: 5, ImageInputTokens: 5, AudioInputTokens: 5, AudioOutputTokens: 5, FileInputTokens: 5, VideoInputTokens: 5, ImageGenerationUnits: 4}
  275: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(got.Usage, wantUsage) {
  276: 		t.Fatalf("usage = %+v want %+v", got.Usage, wantUsage)
  277: 	}
  278: 	if got.UpstreamCostCents != 40 || got.ClientAmountCents != 80 {
  279: 		t.Fatalf("estimate amounts got %d/%d", got.UpstreamCostCents, got.ClientAmountCents)
  280: 	}
  281: 	if !reflect.DeepEqual(usage, original) {
  282: 		t.Fatalf("input usage mutated")
  283: 	}
  284: 	actualGot, err := c.CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: usage, Price: p, InputMode: InputPricingModeDetailed})
  285: 	if err != nil {
  286: 		t.Fatal(err)
  287: 	}
  288: 	if actualGot.Usage.InputTokens != 4 {
  289: 		t.Fatalf("actual applied factor")
  290: 	}
  291: 	for _, f := range []float64{0, -1, math.NaN(), math.Inf(1), math.Inf(-1)} {
  292: 		if _, err := NewCalculator(f, 1); !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidPricingInput) {
  293: 			t.Fatalf("token factor %v err %v", f, err)
  294: 		}
  295: 		if _, err := NewCalculator(1, f); !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidPricingInput) {
  296: 			t.Fatalf("cost factor %v err %v", f, err)
  297: 		}
  298: 	}
  299: 	overflowPrice := testPrice()
  300: 	overflowPrice.InputPricePer1MTokensCents = math.MaxInt64
  301: 	_, err = c.CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 2}, Price: overflowPrice})
  302: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrAmountOverflow) {
  303: 		t.Fatalf("mul overflow err %v", err)
  304: 	}
  305: 	sumPrice := testPrice()
  306: 	sumPrice.InputPricePer1MTokensCents = math.MaxInt64
  307: 	sumPrice.OutputPricePer1MTokensCents = 1
  308: 	_, err = c.CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 1, OutputTokens: 1}, Price: sumPrice})
  309: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrAmountOverflow) {
  310: 		t.Fatalf("sum overflow err %v", err)
  311: 	}
  312: 	bigMarkup := testPrice()
  313: 	bigMarkup.MarkupCoefficient = 1e18
  314: 	_, err = c.CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{ImageGenerationUnits: 10}, Price: bigMarkup})
  315: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrAmountOverflow) {
  316: 		t.Fatalf("final overflow err %v", err)
  317: 	}
  318: 	stable := testPrice()
  319: 	stable.MarkupCoefficient = 1.333333333
  320: 	one, _ := c.CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 12345}, Price: stable})
  321: 	two, _ := c.CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 12345}, Price: stable})
  322: 	if one.ClientAmountCents != two.ClientAmountCents {
  323: 		t.Fatalf("non-deterministic fractional markup")
  324: 	}
  325: }

  327: func TestRoutePriceValidation(t *testing.T) {

  341: 		t.Fatalf("price err %v", err)
  342: 	}

GIT_BLOB_SHA: a4167ee16728f92c44316aadd90958957fa41ea5

    1: package pricing
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"fmt"
    6: 	"strings"
    7: 
    8: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
    9: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/ports"
   10: )
   11: 
   12: type PreflightInput struct {
   13: 	Route                 domain.Route
   14: 	Price                 domain.RoutePrice
   15: 	RequestBody           []byte
   16: 	RequestedCapabilities domain.CapabilitySet
   17: 
   18: 	InputMode  InputPricingMode
   19: 	Modalities InputModalities
   20: }
   21: 
   22: type PreflightResult struct {
   23: 	EstimatedUsage domain.TokenUsage
   24: 
   25: 	EstimatedUpstreamCostCents int64
   26: 	EstimatedClientAmountCents int64
   27: 
   28: 	Currency   string
   29: 	Confidence string
   30: }
   31: 
   32: type PreflightPricer struct {
   33: 	estimator  ports.TokenEstimator
   34: 	calculator *Calculator
   35: }
   36: 
   37: func NewPreflightPricer(estimator ports.TokenEstimator, calculator *Calculator) (*PreflightPricer, error) {
   38: 	if estimator == nil {
   39: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil token estimator", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   40: 	}
   41: 	if calculator == nil {
   42: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil calculator", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   43: 	}
   44: 	return &PreflightPricer{estimator: estimator, calculator: calculator}, nil
   45: }
   46: 
   47: func (p *PreflightPricer) Price(ctx context.Context, input PreflightInput) (PreflightResult, error) {
   48: 	if p == nil || p.estimator == nil || p.calculator == nil {
   49: 		return PreflightResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil preflight pricer", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   50: 	}
   51: 	if err := validateRouteAndPrice(input.Route, input.Price); err != nil {
   52: 		return PreflightResult{}, err
   53: 	}
   54: 	if input.RequestBody == nil {
   55: 		return PreflightResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: request body is nil", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   56: 	}
   57: 	estimate, err := p.estimator.Estimate(ctx, ports.TokenEstimateRequest{
   58: 		APIFamily:              input.Route.APIFamily,
   59: 		EndpointKind:           input.Route.EndpointKind,
   60: 		ClientModel:            input.Route.ClientModel,
   61: 		RequestBody:            append([]byte(nil), input.RequestBody...),
   62: 		DefaultMaxOutputTokens: input.Route.DefaultMaxOutputTokens,
   63: 		RequestedCapabilities:  input.RequestedCapabilities,
   64: 	})
   65: 	if err != nil {
   66: 		return PreflightResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: estimate usage: %w", ErrPricingUnavailable, err)
   67: 	}
   68: 	if err := ValidateUsage(estimate.Usage); err != nil {
   69: 		return PreflightResult{}, err
   70: 	}
   71: 	if strings.TrimSpace(estimate.Confidence) == "" {
   72: 		return PreflightResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: estimator confidence is blank", ErrPricingUnavailable)
   73: 	}
   74: 	calculation, err := p.calculator.CalculateEstimate(EstimateCalculationInput{
   75: 		Usage:      estimate.Usage,
   76: 		Price:      input.Price,
   77: 		InputMode:  input.InputMode,
   78: 		Modalities: input.Modalities,
   79: 	})
   80: 	if err != nil {
   81: 		return PreflightResult{}, err
   82: 	}
   83: 	return PreflightResult{
   84: 		EstimatedUsage:             calculation.Usage,
   85: 		EstimatedUpstreamCostCents: calculation.UpstreamCostCents,
   86: 		EstimatedClientAmountCents: calculation.ClientAmountCents,
   87: 		Currency:                   calculation.Currency,
   88: 		Confidence:                 estimate.Confidence,
   89: 	}, nil
   90: }
   91: 
   92: func validateRouteAndPrice(route domain.Route, price domain.RoutePrice) error {
   93: 	if route.ID == "" {
   94: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: route id is empty", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   95: 	}
   96: 	if price.RouteID == "" {
   97: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: price route id is empty", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   98: 	}
   99: 	if price.RouteID != route.ID {
  100: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: price route id mismatch", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
  101: 	}
  102: 	if route.APIFamily == "" {
  103: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: api family is empty", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
  104: 	}
  105: 	if route.EndpointKind == "" {
  106: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: endpoint kind is empty", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
  107: 	}
  108: 	if route.ClientModel == "" {
  109: 		return fmt.Errorf("%w: client model is empty", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
  110: 	}
  111: 	return nil
  112: }

FILE: internal/application/pricing/resolver.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: 40b6562f5579f755d80bc0c5fc4b484179820dc7
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package pricing
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"context"
    5: 	"fmt"
    6: 
    7: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
    8: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/ports"
    9: )
   10: 
   11: type ResolveUsageInput struct {
   12: 	Route        domain.Route
   13: 	Price        domain.RoutePrice
   14: 	RequestBody  []byte
   15: 	ResponseBody []byte
   16: 
   17: 	RequestedCapabilities domain.CapabilitySet
   18: 	Modalities            InputModalities
   19: 
   20: 	ZeroUsageAllowed bool
   21: }
   22: 
   23: type ResolvedUsageResult struct {
   24: 	Usage        domain.TokenUsage
   25: 	Completeness UsageCompleteness
   26: 	Estimated    bool
   27: 
   28: 	UpstreamCostCents int64
   29: 	ClientAmountCents int64
   30: 	Currency          string
   31: 
   32: 	ProviderRequestID     string
   33: 	ProviderResponseModel string
   34: }
   35: 
   36: type UsageResolver struct {
   37: 	extractor  ports.UsageExtractor
   38: 	estimator  ports.TokenEstimator
   39: 	calculator *Calculator
   40: }
   41: 
   42: func NewUsageResolver(extractor ports.UsageExtractor, estimator ports.TokenEstimator, calculator *Calculator) (*UsageResolver, error) {
   43: 	if extractor == nil {
   44: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil usage extractor", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   45: 	}
   46: 	if estimator == nil {
   47: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil token estimator", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   48: 	}
   49: 	if calculator == nil {
   50: 		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil calculator", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   51: 	}
   52: 	return &UsageResolver{extractor: extractor, estimator: estimator, calculator: calculator}, nil
   53: }
   54: 
   55: func (r *UsageResolver) Resolve(ctx context.Context, input ResolveUsageInput) (ResolvedUsageResult, error) {
   56: 	if r == nil || r.extractor == nil || r.estimator == nil || r.calculator == nil {
   57: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: nil usage resolver", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   58: 	}
   59: 	if err := validateRouteAndPrice(input.Route, input.Price); err != nil {
   60: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, err
   61: 	}
   62: 	if input.RequestBody == nil || input.ResponseBody == nil {
   63: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: request or response body is nil", ErrInvalidPricingInput)
   64: 	}
   65: 	extracted, err := r.extractor.Extract(ctx, ports.UsageExtractionRequest{
   66: 		APIFamily:    input.Route.APIFamily,
   67: 		EndpointKind: input.Route.EndpointKind,
   68: 		ClientModel:  input.Route.ClientModel,
   69: 		RequestBody:  append([]byte(nil), input.RequestBody...),
   70: 		ResponseBody: append([]byte(nil), input.ResponseBody...),
   71: 	})
   72: 	if err != nil {
   73: 		return r.estimateFallback(ctx, input, UsageCompletenessEstimated, err)
   74: 	}
   75: 	completeness, err := ParseUsageCompleteness(extracted.Completeness)
   76: 	if err != nil {
   77: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, err
   78: 	}
   79: 	required := requiredUsagePresence(input.Route.EndpointKind)
   80: 	if completeness == UsageCompletenessAggregate &&
   81: 		!presenceContains(extracted.Presence, required) {
   82: 		return r.partialActualResult(
   83: 			ctx,
   84: 			input,
   85: 			extracted,
   86: 			required,
   87: 		)
   88: 	}
   89: 	if IsZeroUsage(extracted.Usage) && !input.ZeroUsageAllowed {
   90: 		return r.estimateFallback(ctx, input, UsageCompletenessEstimated, nil)
   91: 	}
   92: 	switch completeness {
   93: 	case UsageCompletenessDetailed:
   94: 		return r.actualResult(extracted, completeness, input.Price, InputPricingModeDetailed, input.Modalities)
   95: 	case UsageCompletenessAggregate:
   96: 		return r.actualResult(extracted, completeness, input.Price, InputPricingModeAggregateMax, input.Modalities)
   97: 	case UsageCompletenessEstimated:
   98: 		return r.estimatedResult(extracted, completeness, input.Price, input.Modalities)
   99: 	case UsageCompletenessMissing, UsageCompletenessFailed:
  100: 		return r.estimateFallback(ctx, input, UsageCompletenessEstimated, nil)
  101: 	default:
  102: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: %q", ErrInvalidUsageCompleteness, completeness)
  103: 	}
  104: }
  105: 
  106: func (r *UsageResolver) partialActualResult(
  107: 	ctx context.Context,
  108: 	input ResolveUsageInput,
  109: 	extracted ports.UsageExtractionResult,
  110: 	required ports.UsageDimensionPresence,
  111: ) (ResolvedUsageResult, error) {
  112: 	estimate, err := r.estimate(ctx, input)
  113: 	if err != nil {
  114: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, fmt.Errorf(
  115: 			"%w: estimate missing usage: %v",
  116: 			ErrUsageUnresolved,
  117: 			err,
  118: 		)
  119: 	}
  120: 	estimatedUsage := selectMissingRequiredUsage(
  121: 		estimate.Usage,
  122: 		extracted.Presence,
  123: 		required,
  124: 	)
  125: 	calculation, err := r.calculator.CalculateMixed(
  126: 		MixedCalculationInput{
  127: 			ActualUsage:        extracted.Usage,
  128: 			EstimatedUsage:     estimatedUsage,
  129: 			Price:              input.Price,
  130: 			ActualInputMode:    InputPricingModeAggregateMax,
  131: 			EstimatedInputMode: InputPricingModeDetailed,
  132: 			Modalities:         input.Modalities,
  133: 		},
  134: 	)
  135: 	if err != nil {
  136: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, err
  137: 	}
  138: 	return resolvedFromCalculation(
  139: 		calculation,
  140: 		UsageCompletenessAggregate,
  141: 		extracted.ProviderRequestID,
  142: 		extracted.ProviderResponseModel,
  143: 	), nil
  144: }
  145: 
  146: func (r *UsageResolver) actualResult(extracted ports.UsageExtractionResult, completeness UsageCompleteness, price domain.RoutePrice, mode InputPricingMode, modalities InputModalities) (ResolvedUsageResult, error) {
  147: 	calculation, err := r.calculator.CalculateActual(ActualCalculationInput{Usage: extracted.Usage, Price: price, InputMode: mode, Modalities: modalities})
  148: 	if err != nil {
  149: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, err
  150: 	}
  151: 	return resolvedFromCalculation(calculation, completeness, extracted.ProviderRequestID, extracted.ProviderResponseModel), nil
  152: }
  153: 
  154: func (r *UsageResolver) estimatedResult(extracted ports.UsageExtractionResult, completeness UsageCompleteness, price domain.RoutePrice, modalities InputModalities) (ResolvedUsageResult, error) {
  155: 	calculation, err := r.calculator.CalculateEstimate(EstimateCalculationInput{Usage: extracted.Usage, Price: price, InputMode: InputPricingModeDetailed, Modalities: modalities})
  156: 	if err != nil {
  157: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, err
  158: 	}
  159: 	return resolvedFromCalculation(calculation, completeness, extracted.ProviderRequestID, extracted.ProviderResponseModel), nil
  160: }
  161: 
  162: func (r *UsageResolver) estimateFallback(ctx context.Context, input ResolveUsageInput, completeness UsageCompleteness, cause error) (ResolvedUsageResult, error) {
  163: 	estimate, err := r.estimate(ctx, input)
  164: 	if err != nil {
  165: 		if cause != nil {
  166: 			return ResolvedUsageResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: extract usage failed: %w; estimate usage failed: %v", ErrUsageUnresolved, cause, err)
  167: 		}
  168: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, fmt.Errorf("%w: estimate usage failed: %v", ErrUsageUnresolved, err)
  169: 	}
  170: 	calculation, err := r.calculator.CalculateEstimate(EstimateCalculationInput{Usage: estimate.Usage, Price: input.Price, InputMode: InputPricingModeDetailed, Modalities: input.Modalities})
  171: 	if err != nil {
  172: 		return ResolvedUsageResult{}, err
  173: 	}
  174: 	return resolvedFromCalculation(calculation, completeness, "", ""), nil
  175: }
  176: 
  177: func (r *UsageResolver) estimate(
  178: 	ctx context.Context,
  179: 	input ResolveUsageInput,
  180: ) (ports.TokenEstimate, error) {
  181: 	estimate, err := r.estimator.Estimate(ctx, ports.TokenEstimateRequest{
  182: 		APIFamily:              input.Route.APIFamily,
  183: 		EndpointKind:           input.Route.EndpointKind,
  184: 		ClientModel:            input.Route.ClientModel,
  185: 		RequestBody:            append([]byte(nil), input.RequestBody...),
  186: 		DefaultMaxOutputTokens: input.Route.DefaultMaxOutputTokens,
  187: 		RequestedCapabilities:  input.RequestedCapabilities,
  188: 	})
  189: 	if err != nil {
  190: 		return ports.TokenEstimate{}, err
  191: 	}
  192: 	if err := ValidateUsage(estimate.Usage); err != nil {
  193: 		return ports.TokenEstimate{}, err
  194: 	}
  195: 	return estimate, nil
  196: }
  197: 
  198: func requiredUsagePresence(
  199: 	endpoint domain.EndpointKind,
  200: ) ports.UsageDimensionPresence {
  201: 	switch endpoint {
  202: 	case domain.EndpointChat:
  203: 		return ports.UsageDimensionPresence{
  204: 			InputTokens:  true,
  205: 			OutputTokens: true,
  206: 		}
  207: 	case domain.EndpointEmbeddings:
  208: 		return ports.UsageDimensionPresence{
  209: 			InputTokens: true,
  210: 		}
  211: 	case domain.EndpointImagesGeneration:
  212: 		return ports.UsageDimensionPresence{
  213: 			ImageGenerationUnits: true,
  214: 		}
  215: 	default:
  216: 		return ports.UsageDimensionPresence{}
  217: 	}
  218: }
  219: 
  220: func presenceContains(
  221: 	actual ports.UsageDimensionPresence,
  222: 	required ports.UsageDimensionPresence,
  223: ) bool {
  224: 	return (!required.InputTokens || actual.InputTokens) &&
  225: 		(!required.CachedInputTokens || actual.CachedInputTokens) &&
  226: 		(!required.OutputTokens || actual.OutputTokens) &&
  227: 		(!required.ReasoningTokens || actual.ReasoningTokens) &&
  228: 		(!required.ImageInputTokens || actual.ImageInputTokens) &&
  229: 		(!required.AudioInputTokens || actual.AudioInputTokens) &&
  230: 		(!required.AudioOutputTokens || actual.AudioOutputTokens) &&
  231: 		(!required.FileInputTokens || actual.FileInputTokens) &&
  232: 		(!required.VideoInputTokens || actual.VideoInputTokens) &&
  233: 		(!required.ImageGenerationUnits || actual.ImageGenerationUnits)
  234: }
  235: 
  236: func selectMissingRequiredUsage(
  237: 	estimate domain.TokenUsage,
  238: 	actual ports.UsageDimensionPresence,
  239: 	required ports.UsageDimensionPresence,
  240: ) domain.TokenUsage {
  241: 	var selected domain.TokenUsage
  242: 	if required.InputTokens && !actual.InputTokens {
  243: 		selected.InputTokens = estimate.InputTokens
  244: 	}
  245: 	if required.CachedInputTokens && !actual.CachedInputTokens {
  246: 		selected.CachedInputTokens = estimate.CachedInputTokens
  247: 	}
  248: 	if required.OutputTokens && !actual.OutputTokens {
  249: 		selected.OutputTokens = estimate.OutputTokens
  250: 	}
  251: 	if required.ReasoningTokens && !actual.ReasoningTokens {
  252: 		selected.ReasoningTokens = estimate.ReasoningTokens
  253: 	}
  254: 	if required.ImageInputTokens && !actual.ImageInputTokens {
  255: 		selected.ImageInputTokens = estimate.ImageInputTokens
  256: 	}
  257: 	if required.AudioInputTokens && !actual.AudioInputTokens {
  258: 		selected.AudioInputTokens = estimate.AudioInputTokens
  259: 	}
  260: 	if required.AudioOutputTokens && !actual.AudioOutputTokens {
  261: 		selected.AudioOutputTokens = estimate.AudioOutputTokens
  262: 	}
  263: 	if required.FileInputTokens && !actual.FileInputTokens {
  264: 		selected.FileInputTokens = estimate.FileInputTokens
  265: 	}
  266: 	if required.VideoInputTokens && !actual.VideoInputTokens {
  267: 		selected.VideoInputTokens = estimate.VideoInputTokens
  268: 	}
  269: 	if required.ImageGenerationUnits && !actual.ImageGenerationUnits {
  270: 		selected.ImageGenerationUnits = estimate.ImageGenerationUnits
  271: 	}
  272: 	return selected
  273: }
  274: 
  275: func resolvedFromCalculation(calculation CalculationResult, completeness UsageCompleteness, requestID, responseModel string) ResolvedUsageResult {
  276: 	return ResolvedUsageResult{
  277: 		Usage:                 calculation.Usage,
  278: 		Completeness:          completeness,
  279: 		Estimated:             calculation.Estimated,
  280: 		UpstreamCostCents:     calculation.UpstreamCostCents,
  281: 		ClientAmountCents:     calculation.ClientAmountCents,
  282: 		Currency:              calculation.Currency,
  283: 		ProviderRequestID:     requestID,
  284: 		ProviderResponseModel: responseModel,
  285: 	}
  286: }

   15: type fakeExtractor struct {
   16: 	result  ports.UsageExtractionResult
   17: 	err     error

   22: 
   23: func (f *fakeExtractor) Extract(_ context.Context, request ports.UsageExtractionRequest) (ports.UsageExtractionResult, error) {
   24: 	f.calls++
   25: 	f.request = request
   26: 	if f.mutate {
   27: 		if len(request.RequestBody) > 0 {
   28: 			request.RequestBody[0] = 'X'
   29: 		}
   30: 		if len(request.ResponseBody) > 0 {
   31: 			request.ResponseBody[0] = 'Y'
   32: 		}
   33: 	}
   34: 	if f.err != nil {
   35: 		return ports.UsageExtractionResult{}, f.err
   36: 	}
   37: 	return f.result, nil
   38: }

   44: 		t.Fatal(err)

   46: 	return r

   49: func TestUsageResolverCompletenessPriority(t *testing.T) {
   50: 	price := testPrice()
   51: 	route := testRoute()
   52: 	input := ResolveUsageInput{Route: route, Price: price, RequestBody: []byte(`{"prompt":"secret-body"}`), ResponseBody: []byte(`{"usage":"secret-body"}`), Modalities: InputModalities{Audio: true}}
   53: 	cases := []struct {
   54: 		name, completeness string
   55: 		usage              domain.TokenUsage
   56: 		estimated          bool
   57: 		wantCompleteness   UsageCompleteness
   58: 		wantUpstream       int64
   59: 		estimatorCalls     int
   60: 	}{
   61: 		{"detailed", "detailed", domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 10_000}, false, UsageCompletenessDetailed, 1, 0},
   62: 		{"aggregate", "aggregate", domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 10_000}, false, UsageCompletenessAggregate, 5, 0},
   63: 		{"estimated", "estimated", domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 10_000}, true, UsageCompletenessEstimated, 2, 0},
   64: 		{"missing", "missing", domain.TokenUsage{}, true, UsageCompletenessEstimated, 2, 1},
   65: 		{"failed", "failed", domain.TokenUsage{}, true, UsageCompletenessEstimated, 2, 1},
   66: 	}
   67: 	for _, tt := range cases {
   68: 		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   69: 			presence := ports.UsageDimensionPresence{}
   70: 			if tt.completeness == "detailed" ||
   71: 				tt.completeness == "aggregate" {
   72: 				presence.InputTokens = true
   73: 				presence.OutputTokens = true
   74: 			}
   75: 			extractor := &fakeExtractor{result: ports.UsageExtractionResult{Usage: tt.usage, Presence: presence, Completeness: tt.completeness, ProviderRequestID: "req-1", ProviderResponseModel: "response-model"}}
   76: 			estimator := &fakeEstimator{estimate: ports.TokenEstimate{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 10_000}, Confidence: "ok"}}
   77: 			result, err := newResolver(t, extractor, estimator).Resolve(context.Background(), input)
   78: 			if err != nil {
   79: 				t.Fatalf("Resolve error: %v", err)
   80: 			}
   81: 			if result.Estimated != tt.estimated || result.Completeness != tt.wantCompleteness || result.UpstreamCostCents != tt.wantUpstream || estimator.calls != tt.estimatorCalls {
   82: 				t.Fatalf("result %+v estimator calls %d", result, estimator.calls)
   83: 			}
   84: 			if tt.estimatorCalls == 0 && (result.ProviderRequestID != "req-1" || result.ProviderResponseModel != "response-model") {
   85: 				t.Fatalf("metadata not preserved: %+v", result)
   86: 			}
   87: 		})
   88: 	}
   89: }

  270: 		t.Fatalf("fakes did not mutate copies")
  271: 	}

  273: 		t.Fatalf("secret leaked in resolver result")

  284: 	result, err = newResolver(t, extractor, estimator).Resolve(context.Background(), input)
  285: 	if err != nil || result.Estimated || result.UpstreamCostCents != 0 || estimator.calls != 0 {
  286: 		t.Fatalf("zero allowed result %+v err %v", result, err)
  287: 	}

  290: func TestUsageResolverErrors(t *testing.T) {
  291: 	input := ResolveUsageInput{Route: testRoute(), Price: testPrice(), RequestBody: []byte("raw-secret"), ResponseBody: []byte("raw-secret")}
  292: 	estimatorFail := &fakeEstimator{err: errors.New("estimate failed")}
  293: 	_, err := newResolver(t, &fakeExtractor{err: errors.New("extract failed")}, estimatorFail).Resolve(context.Background(), input)
  294: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrUsageUnresolved) {
  295: 		t.Fatalf("err %v", err)
  296: 	}
  297: 	if bytes.Contains([]byte(err.Error()), []byte("raw-secret")) {
  298: 		t.Fatalf("raw body leaked: %v", err)
  299: 	}
  300: 	_, err = newResolver(t, &fakeExtractor{result: ports.UsageExtractionResult{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: -1}, Completeness: "detailed"}}, &fakeEstimator{estimate: ports.TokenEstimate{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 1}, Confidence: "ok"}}).Resolve(context.Background(), input)
  301: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidUsage) {
  302: 		t.Fatalf("negative usage err %v", err)
  303: 	}
  304: 	_, err = newResolver(t, &fakeExtractor{result: ports.UsageExtractionResult{Usage: domain.TokenUsage{InputTokens: 1}, Completeness: "unknown"}}, &fakeEstimator{}).Resolve(context.Background(), input)
  305: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidUsageCompleteness) {
  306: 		t.Fatalf("unknown completeness err %v", err)
  307: 	}
  308: 	_, err = NewUsageResolver(nil, &fakeEstimator{}, newTestCalculator(t))
  309: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidPricingInput) {
  310: 		t.Fatalf("nil extractor err %v", err)
  311: 	}
  312: 	_, err = NewUsageResolver(&fakeExtractor{}, nil, newTestCalculator(t))
  313: 	if !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidPricingInput) {
  314: 		t.Fatalf("nil estimator err %v", err)
  315: 	}
  316: }
  317: 
  318: func containsSecret(v any, secret string) bool {
  319: 	return bytes.Contains([]byte(fmt.Sprintf("%+v", v)), []byte(secret))
  320: }

FILE: internal/application/pricing/usage.go
GIT_BLOB_SHA: 00b05e1abeaf588356caef6d1b606e7adffe847e
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    1: package pricing
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"fmt"
    5: 
    6: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"
    7: )
    8: 
    9: type UsageCompleteness string
   10: 
   11: const (
   12: 	UsageCompletenessDetailed  UsageCompleteness = "detailed"
   13: 	UsageCompletenessAggregate UsageCompleteness = "aggregate"
   14: 	UsageCompletenessEstimated UsageCompleteness = "estimated"
   15: 	UsageCompletenessMissing   UsageCompleteness = "missing"
   16: 	UsageCompletenessFailed    UsageCompleteness = "failed"
   17: )
   18: 
   19: func ParseUsageCompleteness(value string) (UsageCompleteness, error) {
   20: 	switch UsageCompleteness(value) {
   21: 	case UsageCompletenessDetailed, UsageCompletenessAggregate, UsageCompletenessEstimated, UsageCompletenessMissing, UsageCompletenessFailed:
   22: 		return UsageCompleteness(value), nil
   23: 	default:
   24: 		return "", fmt.Errorf("%w: %q", ErrInvalidUsageCompleteness, value)
   25: 	}
   26: }
   27: 
   28: func ValidateUsage(usage domain.TokenUsage) error {
   29: 	fields := []struct {
   30: 		name  string
   31: 		value int64
   32: 	}{
   33: 		{"input_tokens", usage.InputTokens},
   34: 		{"cached_input_tokens", usage.CachedInputTokens},
   35: 		{"output_tokens", usage.OutputTokens},
   36: 		{"reasoning_tokens", usage.ReasoningTokens},
   37: 		{"image_input_tokens", usage.ImageInputTokens},
   38: 		{"audio_input_tokens", usage.AudioInputTokens},
   39: 		{"audio_output_tokens", usage.AudioOutputTokens},
   40: 		{"file_input_tokens", usage.FileInputTokens},
   41: 		{"video_input_tokens", usage.VideoInputTokens},
   42: 		{"image_generation_units", usage.ImageGenerationUnits},
   43: 	}
   44: 	for _, field := range fields {
   45: 		if field.value < 0 {
   46: 			return fmt.Errorf("%w: %s is negative", ErrInvalidUsage, field.name)
   47: 		}
   48: 	}
   49: 	return nil
   50: }
   51: 
   52: func IsZeroUsage(usage domain.TokenUsage) bool {
   53: 	return usage.InputTokens == 0 &&
   54: 		usage.CachedInputTokens == 0 &&
   55: 		usage.OutputTokens == 0 &&
   56: 		usage.ReasoningTokens == 0 &&
   57: 		usage.ImageInputTokens == 0 &&
   58: 		usage.AudioInputTokens == 0 &&
   59: 		usage.AudioOutputTokens == 0 &&
   60: 		usage.FileInputTokens == 0 &&
   61: 		usage.VideoInputTokens == 0 &&
   62: 		usage.ImageGenerationUnits == 0
   63: }
   64: 
   65: type InputModalities struct {
   66: 	Image bool
   67: 	Audio bool
   68: 	File  bool
   69: 	Video bool
   70: }
   71: 
   72: type InputPricingMode string
   73: 
   74: const (
   75: 	InputPricingModeDetailed     InputPricingMode = "detailed"
   76: 	InputPricingModeAggregateMax InputPricingMode = "aggregate_max"
   77: )

    1: package pricing
    2: 
    3: import (
    4: 	"errors"

    7: 
    8: 	"github.com/bogachenko/tokenio-gateway/internal/domain"

   10: 
   11: func TestValidateUsage(t *testing.T) {
   12: 	if err := ValidateUsage(domain.TokenUsage{}); err != nil {
   13: 		t.Fatalf("zero usage invalid: %v", err)
   14: 	}
   15: 	positive := map[string]domain.TokenUsage{
   16: 		"input": {InputTokens: 1}, "cached": {CachedInputTokens: 1}, "output": {OutputTokens: 1}, "reasoning": {ReasoningTokens: 1},
   17: 		"image input": {ImageInputTokens: 1}, "audio input": {AudioInputTokens: 1}, "audio output": {AudioOutputTokens: 1},
   18: 		"file input": {FileInputTokens: 1}, "video input": {VideoInputTokens: 1}, "image units": {ImageGenerationUnits: 1},
   19: 	}
   20: 	for name, usage := range positive {
   21: 		t.Run(name, func(t *testing.T) {
   22: 			if err := ValidateUsage(usage); err != nil {
   23: 				t.Fatalf("positive category invalid: %v", err)
   24: 			}
   25: 			if IsZeroUsage(usage) {
   26: 				t.Fatalf("positive category treated as zero")
   27: 			}
   28: 		})
   29: 	}
   30: 	negative := map[string]domain.TokenUsage{
   31: 		"input": {InputTokens: -1}, "cached": {CachedInputTokens: -1}, "output": {OutputTokens: -1}, "reasoning": {ReasoningTokens: -1},
   32: 		"image input": {ImageInputTokens: -1}, "audio input": {AudioInputTokens: -1}, "audio output": {AudioOutputTokens: -1},
   33: 		"file input": {FileInputTokens: -1}, "video input": {VideoInputTokens: -1}, "image units": {ImageGenerationUnits: -1},
   34: 	}
   35: 	for name, usage := range negative {
   36: 		t.Run("negative "+name, func(t *testing.T) {
   37: 			if err := ValidateUsage(usage); !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidUsage) {
   38: 				t.Fatalf("err = %v, want ErrInvalidUsage", err)
   39: 			}
   40: 		})
   41: 	}
   42: 	if !IsZeroUsage(domain.TokenUsage{}) {
   43: 		t.Fatalf("all-zero usage should be zero")
   44: 	}
   45: }
   46: 
   47: func TestParseUsageCompleteness(t *testing.T) {
   48: 	for _, value := range []string{"detailed", "aggregate", "estimated", "missing", "failed"} {
   49: 		t.Run(value, func(t *testing.T) {
   50: 			got, err := ParseUsageCompleteness(value)
   51: 			if err != nil || string(got) != value {
   52: 				t.Fatalf("got %q err %v", got, err)
   53: 			}
   54: 		})
   55: 	}
   56: 	for _, value := range []string{"unknown", "Detailed", " detailed", "detailed "} {
   57: 		t.Run("reject "+value, func(t *testing.T) {
   58: 			_, err := ParseUsageCompleteness(value)
   59: 			if !errors.Is(err, ErrInvalidUsageCompleteness) {
   60: 				t.Fatalf("err = %v, want ErrInvalidUsageCompleteness", err)
   61: 			}
   62: 		})
   63: 	}
   64: }
   65: 
   66: func TestExportedResultDTOsDoNotContainSecretsOrBodies(t *testing.T) {
   67: 	for _, typ := range []reflect.Type{reflect.TypeOf(CalculationResult{}), reflect.TypeOf(PreflightResult{}), reflect.TypeOf(ResolvedUsageResult{})} {
   68: 		for _, forbidden := range []string{"RawAPIKey", "ResellerAPIKey", "Authorization", "BillingJWT", "ServiceToken", "APIKeyEnv", "RequestBody", "ResponseBody"} {
   69: 			if _, ok := typ.FieldByName(forbidden); ok {
   70: 				t.Fatalf("%s contains forbidden field %s", typ.Name(), forbidden)
   71: 			}
   72: 		}
   73: 	}
   74: }

  268: func TestBillingChargeDomainContracts(t *testing.T) {
  269: 	if BillingChargeStatusPending != "pending" || BillingChargeStatusSucceeded != "succeeded" || BillingChargeStatusFailed != "failed" {
  270: 		t.Fatal("BillingChargeStatus values changed")
  271: 	}
  272: 	batchType := reflect.TypeOf(BillingChargeBatch{})
  273: 	for _, name := range []string{"ID", "UserID", "BillingSubjectUserID", "ProviderType", "ClientModel", "BillingModel", "InputTokens", "OutputTokens", "AmountCents", "Currency", "Status", "BillingResponseBalanceCents", "BillingErrorCode", "CreatedAt", "ChargedAt", "FailedAt", "UpdatedAt"} {
  274: 		if _, ok := batchType.FieldByName(name); !ok {
  275: 			t.Fatalf("BillingChargeBatch.%s is missing", name)
  276: 		}
  277: 	}
  278: 	allocType := reflect.TypeOf(BillingChargeAllocation{})
  279: 	for _, name := range []string{"ID", "BatchID", "LocalRequestID", "ChargedAmountCents", "RemainingAmountCents", "CreatedAt"} {
  280: 		if _, ok := allocType.FieldByName(name); !ok {
  281: 			t.Fatalf("BillingChargeAllocation.%s is missing", name)
  282: 		}
  283: 	}
  284: 	for _, forbidden := range []string{"Credential", "Token", "RawRequest", "RawResponse", "RawError", "ServiceToken", "JWT"} {
  285: 		if _, ok := batchType.FieldByName(forbidden); ok {
  286: 			t.Fatalf("BillingChargeBatch exposes forbidden field %s", forbidden)
  287: 		}
  288: 	}
  289: }

   15: 	ErrStoreContractViolation = errors.New("store contract violation")

   18: 		"route capacity unavailable",

   22: 	)

   60: }

   63: 	FindByRouteIDs(ctx context.Context, routeIDs []string) (map[string]domain.RoutePrice, error)
   64: }

   66: type RouteCapacityCheckInput struct {
   67: 	Route          domain.Route
   68: 	Reseller       domain.Reseller
   69: 	EstimatedUsage domain.TokenUsage
   70: }
   71: 
   72: type RouteCapacityResult struct {
   73: 	RateLimitAllowed   bool
   74: 	ConcurrencyAllowed bool
   75: }
   76: 
   77: type RouteCapacityChecker interface {
   78: 	Check(
   79: 		context.Context,
   80: 		RouteCapacityCheckInput,
   81: 	) (RouteCapacityResult, error)
   82: }
   83: 
   84: type RouteCapacityAcquireInput struct {
   85: 	LocalRequestID string
   86: 	ReservationID  string
   87: 	Route          domain.Route
   88: 	Reseller       domain.Reseller
   89: 	EstimatedUsage domain.TokenUsage
   90: }
   91: 
   92: type RouteCapacityReservation struct {
   93: 	LocalRequestID string
   94: 	ReservationID  string
   95: 	RouteID        string
   96: }
   97: 
   98: // RouteCapacityManager implementations must return
   99: // ErrRouteCapacityUnavailable when a valid route cannot accept this
  100: // attempt because of RPM, TPM, or concurrency limits. Contract and
  101: // identity violations must not be reported as capacity exhaustion.
  102: type RouteCapacityManager interface {
  103: 	RouteCapacityChecker
  104: 
  105: 	// Acquire atomically re-checks route limits and records one route attempt
  106: 	// against RPM, TPM, and concurrency. Repeated acquisition for the same
  107: 	// ReservationID must be idempotent. LocalRequestID is correlation only and
  108: 	// may be shared by multiple sequential attempt reservations.
  109: 	Acquire(
  110: 		context.Context,
  111: 		RouteCapacityAcquireInput,
  112: 	) (RouteCapacityReservation, error)
  113: 
  114: 	// Release removes only the in-flight concurrency slot. RPM and TPM usage
  115: 	// remain accounted for until their limiter window expires. Repeated release
  116: 	// of the same reservation must be idempotent.
  117: 	Release(
  118: 		context.Context,
  119: 		RouteCapacityReservation,
  120: 	) error
  121: }
  122: 
  123: type SecretResolver interface {
  124: 	Resolve(ctx context.Context, name string) (string, error)
  125: }
  126: 
  127: type ForwardingAdapterEndpointSupport interface {
  128: 	SupportsForwardingEndpoint(
  129: 		domain.EndpointKind,
  130: 	) bool
  131: }
  132: 
  133: type ForwardingAdapterSupport interface {
  134: 	SupportsForwardingAdapter(
  135: 		domain.APIFamily,
  136: 		domain.ProviderType,
  137: 		domain.EndpointKind,
  138: 	) bool
  139: }
  140: 
  141: type ModelIdentifierRewriteSupport interface {

  288: type UsageReserveOutcome string
  289: 
  290: const (
  291: 	UsageReserveOutcomeCreated            UsageReserveOutcome = "created"
  292: 	UsageReserveOutcomeLocalRequestExists UsageReserveOutcome = "local_request_exists"
  293: 	UsageReserveOutcomeIdempotencyExists  UsageReserveOutcome = "idempotency_exists"
  294: 	UsageReserveOutcomeUnresolvedUsage    UsageReserveOutcome = "unresolved_usage"
  295: )
  296: 
  297: type UsageReserveResult struct {
  298: 	Outcome  UsageReserveOutcome
  299: 	Existing *domain.UsageRecord
  300: }
  301: 
  302: type UsageTransitionResult struct {
  303: 	Applied bool
  304: 	Current *domain.UsageRecord
  305: }
  306: 
  307: type ForwardingAttemptStore interface {
  308: 	// StartAttempt durably inserts exactly one started attempt before any
  309: 	// upstream network write. The pair local_request_id + attempt_number is
  310: 	// unique. Repeating an identical command is idempotent; conflicting facts
  311: 	// must return ErrStoreConflict or ErrStoreContractViolation.
  312: 	StartAttempt(
  313: 		context.Context,
  314: 		domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  315: 	) (domain.ForwardingAttempt, error)
  316: 
  317: 	// CompleteAttempt atomically transitions the exact persisted started
  318: 	// attempt to succeeded or failed. Terminal attempts are immutable.
  319: 	// Repeating the identical completion is idempotent.
  320: 	CompleteAttempt(
  321: 		context.Context,
  322: 		domain.ForwardingAttempt,
  323: 	) (domain.ForwardingAttempt, error)
  324: 
  325: 	// LoadAttempts returns every persisted attempt for one request ordered by
  326: 	// attempt_number ASC. Missing requests return an empty slice.
  327: 	LoadAttempts(
  328: 		context.Context,
  329: 		string,
  330: 	) ([]domain.ForwardingAttempt, error)
  331: 
  332: 	// LoadStartedBefore returns at most limit durable attempts that are
  333: 	// still started and have started_at strictly before cutoff. Results
  334: 	// are ordered by started_at ASC, local_request_id ASC, then
  335: 	// attempt_number ASC so recovery can process bounded deterministic
  336: 	// batches. cutoff must be non-zero UTC and limit must be positive.
  337: 	LoadStartedBefore(
  338: 		context.Context,
  339: 		time.Time,
  340: 		int,
  341: 	) ([]domain.ForwardingAttempt, error)
  342: }
  343: 
  344: type UsageExposureSnapshot struct {
  345: 	Currency string
  346: 
  347: 	ReservedEstimatedAmountCents         int64
  348: 	BillableRemainingAmountCents         int64
  349: 	PartiallyChargedRemainingAmountCents int64
  350: 	PricingFailedCount                   int64
  351: }
  352: 
  353: type BillingChargeBatchSnapshot struct {
  354: 	Batch           domain.BillingChargeBatch
  355: 	Allocations     []domain.BillingChargeAllocation
  356: 	ExpectedRecords []domain.UsageRecord
  357: }
  358: 
  359: type UsageChargeBatchPlan struct {
  360: 	Batch           domain.BillingChargeBatch
  361: 	Allocations     []domain.BillingChargeAllocation
  362: 	ExpectedRecords []domain.UsageRecord
  363: }
  364: 
  365: type UsageChargeSuccess struct {
  366: 	BatchID             string
  367: 	BillingBalanceCents *int64
  368: 	ChargedAt           time.Time
  369: 	Allocations         []domain.BillingChargeAllocation
  370: 	ExpectedRecords     []domain.UsageRecord
  371: }
  372: 
  373: type UsageLedger interface {
  374: 	// CreateReserved atomically checks unresolved user pricing failures, local_request_id
  375: 	// uniqueness, optional client idempotency scope (user_id + endpoint_kind +
  376: 	// idempotency_key), and inserts the reserved usage record in one persistence
  377: 	// transaction. Callers must not emulate this with a Find-then-Insert sequence.
  378: 	CreateReserved(ctx context.Context, record domain.UsageRecord) (UsageReserveResult, error)
  379: 	FindByLocalRequestID(ctx context.Context, localRequestID string) (*domain.UsageRecord, error)
  380: 	// CompareAndSwap persists next only when the current record identified by
  381: 	// localRequestID is still in expectedStatus; when Applied is false Current
  382: 	// contains the actual current record.
  383: 	CompareAndSwap(ctx context.Context, localRequestID string, expectedStatus domain.UsageStatus, next domain.UsageRecord) (UsageTransitionResult, error)
  384: 	LoadExposure(ctx context.Context, userID string, currency string) (UsageExposureSnapshot, error)
  385: 	// LoadOpenChargeBatches returns durable pending/failed batches that must be
  386: 	// retried before creating new charge batches. Succeeded batches are not open.
  387: 	// Repository order is unspecified; application code must process snapshots by
  388: 	// batch.created_at ASC, then batch.id ASC.
  389: 	LoadOpenChargeBatches(ctx context.Context, userID string, billingSubjectUserID string, currency string) ([]BillingChargeBatchSnapshot, error)
  390: 	// LoadChargeCandidates returns chargeable billable or partially_charged records
  391: 	// with positive remaining amount. Billable records must be unclaimed. Partially
  392: 	// charged records must reference a succeeded historical charge batch and must
  393: 	// not be owned by any pending/failed active charge batch; PrepareChargeBatch
  394: 	// must atomically re-check this before replacing the claim for remaining amount.
  395: 	LoadChargeCandidates(ctx context.Context, userID string, currency string) ([]domain.UsageRecord, error)
  396: 	// PrepareChargeBatch atomically verifies ExpectedRecords, creates the pending
  397: 	// batch and allocations, and claims all records with BillingChargeRequestID.
  398: 	PrepareChargeBatch(ctx context.Context, plan UsageChargeBatchPlan) (BillingChargeBatchSnapshot, error)
  399: 	// MarkChargeBatchFailed atomically transitions pending -> failed only when
  400: 	// the current batch status matches expectedStatus. Succeeded is terminal;
  401: 	// an identical already-terminal succeeded batch must not be overwritten.
  402: 	MarkChargeBatchFailed(ctx context.Context, batchID string, expectedStatus domain.BillingChargeStatus, billingErrorCode string, failedAt time.Time) error
  403: 	// ApplyChargeSuccess atomically loads the persisted immutable batch command,
  404: 	// verifies caller metadata against persisted allocations/expected records,
  405: 	// transitions pending|failed -> succeeded, applies allocation deltas to usage
  406: 	// records, sets charged/partially_charged record status, clears any failed
  407: 	// metadata, and treats identical already-succeeded batches as idempotent success.
  408: 	ApplyChargeSuccess(ctx context.Context, success UsageChargeSuccess) error
  409: }
